            <div id="proxyInfo" class="small">No proxy bone layers</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="panelPage" data-page="stamp">
        <div class="section">
          <h3>Commit animation to Wick</h3>
          <div class="notice">Choose PNG, SVG mesh warp, or SVG Native Mode. SVG Native Mode warps parsed SVG points directly and keeps the result vector. Frame Bones are also committed into the final Wick clip.</div>
          <div class="row" style="margin-top:8px;">
            <label>Clip name</label>
            <input type="text" id="inpClipName" value="BoneWarpClip">
          </div>
          <div class="row">
            <label>Export mode</label>
            <select id="selExportMode">
              <option value="png">PNG with transparency</option>
              <option value="svg">SVG mesh warp</option>
              <option value="svgNative">SVG Native point warp</option>
              <option value="nativeCurve" selected>Native Wick curves</option> <!-- FIX v16.9 -->
            </select>
          </div>
          <div class="row">
            <label>Place at source</label>
            <input type="checkbox" id="chkPlaceAtSource" checked>
          </div>
          <div class="row">
            <label>Sync with parent</label>
            <input type="checkbox" id="chkSyncWithParent" checked>
          </div>
          <div class="row">
            <button id="btnStampClip">Commit To Wick</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="panelPage" data-page="smoothsvg">
        <div class="section">
          <h3>Smooth</h3> <!-- FIX v16.2 -->
          <div class="notice">Smooths the native SVG output and preview only. It does not change the bones. Use this when imported SVG points look jagged or segmented after warping.</div>
          <div class="row" style="margin-top:8px;">
            <label>Enable smoothing</label>
            <input type="checkbox" id="chkSvgSmoothEnabled">
          </div>
          <div class="row">

            <span id="txtSvgSmoothAmount" class="small">35%</span>
          </div>
          <div class="row">
            <label>Curve strength</label>

            <span id="txtSvgCurveStrength" class="small">70%</span>
          </div>

            <label>Preserve ends</label>
            <input type="checkbox" id="chkSvgSmoothPreserveEnds" checked>
          </div>

            <label>Keep flat ends</label>
            <input type="checkbox" id="chkSvgSmoothKeepFlatEnds" checked> <!-- FIX v16.2 -->
          </div>
          <div class="row">
            <button id="btnSvgSmoothPreview" class="secondary">Refresh Smooth Preview</button>
          </div>
          <div class="notice small">SVG Native point warp must be used in the Commit tab for smoothed vector output.</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="panelPage" data-page="help">
        <div class="section">
          <h3>Bone Warp Stamp help</h3>
          <div class="notice">This version is built around SVG Native warping. It loads SVG artwork, lets bones deform the SVG points, supports Frame Bones for swapping attached SVG artwork, and commits the result into Wick as a clip that remains in the project after the Luke Tool is closed.</div>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>1. Save and load</h3>
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li><b>Save Project</b> stores the Bone Warp setup as a project JSON file.</li>
            <li>The saved file includes the source SVG, normal bones, Frame Bones, loaded Frame Bone SVG slots, bone keys, Frame Bone keys, scale, rotation, and tool settings.</li>
            <li><b>Load Project</b> restores that setup so you can keep working later.</li>
            <li>Save and Load are at the top of the Source tab because they are project level actions.</li>
          </ol>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>2. Source SVG</h3>
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li>Click <b>Set Area</b> and drag the first placement area on the Wick stage.</li>
            <li>Click <b>Load SVG</b> and choose a normal SVG or Inkscape SVG file.</li>
            <li>Or select a Wick curve on the stage and click <b>Use Selected Wick Curve</b>. The selected curve is converted into an internal SVG source and its current stage bounds are used as the placement area.</li> <!-- FIX v14.4 -->
            <li>Use <b>Use Selected Curve And Remove Original</b> if you want the tool to ingest the selected Wick curve and then delete the original stage object only after the conversion succeeds.</li> <!-- FIX v14.5 -->
            <li>Use <b>Curve point density</b> before ingesting a selected Wick curve if the artwork needs more points for smoother bone bending. This inserts extra points between the existing corner points only. Corner points are preserved exactly, so the design is not smoothed, averaged, simplified, or rearranged.</li> <!-- FIX v14.7 -->
            <li>The Set Area frame is only used for initial placement. After loading or converting a selected curve, the visible tool overlay shows the SVG, bones, envelopes, handles, and Frame Bones.</li>
            <li>The SVG keeps its aspect ratio. Mesh controls are not part of this SVG Native workflow.</li>
            <li>Wick pan and zoom are followed by the overlay, but pan and zoom are not recorded as animation.</li>
          </ol>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>3. Bones</h3>
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li>The Bones tab is automatically in Add Bone mode.</li>
            <li>Drag on empty SVG space to create a normal warp bone, or set Bone type to Stretchy Bone before dragging if you want the tail length to be keyable and to pull nearby curve points along the bone axis.</li> <!-- FIX v17.1 -->
            <li>Click an existing bone to select it.</li>
            <li><b>Delete Selected Bone</b> only deletes the currently selected bone. After deletion, no other bone is deleted unless you select another bone and click delete again.</li>
            <li>Connected child bones keep their head locked to the parent tail and evaluate their angle relative to the parent bone.</li>
            <li>Use <b>Edit Bone</b> for precise rest bone position values and <b>Edit Envelope</b> for rest influence envelope values. These modes do not create animation keys.</li> <!-- FIX v16.6 -->
          </ol>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>4. Frame Bones</h3>
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li>A Frame Bone follows the normal bone it is attached to.</li>
            <li><b>Attach Frame Bone</b> attaches a Frame Bone to the selected normal bone.</li>
            <li><b>Pin Frame Bone</b> lets you click a place on the SVG and place the Frame Bone there.</li>
            <li>Enter the number of Frame Bone frames. The tool creates a visual slot for each frame.</li>
            <li>Each slot has a blank preview area and a <b>Load SVG</b> button.</li>
            <li><b>Load All SVGs</b> fills slots from filenames such as 001.svg, 002.svg, and 003.svg.</li>
            <li>If no Frame Bone key exists on a Wick frame, the Frame Bone displays slot 001 by default.</li>
            <li>Use the Frame Bone scale and rotate controls to orient the attached SVG artwork.</li>
          </ol>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>5. Animate</h3>
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li>Move the real Wick playhead to the frame you want to key.</li> <!-- FIX v16.6 -->
            <li>Use the <b>Animate</b> tab to set, clear, copy, and reset selected bone keys. Edit Bone is only for changing rest bone values.</li> <!-- FIX v16.5 -->
            <li>Drag a normal bone handle to create or update a key for only that bone.</li>
            <li>Normal bone key layers appear in the Wick timeline as locked proxy rows.</li>
            <li>Drag a normal bone key diamond in the Wick timeline to move that one bone key to another frame.</li>
            <li>Frame Bone key layers appear as separate locked proxy rows.</li>
            <li>To key a Frame Bone, scrub to a Wick frame and click the Frame Bone slot image you want. That slot is then shown on the Frame Bone at that Wick frame.</li>
          </ol>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>6. Smooth</h3> <!-- FIX v16.2 -->
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li>Use Smooth only if the warped SVG looks too jagged or segmented.</li> <!-- FIX v16.2 -->
            <li>Smoothing affects the SVG Native preview and committed SVG output.</li>
            <li>Smoothing does not change the bones.</li>
          </ol>
        </div>
        <div class="section">
          <h3>7. Commit to Wick</h3>
          <ol class="small" style="line-height:1.6; padding-left:18px;">
            <li>Go to <b>Commit</b> when the animation is ready.</li>
            <li>Choose SVG Native output for SVG based commits.</li>
            <li><b>Commit to Wick</b> creates a real Wick clip in the project.</li>
            <li>The committed clip uses expanded bounds so the warped SVG and Frame Bone SVGs are not clipped by the old Set Area.</li>
            <li>Generated SVG frames are kept as SVG assets where Wick supports SVG assets. They are not intentionally converted to PNG.</li>
            <li>Closing the Luke Tool removes the temporary tool overlay and proxy UI, but the committed Wick clip remains in the Wick project.</li>
          </ol>
          <div class="notice">Overlay controls: drag a head or tail circle to move a bone handle. Drag a bone line to move the whole bone. <span class="kbd">Shift</span> constrains movement to the dominant axis.</div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="section">
        <h3>Status</h3>
        <div id="status">Ready.</div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

      pointDensity: 50
    },
    proxy: { // FIX v10.2
      active: false,
      wickLayer: null,
      overlayCanvas: null,
      hitDivs: [],
      blockDivs: [],
      container: null,
      scrollContainer: null,
      rafId: null,
      framePending: false,
      name: 'BoneWarp_Proxy_Keys', // FIX v12.7: internal identifier safe
      layers: [], // FIX v10.9: one real Wick proxy layer per BoneWarp bone
      hitMeta: [], // FIX v10.9
      eventTargets: [], // FIX v10.9: listeners that keep proxy overlay following mouse and scrollbar interaction
      lastScrollX: null, // FIX v10.9
      lastScrollY: null // FIX v10.9
    },
    overlay: {
      root: null,
      clipHost: null, // FIX v8.9
      canvas: null,
      svgLayer: null, // FIX v7.5
      ctx: null,
      opacity: 1,
      active: false,
      timelineRoot: null,
      timelineCanvas: null,
      timelineCtx: null,
      needsRender: false,
      previewBounds: null // FIX v7.0
    },
    interaction: {
      addBoneMode: false,
      dragging: false,
      dragType: '',

      setAreaKey: null, // FIX v6.0
      hoverLocal: null, // FIX v6.4

      cleanupDone: false, // FIX v9.7
      preKeyedBoneIds: [], // FIX v11.3
      preExistingKeyFrame: false // FIX v11.3
    },
    bones: [],
    nextBoneId: 1,
    selectedBoneId: null,
    frameBones: [], // FIX v13.2
    nextFrameBoneId: 1, // FIX v13.2
    selectedFrameBoneId: null, // FIX v13.2
    committedClipIdentifiers: [], // FIX v14.0: committed Wick clips are real project content and must survive LukeTool close cleanup
    frameBoneCreateMode: 'attach', // FIX v13.2
    frameBonePinMode: false, // FIX v13.2
    frameBoneKeys: {}, // FIX v13.2 frame -> frameBoneId -> internal SVG slot
    frameCount: 24,
    frameCountSource: 'Wick timeline',
    fps: 12,
    currentFrame: 1,
    keyframes: {},
    playing: false,
    playTimer: null,
    wickFollowTimer: null,
    closeWatchTimer: null,
    lastStageViewSignature: '', // FIX v8.8

    timeline: {
      breadcrumbsH: 30,
      numberLineH: 35,
      layersW: 160,
      cellW: 38,
      cellH: 42,
      gridMargin: 1,
      scrollbarH: 18,
      totalH: 30 + 35 + 42 + 18,
      currentCellStart: 0
    },
    paint: {
      enabled: false,
      action: 'paint',
      brushSize: 28,
      brushStrength: 0.35,
      showOverlay: false
    }
  };

  function el(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function q(sel, root){ return (root || document).querySelector(sel); }
  function qa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root || document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }
  function clamp(v, a, b){ return Math.max(a, Math.min(b, v)); }
  function lerp(a, b, t){ return a + (b - a) * t; }
  function dist(a, b){ var dx = a.x - b.x, dy = a.y - b.y; return Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy); }
  function clone(obj){ return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj)); }
  function round(n){ return Math.round(n * 1000) / 1000; }
  function nowName(){ return 'BW_' + Date.now(); }

  function makeValidIdentifier(value, fallback){ // FIX v12.7
    var raw = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
    if (!raw) raw = String(fallback || 'item');
    var cleaned = raw.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9_$]/g, '_');
    if (!/^[A-Za-z_$]/.test(cleaned)) cleaned = '_' + cleaned;
    cleaned = cleaned.replace(/_+/g, '_');
    if (!cleaned || !/^[A-Za-z_$][A-Za-z0-9_$]*$/.test(cleaned)) cleaned = String(fallback || 'item').replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9_$]/g, '_');
    if (!/^[A-Za-z_$]/.test(cleaned)) cleaned = '_' + cleaned;
    return cleaned;
  }

  function boneProxyIdentifierForBone(bone){ // FIX v12.7
    return makeValidIdentifier(String((bone && bone.name) || ('Bone_' + (bone && bone.id || ''))), 'Bone_' + (bone && bone.id || '')); // FIX v16.1
  }

  function frameBoneProxyIdentifierForFrameBone(frameBone){ // FIX v13.7
    return makeValidIdentifier('F_Bone_' + (frameBone && frameBone.id || ''), 'F_Bone_' + (frameBone && frameBone.id || '')); // FIX v16.1
  }


  function log(msg){
    var box = el('status');
    var text = (typeof msg === 'string') ? msg : JSON.stringify(msg, null, 2);
    var stamp = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
    box.textContent = '[' + stamp + '] ' + text + '\n' + box.textContent;
  }

  function setStatusOnce(msg){
    el('status').textContent = msg;
  }

  function getBridge(){
    try { if (window.LukeToolsBridge) return window.LukeToolsBridge; } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent.LukeToolsBridge) return window.parent.LukeToolsBridge; } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.top && window.top.LukeToolsBridge) return window.top.LukeToolsBridge; } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function getEditor(bridge){
    try { if (bridge && typeof bridge.getEditor === 'function') return bridge.getEditor(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent.wickEditor) return window.parent.wickEditor; } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent.wickEditor && window.parent.wickEditor.editor) return window.parent.wickEditor.editor; } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent.editor) return window.parent.editor; } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function getProject(bridge){
    try { if (bridge && typeof bridge.getProject === 'function') return bridge.getProject(); } catch(e){}
    var ed = getEditor(bridge);
    try { if (ed && ed.project) return ed.project; } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function refreshBridgeRefs(){
    App.B = getBridge();
    App.ed = getEditor(App.B);
    App.project = getProject(App.B);
    try { App.Wick = window.parent.Wick; } catch(e){ App.Wick = null; }
    try { App.paper = window.parent.paper; } catch(e){ App.paper = null; }
    return !!(App.ed && App.project && App.Wick);
  }

  function markDirty(){
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.project) App.ed.project.unsavedChanges = true; } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.project && typeof App.ed.project.markAsModified === 'function') App.ed.project.markAsModified(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.canvas && typeof App.ed.canvas.render === 'function') App.ed.canvas.render(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.projectDidChange === 'function') App.ed.projectDidChange(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.syncInterfaces === 'function') App.ed.syncInterfaces(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.updateUI === 'function') App.ed.updateUI(); } catch(e){}
    try { window.parent.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize')); } catch(e){}
  }

  function setActiveTab(name){
    App.activeTab = name;
    if (name === 'bones') { // FIX v13.2: Bones tab defaults to Add Bone mode
      App.interaction.addBoneMode = true;
      if (App.paint.enabled) App.paint.enabled = false;
    } else { // FIX v4.7: Add Bone mode must not carry into Animate or other tabs.
      App.interaction.addBoneMode = false; // FIX v4.7
      App.frameBonePinMode = false; // FIX v13.2
      App.interaction.dragging = false; // FIX v4.7
      App.interaction.dragType = ''; // FIX v4.7
      App.paint.enabled = false; // FIX v6.4
    }
    qa('.tabBtn').forEach(function(btn){ btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.getAttribute('data-tab') === name); });
    qa('.panelPage').forEach(function(page){ page.classList.toggle('active', page.getAttribute('data-page') === name); });
    updateEditBoneControls(); // FIX v6.7
    updateFrameBoneUI(); // FIX v13.2
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function isRestBoneEditContext(){ // FIX v16.6
    return App.activeTab === 'bones' || App.activeTab === 'editbone';
  }

  function normaliseBoneType(value){ // FIX v17.0
    return value === 'stretchy' ? 'stretchy' : 'normal';
  }

  function isStretchyBone(bone){ // FIX v17.0
    return !!(bone && normaliseBoneType(bone.type) === 'stretchy');
  }

  function boneTypeLabel(bone){ // FIX v17.0
    return isStretchyBone(bone) ? 'Stretchy Bone' : 'Normal Bone';
  }

  function isAnimateKeyContext(){ // FIX v16.6
    return App.activeTab === 'animate';
  }

  function isEnvelopeDragType(type){ // FIX v16.6
    return type === 'envHeadPos' || type === 'envHeadNeg' || type === 'envTailPos' || type === 'envTailNeg';
  }

  function editBoneModeAllowsDragType(type){ // FIX v16.6
    if (App.activeTab !== 'editbone') return true;
    if (App.editBoneMode === 'envelope') return isEnvelopeDragType(type);
    return type === 'head' || type === 'tail' || type === 'line';
  }

  function setEditBoneMode(mode){ // FIX v16.6
    App.editBoneMode = mode === 'envelope' ? 'envelope' : 'bone';
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function editBoneAngleDeg(bone){ // FIX v6.7
    if (!bone) return 0;
    return Math.atan2(bone.tail.y - bone.head.y, bone.tail.x - bone.head.x) * 180 / Math.PI;
  }

  function setInputValueIfPresent(id, value){ // FIX v6.7
    var node = el(id);
    if (!node) return;
    if (document.activeElement === node) return;
    node.value = String(value);
  }

  function updateEditBoneControls(){ // FIX v6.7
    var bone = getSelectedBone();
    if (el('editBoneInfo')) el('editBoneInfo').textContent = bone ? (bone.name + '  ' + boneTypeLabel(bone)) : 'None'; // FIX v17.0
    if (!bone) return;
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditHeadX', Math.round(bone.head.x));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditHeadY', Math.round(bone.head.y));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditTailX', Math.round(bone.tail.x));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditTailY', Math.round(bone.tail.y));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditLength', Math.round(Math.max(1, dist(bone.head, bone.tail))));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditAngle', Math.round(editBoneAngleDeg(bone)));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditEnvStart', Math.round(getBoneEnvStart(bone)));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditEnvEnd', Math.round(getBoneEnvEnd(bone)));
    setInputValueIfPresent('numEditStrength', round(bone.strength || 1));
  }

  function readNumberInput(id, fallback){ // FIX v6.7
    var node = el(id);
    if (!node) return fallback;
    var n = Number(node.value);
    return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
  }

  function applyEditBoneFields(){ // FIX v6.7
    var bone = getSelectedBone();
    if (!bone) {
      log('No selected bone to edit.');
      return;
    }
    var oldParentBone = { head: clone(bone.head), tail: clone(bone.tail) };
    var startDesc = captureDescendantStateForBone(bone.id, null);
    var hx = readNumberInput('numEditHeadX', bone.head.x);
    var hy = readNumberInput('numEditHeadY', bone.head.y);
    var tx = readNumberInput('numEditTailX', bone.tail.x);
    var ty = readNumberInput('numEditTailY', bone.tail.y);
    bone.head = { x: hx, y: hy };
    bone.tail = { x: tx, y: ty };
    var requestedLength = readNumberInput('numEditLength', dist(bone.head, bone.tail));
    var requestedAngle = readNumberInput('numEditAngle', editBoneAngleDeg(bone));
    requestedLength = Math.max(1, requestedLength);
    var rad = requestedAngle * Math.PI / 180;
    bone.tail = { x: bone.head.x + Math.cos(rad) * requestedLength, y: bone.head.y + Math.sin(rad) * requestedLength };
    bone.restLength = requestedLength;
    bone.envStart = clamp(readNumberInput('numEditEnvStart', getBoneEnvStart(bone)), 2, 500);
    bone.envEnd = clamp(readNumberInput('numEditEnvEnd', getBoneEnvEnd(bone)), 2, 500);
    bone.radius = Math.max(getBoneEnvStart(bone), getBoneEnvEnd(bone));
    bone.strength = Math.max(0, readNumberInput('numEditStrength', bone.strength || 1));
    var newParentBone = { head: clone(bone.head), tail: clone(bone.tail) };
    applyDescendantTransformToRest(startDesc || [], oldParentBone, newParentBone);
    enforceAllRestChains();
    Object.keys(App.keyframes).forEach(function(fr){
      if (!App.keyframes[fr]) return;
      if (!App.keyframes[fr][bone.id]) App.keyframes[fr][bone.id] = { head: clone(bone.head), tail: clone(bone.tail), angle: Math.atan2(bone.tail.y - bone.head.y, bone.tail.x - bone.head.x), envStart: getBoneEnvStart(bone), envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(bone) };
      App.keyframes[fr][bone.id].envStart = getBoneEnvStart(bone);
      App.keyframes[fr][bone.id].envEnd = getBoneEnvEnd(bone);
      enforceAllPoseChains(App.keyframes[fr]);
    });
    updateEditBoneControls();
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function updateUI(){
    el('txtOverlayOpacity').textContent = Math.round(App.overlay.opacity * 100) + '%';
    if (el('txtGridResolution')) el('txtGridResolution').textContent = App.grid.resolution + ' x ' + App.grid.resolution; // FIX v4.7

    if (el('txtEnvEnd')) el('txtEnvEnd').textContent = String(Math.round(bone ? getBoneEnvEnd(bone) : 90));

    el('sourceInfo').textContent = App.source.image ? '  SVG shapes=' + App.source.svgNative.shapes.length : '')).trim()) : 'No SVG loaded'; // FIX v7.1
    el('overlayInfo').textContent = App.overlay.active ? ('Overlay active ' + Math.round((App.source.viewportRect ? App.source.viewportRect.width : 0)) + ' x ' + Math.round((App.source.viewportRect ? App.source.viewportRect.height : 0)) + ' vp px') : (App.interaction.setAreaActive ? 'Set Area mode active' : 'Not active'); // FIX v6.0
    el('selectedBoneInfo').textContent = bone ? (bone.name + '  type=' + boneTypeLabel(bone) + '  parent=' + getBoneName(bone.parentId) + '  env=' + Math.round(getBoneEnvStart(bone)) + '/' + Math.round(getBoneEnvEnd(bone)) + '  strength=' + round(bone.strength)) : 'None'; // FIX v17.0
    if (bone) {

      if (el('rngEnvEnd')) el('rngEnvEnd').value = String(Math.round(getBoneEnvEnd(bone)));
      el('rngBoneStrength').value = String(Math.round(bone.strength * 100));

    } else if (el('selBoneType')) {

    }
    updateParentSelect();

  function getSelectedTimeline(){
    try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.getSelectedTimeline === 'function') return App.B.getSelectedTimeline(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project && App.project.activeTimeline) return App.project.activeTimeline; } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project && App.project.timeline) return App.project.timeline; } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function getFrameEnd(frame){
    if (!frame) return 0;
    var start = 1;
    var end = 0;
    try { start = Number(frame.start || frame.startFrame || frame.startFrameNumber || 1); } catch(e){}
    try { end = Number(frame.end || frame.endFrame || frame.endFrameNumber || 0); } catch(e){}
    if (!end) {
      try {
        if (typeof frame.length === 'number') end = start + frame.length - 1;
      } catch(e){}
    }
    if (!end) {
      try {
        if (typeof frame.getEnd === 'function') end = Number(frame.getEnd());
      } catch(e){}
    }
    return Math.max(0, Math.round(end || start || 1));
  }

  function getWickTimelineFrameCount(){
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    var tl = getSelectedTimeline();
    var maxEnd = 1;
    try {
      if (tl && tl.layers && tl.layers.length) {
        tl.layers.forEach(function(layer){
          try {
            if (layer && layer.frames && layer.frames.length) {
              layer.frames.forEach(function(frame){
                maxEnd = Math.max(maxEnd, getFrameEnd(frame));
              });
            }
          } catch(e){}
        });
      }
    } catch(e){}
    try { maxEnd = Math.max(maxEnd, Math.round(Number(tl.playheadPosition || 1))); } catch(e){}
    try { maxEnd = Math.max(maxEnd, Math.round(Number(App.project.currentFrameNumber || 1))); } catch(e){}
    return clamp(maxEnd || 1, 1, 300);
  }

  function syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline(){
    var count = getWickTimelineFrameCount();
    App.frameCount = count;
    App.currentFrame = clamp(App.currentFrame, 1, App.frameCount);
    return count;
  }

  function getSelectedObject(){
    try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.getSelectedObject === 'function') return App.B.getSelectedObject(); } catch(e){}
    try {
      var sel = (App.project && App.project.selection) || (App.ed && App.ed.selection);
      if (sel) {
        if (typeof sel.getSelectedObjects === 'function') {
          var arr = sel.getSelectedObjects();
          return arr && arr[0] ? arr[0] : null;
        }
        if (Array.isArray(sel.selectedObjects)) return sel.selectedObjects[0] || null;
      }
    } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function getSelectionInfo(){
    try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.captureSelectionNow === 'function') App.B.captureSelectionNow(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.getSelectionInfo === 'function') return App.B.getSelectionInfo(); } catch(e){}
    try {
      var obj = getSelectedObject();
      if (!obj) return { ok:false };
      return { ok:true, identifier: obj.identifier || obj.name || '', uuid: obj.uuid || '' };
    } catch(e){}
    return { ok:false };
  }

  function findLargestParentCanvas(){
    try {
      var list = Array.prototype.slice.call(window.parent.document.querySelectorAll('canvas'));
      var best = null;
      var bestArea = 0;
      list.forEach(function(c){
        try { if (c.closest && c.closest('[data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay],[data-luketools-bonewarp-kind]')) return; } catch(skipErr){} // FIX v8.8
        var r = c.getBoundingClientRect();
        var area = r.width * r.height;
        if (area > bestArea && r.width > 100 && r.height > 100) {
          best = c;
          bestArea = area;
        }
      });
      return best;
    } catch(e) { return null; }
  }

  function getStageSize(){
    var p = App.project || {};
    return {
      width: p.width || p.projectWidth || 720,
      height: p.height || p.projectHeight || 480
    };
  }

  function getFittedStageRect(){
    var canvas = findLargestParentCanvas();
    if (!canvas) return null;
    var rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    var size = getStageSize();
    var sw = size.width, sh = size.height;
    var stageAR = sw / sh;
    var canvasAR = rect.width / rect.height;
    var fw, fh, fl, ft;
    if (canvasAR > stageAR) {
      fh = rect.height;
      fw = fh * stageAR;
      fl = rect.left + (rect.width - fw) * 0.5;
      ft = rect.top;
    } else {
      fw = rect.width;
      fh = fw / stageAR;
      fl = rect.left;
      ft = rect.top + (rect.height - fh) * 0.5;
    }
    return {
      left: fl,
      top: ft,
      width: fw,
      height: fh,
      stageW: sw,
      stageH: sh,
      canvas: canvas,
      canvasRect: rect
    };
  }


  function getWickPaperView(){ // FIX v8.8
    try { if (App.project && App.project.view && App.project.view.paper && App.project.view.paper.view) return App.project.view.paper.view; } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.project && App.ed.project.view && App.ed.project.view.paper && App.ed.project.view.paper.view) return App.ed.project.view.paper.view; } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent.paper && window.parent.paper.view) return window.parent.paper.view; } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.paper && App.paper.view) return App.paper.view; } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function getWickViewCanvasRect(){ // FIX v8.8
    var view = getWickPaperView();
    try { if (view && view.element && view.element.getBoundingClientRect) return view.element.getBoundingClientRect(); } catch(e){}
    try { if (view && view._element && view._element.getBoundingClientRect) return view._element.getBoundingClientRect(); } catch(e){}
    var canvas = findLargestParentCanvas();
    return canvas ? canvas.getBoundingClientRect() : null;
  }

  function pointToPaperPoint(x, y){ // FIX v8.8
    try { if (App.paper && App.paper.Point) return new App.paper.Point(x, y); } catch(e){}
    try { if (window.parent && window.parent.paper && window.parent.paper.Point) return new window.parent.paper.Point(x, y); } catch(e){}
    return { x: x, y: y };
  }

  function getStageViewSignature(){ // FIX v8.8
    var view = getWickPaperView();
    var rect = getWickViewCanvasRect();
    var parts = [];
    try { parts.push('pz:' + (App.project && App.project.zoom)); } catch(e){}
    try { parts.push('pp:' + JSON.stringify(App.project && App.project.pan)); } catch(e){}
    try { parts.push('vz:' + (view && view.zoom)); } catch(e){}
    try { parts.push('vc:' + (view && view.center ? [round(view.center.x), round(view.center.y)].join(',') : '')); } catch(e){}
    try { parts.push('vr:' + (rect ? [round(rect.left), round(rect.top), round(rect.width), round(rect.height)].join(',') : '')); } catch(e){}
    return parts.join('|');
  }

  function stageToVp(x, y, fit){
    fit = fit || getFittedStageRect();
    if (!fit) return { x:0, y:0 };
    var view = getWickPaperView(); // FIX v8.8
    var rect = getWickViewCanvasRect(); // FIX v8.8
    if (view && rect && typeof view.projectToView === 'function') { // FIX v8.8
      try {
        var vp = view.projectToView(pointToPaperPoint(x, y));
        return { x: rect.left + vp.x, y: rect.top + vp.y };
      } catch(e){}
    }
    return {
      x: fit.left + (x / fit.stageW) * fit.width,
      y: fit.top + (y / fit.stageH) * fit.height
    };
  }

  function vpToStage(x, y, fit){
    fit = fit || getFittedStageRect();
    if (!fit) return { x:0, y:0 };
    var view = getWickPaperView(); // FIX v8.8
    var rect = getWickViewCanvasRect(); // FIX v8.8
    if (view && rect && typeof view.viewToProject === 'function') { // FIX v8.8
      try {
        var pp = view.viewToProject(pointToPaperPoint(x - rect.left, y - rect.top));
        return { x: pp.x, y: pp.y };
      } catch(e){}
    }
    return {
      x: (x - fit.left) / fit.width * fit.stageW,
      y: (y - fit.top) / fit.height * fit.stageH
    };
  }

  function getObjectStageBounds(obj){
    if (!obj) return null;
    try {
      if (obj.bounds) {
        if (typeof obj.bounds.x === 'number' && typeof obj.bounds.y === 'number' && typeof obj.bounds.width === 'number' && typeof obj.bounds.height === 'number') {
          return { x: obj.bounds.x, y: obj.bounds.y, w: obj.bounds.width, h: obj.bounds.height, cx: obj.bounds.x + obj.bounds.width/2, cy: obj.bounds.y + obj.bounds.height/2 };
        }
        if (typeof obj.bounds.left === 'number' && typeof obj.bounds.top === 'number' && typeof obj.bounds.width === 'number' && typeof obj.bounds.height === 'number') {
          return { x: obj.bounds.left, y: obj.bounds.top, w: obj.bounds.width, h: obj.bounds.height, cx: obj.bounds.left + obj.bounds.width/2, cy: obj.bounds.top + obj.bounds.height/2 };
        }
      }
    } catch(e){}
    try {
      var x = Number(obj.x || 0), y = Number(obj.y || 0);
      var w = Number(obj.width || 0), h = Number(obj.height || 0);
      if (w > 0 && h > 0) {
        return { x: x - w/2, y: y - h/2, w: w, h: h, cx: x, cy: y };
      }
    } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function stageBoundsToViewportRect(bounds){
    var fit = getFittedStageRect();
    if (!fit || !bounds) return null;
    var tl = stageToVp(bounds.x, bounds.y, fit);
    var br = stageToVp(bounds.x + bounds.w, bounds.y + bounds.h, fit);
    return { x: tl.x, y: tl.y, width: br.x - tl.x, height: br.y - tl.y };
  }

  function getSetAreaStageBounds(){ // FIX v6.8
    var fit = getFittedStageRect(); // FIX v6.8
    var vp = App.source && App.source.viewportRect ? App.source.viewportRect : null; // FIX v6.8
    if (!fit || !vp) return null; // FIX v6.8
    var tl = vpToStage(vp.x, vp.y, fit); // FIX v6.8
    var br = vpToStage(vp.x + vp.width, vp.y + vp.height, fit); // FIX v6.8
    var x = tl.x; // FIX v6.8
    var y = tl.y; // FIX v6.8
    var w = br.x - tl.x; // FIX v6.8
    var h = br.y - tl.y; // FIX v6.8
    if (!(isFinite(x) && isFinite(y) && isFinite(w) && isFinite(h))) return null; // FIX v6.8
    return { x: x, y: y, w: w, h: h, cx: x + w * 0.5, cy: y + h * 0.5 }; // FIX v6.8
  }


  function removeSetAreaOverlay(){ // FIX v6.0
    try {
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (pdoc) {
        try { if (App.interaction.setAreaMove) pdoc.removeEventListener('mousemove', App.interaction.setAreaMove, true); } catch(e){}
        try { if (App.interaction.setAreaUp) pdoc.removeEventListener('mouseup', App.interaction.setAreaUp, true); } catch(e){}
        try { if (App.interaction.setAreaKey) pdoc.removeEventListener('keydown', App.interaction.setAreaKey, true); } catch(e){}
      }
      if (App.interaction.setAreaRoot && App.interaction.setAreaRoot.parentNode) App.interaction.setAreaRoot.parentNode.removeChild(App.interaction.setAreaRoot);
    } catch(e){}
    App.interaction.setAreaActive = false;
    App.interaction.setAreaRoot = null;
    App.interaction.setAreaBox = null;
    App.interaction.setAreaStart = null;
    App.interaction.setAreaMove = null;
    App.interaction.setAreaUp = null;
    App.interaction.setAreaKey = null;
  }

  function promptLocalImageFile(){ // FIX v6.0
    var inp = el('fileImageLoader');
    if (!inp) {
      log('SVG file input not found.');
      return;
    }
    try { inp.value = ''; } catch(e){}
    inp.click();
  }

  function hideSetAreaVisualFrame(){ // FIX v7.8
    try {
      if (!App.overlay || !App.overlay.root) return;
      App.overlay.root.style.border = '0px solid transparent';
      App.overlay.root.style.boxShadow = 'none';
      App.overlay.root.style.background = 'transparent';
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function applyLoadedSourceImage(dataUrl, image, meta){ // FIX v6.0
    meta = meta || {};
    App.source.dataUrl = dataUrl || '';
    App.source.embeddedDataUrl = dataUrl || '';
    App.source.image = image || null;
    App.source.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(meta.width || (image ? (image.naturalWidth || image.width || 0) : 0))); // FIX v7.5
    App.source.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(meta.height || (image ? (image.naturalHeight || image.height || 0) : 0))); // FIX v7.5
    App.source.fileName = meta.fileName || '';
    App.source.captureMode = meta.mode || 'local-file';
    App.source.svgRaw = meta.svgRaw || ''; // FIX v7.1
    App.source.svgNative = meta.svgNative || null; // FIX v7.1
    App.source.selectedIdentifier = meta.label || (meta.fileName || 'LoadedImage');
    App.source.selectedUUID = meta.uuid || 'local-file';
    App.source.stageBounds = null;
    if (!App.source.stagePlacementBounds) App.source.stagePlacementBounds = getSetAreaStageBounds(); // FIX v8.8
    App.source.stageCenter = null;
    App.source.stageRotation = 0;
    if (!App.source.viewportRect) {
      App.source.viewportRect = { x: 80, y: 80, width: Math.max(40, App.source.width), height: Math.max(40, App.source.height) };
    }
    buildAlphaMask();
    ensureOverlay();
    hideSetAreaVisualFrame(); // FIX v7.8
    fitOverlayToSource();
    clearAnimationData(false);
    syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
    renderOverlay();
    updateUI();
    log('Loaded SVG file: ' + (App.source.fileName || 'unnamed SVG') + '. Set Area frame hidden. Only SVG and bones remain visible.'); // FIX v7.8
  }

  function parseSvgNumber(value, fallback){ // FIX v7.1
    if (value == null || value === '') return fallback;
    var m = String(value).trim().match(/-?\d+(?:\.\d+)?/);
    return m ? Number(m[0]) : fallback;
  }

  function matrixIdentity(){ return [1,0,0,1,0,0]; } // FIX v7.1
  function matrixMul(m1, m2){ // FIX v7.1
    return [
      m1[0]*m2[0] + m1[2]*m2[1],
      m1[1]*m2[0] + m1[3]*m2[1],
      m1[0]*m2[2] + m1[2]*m2[3],
      m1[1]*m2[2] + m1[3]*m2[3],
      m1[0]*m2[4] + m1[2]*m2[5] + m1[4],
      m1[1]*m2[4] + m1[3]*m2[5] + m1[5]
    ];
  }
  function matrixApply(m, p){ return { x: m[0]*p.x + m[2]*p.y + m[4], y: m[1]*p.x + m[3]*p.y + m[5] }; } // FIX v7.1

  function parseSvgTransform(str){ // FIX v7.1
    var out = matrixIdentity();
    if (!str) return out;
    var re = /(matrix|translate|scale|rotate)\s*\(([^)]*)\)/g;
    var m;
    while ((m = re.exec(str))) {
      var type = m[1];
      var nums = (m[2].match(/-?\d*\.?\d+(?:e[-+]?\d+)?/ig) || []).map(Number);
      var mt = matrixIdentity();
      if (type === 'matrix' && nums.length >= 6) mt = nums.slice(0,6);
      else if (type === 'translate') mt = [1,0,0,1,nums[0] || 0, nums.length > 1 ? nums[1] : 0];
      else if (type === 'scale') mt = [nums[0] == null ? 1 : nums[0],0,0, nums.length > 1 ? nums[1] : (nums[0] == null ? 1 : nums[0]),0,0];
      else if (type === 'rotate') {
        var a = (nums[0] || 0) * Math.PI / 180;
        var c = Math.cos(a), s = Math.sin(a);
        var r = [c,s,-s,c,0,0];
        if (nums.length >= 3) {
          var cx = nums[1], cy = nums[2];
          mt = matrixMul(matrixMul([1,0,0,1,cx,cy], r), [1,0,0,1,-cx,-cy]);
        } else mt = r;
      }
      out = matrixMul(out, mt);
    }
    return out;
  }

  function parseStyleMap(node){ // FIX v7.1
    var out = {};
    var attrs = ['fill','stroke','stroke-width','stroke-linecap','stroke-linejoin','opacity','fill-opacity','stroke-opacity','fill-rule','clip-rule'];
    attrs.forEach(function(k){
      var v = node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute(k);
      if (v != null && v !== '') out[k] = v;
    });
    var style = node.getAttribute && node.getAttribute('style');
    if (style) {
      style.split(';').forEach(function(part){
        var i = part.indexOf(':');
        if (i > 0) out[part.slice(0,i).trim()] = part.slice(i+1).trim();
      });
    }
    if (!out.fill && node.tagName && /line|polyline/i.test(node.tagName)) out.fill = 'none';
    if (!out.fill) out.fill = '#000000';
    return out;
  }

  function styleMapToAttrs(style){ // FIX v7.1
    var keys = ['fill','stroke','stroke-width','stroke-linecap','stroke-linejoin','opacity','fill-opacity','stroke-opacity','fill-rule','clip-rule'];
    var s = '';
    keys.forEach(function(k){ if (style && style[k] != null && style[k] !== '') s += ' ' + k + '="' + escapeXmlAttr(style[k]) + '"'; });
    return s;
  }

  function tokenizePathD(d){ // FIX v7.1
    return String(d || '').match(/[a-zA-Z]|-?\d*\.?\d+(?:e[-+]?\d+)?/ig) || [];
  }

  function isPathCommand(t){ return /^[a-zA-Z]$/.test(t); } // FIX v7.1
  function cubicPoint(p0,p1,p2,p3,t){ var mt=1-t; return { x: mt*mt*mt*p0.x+3*mt*mt*t*p1.x+3*mt*t*t*p2.x+t*t*t*p3.x, y: mt*mt*mt*p0.y+3*mt*mt*t*p1.y+3*mt*t*t*p2.y+t*t*t*p3.y }; } // FIX v7.1
  function quadPoint(p0,p1,p2,t){ var mt=1-t; return { x: mt*mt*p0.x+2*mt*t*p1.x+t*t*p2.x, y: mt*mt*p0.y+2*mt*t*p1.y+t*t*p2.y }; } // FIX v7.1

  function commandPoint(x, y, matrix){ return matrixApply(matrix, { x: x, y: y }); } // FIX v7.3
  function cloneCmdPoint(p){ return { x: p.x, y: p.y }; } // FIX v7.3
  function cubicBezierKappaEllipse(cx, cy, rx, ry){ // FIX v7.3
    var k = 0.5522847498307936;
    return [
      { type: 'M', p: { x: cx + rx, y: cy } },
      { type: 'C', c1: { x: cx + rx, y: cy + ry * k }, c2: { x: cx + rx * k, y: cy + ry }, p: { x: cx, y: cy + ry } },
      { type: 'C', c1: { x: cx - rx * k, y: cy + ry }, c2: { x: cx - rx, y: cy + ry * k }, p: { x: cx - rx, y: cy } },
      { type: 'C', c1: { x: cx - rx, y: cy - ry * k }, c2: { x: cx - rx * k, y: cy - ry }, p: { x: cx, y: cy - ry } },
      { type: 'C', c1: { x: cx + rx * k, y: cy - ry }, c2: { x: cx + rx, y: cy - ry * k }, p: { x: cx + rx, y: cy } },
      { type: 'Z' }
    ];
  }

  function applyMatrixToCommandList(cmds, matrix){ // FIX v7.3
    return (cmds || []).map(function(cmd){
      var out = { type: cmd.type };
      if (cmd.p) out.p = commandPoint(cmd.p.x, cmd.p.y, matrix);
      if (cmd.c1) out.c1 = commandPoint(cmd.c1.x, cmd.c1.y, matrix);
      if (cmd.c2) out.c2 = commandPoint(cmd.c2.x, cmd.c2.y, matrix);
      return out;
    });
  }

  function pathCommandsToD(cmds){ // FIX v7.3
    var out = [];
    (cmds || []).forEach(function(cmd){
      if (!cmd || !cmd.type) return;
      if (cmd.type === 'M' || cmd.type === 'L') out.push(cmd.type + ' ' + round(cmd.p.x) + ' ' + round(cmd.p.y));
      else if (cmd.type === 'Q') out.push('Q ' + round(cmd.c1.x) + ' ' + round(cmd.c1.y) + ' ' + round(cmd.p.x) + ' ' + round(cmd.p.y));
      else if (cmd.type === 'C') out.push('C ' + round(cmd.c1.x) + ' ' + round(cmd.c1.y) + ' ' + round(cmd.c2.x) + ' ' + round(cmd.c2.y) + ' ' + round(cmd.p.x) + ' ' + round(cmd.p.y));
      else if (cmd.type === 'Z') out.push('Z');
    });
    return out.join(' ');
  }

  function smoothPointMix(a, b, amount){ // FIX v8.7
    return { x: lerp(a.x, b.x, amount), y: lerp(a.y, b.y, amount) };
  }

  function cloneNativeCommand(cmd){ // FIX v8.7
    var out = { type: cmd.type };
    if (cmd.p) out.p = clone(cmd.p);
    if (cmd.c1) out.c1 = clone(cmd.c1);
    if (cmd.c2) out.c2 = clone(cmd.c2);
    return out;
  }

  function smoothSvgLineRunToCurves(run, closed){ // FIX v16.2
    if (!run || run.length < 2) return [];
    var amount = clamp(App.smooth.amount, 0, 1);
    var curve = clamp(App.smooth.curveStrength, 0, 1) * amount;
    if (curve <= 0.0001) {
      var raw = [{ type:'M', p: clone(run[0]) }];
      for (var ri = 1; ri < run.length; ri++) raw.push({ type:'L', p: clone(run[ri]) });
      if (closed) raw.push({ type:'Z' });
      return raw;
    }
    var pts = run.map(clone);
    var lastIndex = closed ? pts.length : pts.length - 1;
    var flatSegment = [];
    if (App.smooth.keepFlatEnds !== false && lastIndex > 0) { // FIX v16.4
      var lengths = [];
      var usableLengths = []; // FIX v16.4
      var minLen = Infinity;
      for (var si = 0; si < lastIndex; si++) {
        var sp1 = pts[si];
        var sp2 = pts[(si + 1) % pts.length];
        var sl = dist(sp1, sp2);
        lengths.push(sl);
        if (sl > 0.0001) { // FIX v16.4
          usableLengths.push(sl); // FIX v16.4
          if (sl < minLen) minLen = sl;
        }
      }
      if (isFinite(minLen) && usableLengths.length > 1) { // FIX v16.4
        usableLengths.sort(function(a,b){ return a - b; }); // FIX v16.4
        var medianLen = usableLengths[Math.floor(usableLengths.length * 0.5)] || minLen; // FIX v16.4
        var shortIsRealOutlier = minLen < medianLen * 0.72; // FIX v16.4: if density points make most segments equal, do not protect every segment and block smoothing.
        if (shortIsRealOutlier) { // FIX v16.4
          var flatLimit = minLen * 1.25;
          for (var fi = 0; fi < lengths.length; fi++) flatSegment[fi] = lengths[fi] <= flatLimit;
        }
      }
    }
    if (amount > 0.0001 && pts.length > 2) {
      var relaxed = pts.map(clone);
      for (var i = 0; i < pts.length; i++) {
        var isEnd = !closed && (i === 0 || i === pts.length - 1);
        if (App.smooth.preserveEnds && isEnd) continue;
        if (App.smooth.keepFlatEnds !== false) { // FIX v16.2: endpoints of the shortest segments do not get relaxed.
          var prevSeg = closed ? ((i - 1 + pts.length) % pts.length) : i - 1;
          var nextSeg = i;
          if ((prevSeg >= 0 && flatSegment[prevSeg]) || (nextSeg >= 0 && flatSegment[nextSeg])) continue;
        }
        var p0 = pts[(i - 1 + pts.length) % pts.length];
        var p1 = pts[(i + 1) % pts.length];
        if (!closed && i === 0) p0 = pts[i];
        if (!closed && i === pts.length - 1) p1 = pts[i];
        relaxed[i] = smoothPointMix(pts[i], { x:(p0.x + p1.x) * 0.5, y:(p0.y + p1.y) * 0.5 }, amount * 0.55);
      }
      pts = relaxed;
    }
    var out = [{ type:'M', p: clone(pts[0]) }];
    for (var j = 0; j < lastIndex; j++) {
      var p1a = pts[j];
      var p2a = pts[(j + 1) % pts.length];
      if (App.smooth.keepFlatEnds !== false && flatSegment[j]) { // FIX v16.2: shortest flat end segments stay as straight line segments.
        out.push({ type:'L', p: clone(p2a) });
        continue;
      }
      var p0a = pts[(j - 1 + pts.length) % pts.length];
      var p3a = pts[(j + 2) % pts.length];
      if (!closed && j === 0) p0a = p1a;
      if (!closed && j + 2 >= pts.length) p3a = p2a;
      var c1 = { x: p1a.x + (p2a.x - p0a.x) * curve / 6, y: p1a.y + (p2a.y - p0a.y) * curve / 6 };
      var c2 = { x: p2a.x - (p3a.x - p1a.x) * curve / 6, y: p2a.y - (p3a.y - p1a.y) * curve / 6 };
      out.push({ type:'C', c1:c1, c2:c2, p:clone(p2a) });
    }
    if (closed) out.push({ type:'Z' });
    return out;
  }

  function smoothNativeCommandsForOutput(cmds){ // FIX v8.7
    if (!App.smooth || !App.smooth.enabled) return (cmds || []).map(cloneNativeCommand);
    var out = [];
    var run = [];
    var closedRun = false;
    function flushRun(){
      if (run.length) {
        out = out.concat(smoothSvgLineRunToCurves(run, closedRun));
      }
      run = [];
      closedRun = false;
    }
    (cmds || []).forEach(function(cmd){
      if (!cmd || !cmd.type) return;
      if (cmd.type === 'M') {
        flushRun();
        run = [clone(cmd.p)];
      } else if (cmd.type === 'L' && run.length) {
        run.push(clone(cmd.p));
      } else if (cmd.type === 'Z' && run.length) {
        closedRun = true;
        flushRun();
      } else {
        flushRun();
        var copied = cloneNativeCommand(cmd);
        var amount = clamp(App.smooth.amount, 0, 1);
        if (copied.type === 'Q' && copied.c1 && copied.p && amount > 0) {
          var qRef = copied.p;
          copied.c1 = smoothPointMix(copied.c1, qRef, amount * 0.08);
        }
        if (copied.type === 'C' && copied.c1 && copied.c2 && copied.p && amount > 0) {
          copied.c1 = smoothPointMix(copied.c1, copied.p, amount * 0.04);
          copied.c2 = smoothPointMix(copied.c2, copied.p, amount * 0.04);
        }
        out.push(copied);
      }
    });
    flushRun();
    return out;
  }


  function canvasCssColor(value, fallback){ // FIX v7.5
    value = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
    if (!value || value === 'none') return null;
    return value || fallback || null;
  }

  function svgOpacity(value, fallback){ // FIX v7.5
    var n = Number(value);
    return isFinite(n) ? clamp(n, 0, 1) : fallback;
  }

  function drawNativeCommandPath(ctx, cmds){ // FIX v7.5
    ctx.beginPath();
    (cmds || []).forEach(function(cmd){
      if (!cmd || !cmd.type) return;
      if (cmd.type === 'M' && cmd.p) ctx.moveTo(cmd.p.x, cmd.p.y);
      else if (cmd.type === 'L' && cmd.p) ctx.lineTo(cmd.p.x, cmd.p.y);
      else if (cmd.type === 'Q' && cmd.c1 && cmd.p) ctx.quadraticCurveTo(cmd.c1.x, cmd.c1.y, cmd.p.x, cmd.p.y);
      else if (cmd.type === 'C' && cmd.c1 && cmd.c2 && cmd.p) ctx.bezierCurveTo(cmd.c1.x, cmd.c1.y, cmd.c2.x, cmd.c2.y, cmd.p.x, cmd.p.y);
      else if (cmd.type === 'Z') ctx.closePath();
    });
  }

  function warpedNativeCommands(cmds, pose, ox, oy){ // FIX v7.5
    return (cmds || []).map(function(cmd){
      var out = { type: cmd.type };
      if (cmd.p) { var p = skinPointByPose(cmd.p, pose); out.p = { x: p.x + ox, y: p.y + oy }; }
      if (cmd.c1) { var c1 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c1, pose); out.c1 = { x: c1.x + ox, y: c1.y + oy }; }
      if (cmd.c2) { var c2 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c2, pose); out.c2 = { x: c2.x + ox, y: c2.y + oy }; }
      return out;
    });
  }

  function renderNativeSvgToContext(ctx, pose, renderOpts){ // FIX v7.5
    if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) return false;
    renderOpts = renderOpts || {};
    var w = Number(renderOpts.canvasWidth || App.source.width || 0);
    var h = Number(renderOpts.canvasHeight || App.source.height || 0);
    var ox = Number(renderOpts.offsetX || 0);
    var oy = Number(renderOpts.offsetY || 0);
    ctx.save();
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);
    App.source.svgNative.shapes.forEach(function(shape){
      var style = shape.style || {};
      var fill = canvasCssColor(style.fill, '#000');
      var stroke = canvasCssColor(style.stroke, null);
      var strokeWidth = Math.max(0, Number(style['stroke-width'] || 1));
      var opacity = svgOpacity(style.opacity, 1);
      var fillOpacity = svgOpacity(style['fill-opacity'], 1);
      var strokeOpacity = svgOpacity(style['stroke-opacity'], 1);
      ctx.lineCap = style['stroke-linecap'] || 'butt';
      ctx.lineJoin = style['stroke-linejoin'] || 'miter';
      (shape.cmdSubpaths || []).forEach(function(sp){
        var warped = smoothNativeCommandsForOutput(warpedNativeCommands(sp.commands || [], pose, ox, oy)); // FIX v8.7
        drawNativeCommandPath(ctx, warped);
        if (fill) {
          ctx.save();
          ctx.globalAlpha = opacity * fillOpacity;
          ctx.fillStyle = fill;
          try { ctx.fill(style['fill-rule'] === 'evenodd' ? 'evenodd' : 'nonzero'); } catch(e) { ctx.fill(); }
          ctx.restore();
        }
        if (stroke && strokeWidth > 0) {
          ctx.save();
          ctx.globalAlpha = opacity * strokeOpacity;
          ctx.strokeStyle = stroke;
          ctx.lineWidth = strokeWidth;
          ctx.stroke();
          ctx.restore();
        }
      });
    });
    ctx.restore();
    return true;
  }

  function commandPathToPolyline(cmds){ // FIX v7.3
    var pts = [];
    var cur = null;
    var start = null;
    (cmds || []).forEach(function(cmd){
      if (!cmd || !cmd.type) return;
      if (cmd.type === 'M') {
        cur = cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p);
        start = cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p);
        pts.push(cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p));
      } else if (cmd.type === 'L') {
        cur = cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p);
        pts.push(cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p));
      } else if (cmd.type === 'Q') {
        if (!cur) cur = { x: 0, y: 0 };
        for (var t = 1; t <= 10; t++) pts.push(quadPoint(cur, cmd.c1, cmd.p, t / 10));
        cur = cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p);
      } else if (cmd.type === 'C') {
        if (!cur) cur = { x: 0, y: 0 };
        for (var ct = 1; ct <= 12; ct++) pts.push(cubicPoint(cur, cmd.c1, cmd.c2, cmd.p, ct / 12));
        cur = cloneCmdPoint(cmd.p);
      } else if (cmd.type === 'Z') {
        if (start) pts.push(cloneCmdPoint(start));
        cur = start ? cloneCmdPoint(start) : cur;
      }
    });
    return pts;
  }

  function commandSubpathsToLegacySubpaths(cmdSubs){ // FIX v7.3
    return (cmdSubs || []).map(function(sp){
      return { points: commandPathToPolyline(sp.commands), closed: !!sp.closed };
    }).filter(function(sp){ return sp.points && sp.points.length > 1; });
  }

  function parsePathToCommandSubpaths(d, matrix){ // FIX v7.3
    var tok = tokenizePathD(d), i = 0, cmd = '', cur = {x:0,y:0}, start = {x:0,y:0};
    var paths = [], cmds = [];
    var prevC2 = null, prevQ1 = null;
    function num(){ return Number(tok[i++]); }
    function hasNum(){ return i < tok.length && !isPathCommand(tok[i]); }
    function closeCurrent(closed){
      if (cmds.length) paths.push({ commands: cmds, closed: !!closed });
      cmds = [];
      prevC2 = null;
      prevQ1 = null;
    }
    function addMove(p){ cmds.push({ type: 'M', p: commandPoint(p.x, p.y, matrix) }); cur = {x:p.x,y:p.y}; start = {x:p.x,y:p.y}; prevC2 = null; prevQ1 = null; }
    function addLine(p){ cmds.push({ type: 'L', p: commandPoint(p.x, p.y, matrix) }); cur = {x:p.x,y:p.y}; prevC2 = null; prevQ1 = null; }
    function addQuad(c1, p){ cmds.push({ type: 'Q', c1: commandPoint(c1.x, c1.y, matrix), p: commandPoint(p.x, p.y, matrix) }); cur = {x:p.x,y:p.y}; prevQ1 = {x:c1.x,y:c1.y}; prevC2 = null; }
    function addCubic(c1, c2, p){ cmds.push({ type: 'C', c1: commandPoint(c1.x, c1.y, matrix), c2: commandPoint(c2.x, c2.y, matrix), p: commandPoint(p.x, p.y, matrix) }); cur = {x:p.x,y:p.y}; prevC2 = {x:c2.x,y:c2.y}; prevQ1 = null; }
    while (i < tok.length) {
      if (isPathCommand(tok[i])) cmd = tok[i++];
      if (!cmd) break;
      var rel = cmd === cmd.toLowerCase();
      var C = cmd.toUpperCase();
      if (C === 'M') {
        var first = true;
        while (hasNum()) {
          var x = num(), y = num();
          var p = { x: rel ? cur.x + x : x, y: rel ? cur.y + y : y };
          if (first) {
            if (cmds.length) closeCurrent(false);
            addMove(p);
            first = false;
          } else addLine(p);
        }
      } else if (C === 'L') {
        while (hasNum()) { var lx=num(), ly=num(); addLine({x:rel?cur.x+lx:lx, y:rel?cur.y+ly:ly}); }
      } else if (C === 'H') {
        while (hasNum()) { var hx=num(); addLine({x:rel?cur.x+hx:hx, y:cur.y}); }
      } else if (C === 'V') {
        while (hasNum()) { var vy=num(); addLine({x:cur.x, y:rel?cur.y+vy:vy}); }
      } else if (C === 'C') {
        while (hasNum()) {
          var x1=num(),y1=num(),x2=num(),y2=num(),x3=num(),y3=num();
          var p1={x:rel?cur.x+x1:x1,y:rel?cur.y+y1:y1};
          var p2={x:rel?cur.x+x2:x2,y:rel?cur.y+y2:y2};
          var p3={x:rel?cur.x+x3:x3,y:rel?cur.y+y3:y3};
          addCubic(p1,p2,p3);
        }
      } else if (C === 'S') {
        while (hasNum()) {
          var sx2=num(), sy2=num(), sx=num(), sy=num();
          var rc1 = prevC2 ? { x: cur.x + (cur.x - prevC2.x), y: cur.y + (cur.y - prevC2.y) } : { x: cur.x, y: cur.y };
          var rc2 = { x: rel ? cur.x + sx2 : sx2, y: rel ? cur.y + sy2 : sy2 };
          var rp = { x: rel ? cur.x + sx : sx, y: rel ? cur.y + sy : sy };
          addCubic(rc1, rc2, rp);
        }
      } else if (C === 'Q') {
        while (hasNum()) {
          var qx1=num(), qy1=num(), qx2=num(), qy2=num();
          var q1={x:rel?cur.x+qx1:qx1,y:rel?cur.y+qy1:qy1};
          var q2={x:rel?cur.x+qx2:qx2,y:rel?cur.y+qy2:qy2};
          addQuad(q1,q2);
        }
      } else if (C === 'T') {
        while (hasNum()) {
          var tx=num(), ty=num();
          var tq = prevQ1 ? { x: cur.x + (cur.x - prevQ1.x), y: cur.y + (cur.y - prevQ1.y) } : { x: cur.x, y: cur.y };
          var tp = { x: rel ? cur.x + tx : tx, y: rel ? cur.y + ty : ty };
          addQuad(tq, tp);
        }
      } else if (C === 'A') {
        while (hasNum()) {
          num(); num(); num(); num(); num();
          var ax=num(), ay=num();
          addLine({x:rel?cur.x+ax:ax, y:rel?cur.y+ay:ay});
        }
      } else if (C === 'Z') {
        cmds.push({ type: 'Z' });
        cur = {x:start.x,y:start.y};
        closeCurrent(true);
      } else break;
    }
    if (cmds.length) closeCurrent(false);
    return paths.filter(function(p){ return p.commands && p.commands.length > 0; });
  }

  function rectToCommandSubpaths(x,y,w,h){ // FIX v7.3
    return [{ commands:[{type:'M',p:{x:x,y:y}},{type:'L',p:{x:x+w,y:y}},{type:'L',p:{x:x+w,y:y+h}},{type:'L',p:{x:x,y:y+h}},{type:'Z'}], closed:true }];
  }
  function polygonPoints(str){ // FIX v7.1
    var nums = (String(str||'').match(/-?\d*\.?\d+(?:e[-+]?\d+)?/ig)||[]).map(Number), pts=[];
    for (var i=0;i+1<nums.length;i+=2) pts.push({x:nums[i],y:nums[i+1]});
    return pts;
  }
  function polyPointsToCommandSubpath(points, closed){ // FIX v7.3
    if (!points || !points.length) return [];
    var cmds = [{ type:'M', p:{ x:points[0].x, y:points[0].y } }];
    for (var i = 1; i < points.length; i++) cmds.push({ type:'L', p:{ x:points[i].x, y:points[i].y } });
    if (closed) cmds.push({ type:'Z' });
    return [{ commands: cmds, closed: !!closed }];
  }
  function ellipseToCommandSubpaths(cx,cy,rx,ry){ // FIX v7.3
    return [{ commands: cubicBezierKappaEllipse(cx, cy, rx, ry), closed: true }];
  }

  function parseNativeSvg(svgText, targetW, targetH){ // FIX v7.7
    var doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(svgText, 'image/svg+xml');
    var svg = doc.documentElement;
    if (!svg || !/svg/i.test(svg.tagName)) throw new Error('Not an SVG file.');
    var vb = svg.getAttribute('viewBox');
    var vbVals = vb ? (vb.match(/-?\d*\.?\d+(?:e[-+]?\d+)?/ig)||[]).map(Number) : null;
    var sw = parseSvgNumber(svg.getAttribute('width'), targetW || 100);
    var sh = parseSvgNumber(svg.getAttribute('height'), targetH || 100);
    var srcX = 0, srcY = 0;
    if (vbVals && vbVals.length >= 4) { srcX = vbVals[0]; srcY = vbVals[1]; sw = vbVals[2]; sh = vbVals[3]; }
    sw = Math.max(1, Number(sw) || 1);
    sh = Math.max(1, Number(sh) || 1);
    var outW = Math.max(1, Number(targetW || sw || 100));
    var outH = Math.max(1, Number(targetH || sh || 100));
    var scale = Math.min(outW / sw, outH / sh); // FIX v7.7: preserve SVG aspect ratio inside the Set Area
    if (!isFinite(scale) || scale <= 0) scale = 1;
    var fitW = sw * scale;
    var fitH = sh * scale;
    var dx = (outW - fitW) * 0.5;
    var dy = (outH - fitH) * 0.5;
    var viewM = [scale,0,0,scale,dx - srcX * scale,dy - srcY * scale]; // FIX v7.7
    var shapes=[];
    function walk(node, matrix, inheritedStyle){
      if (!node || node.nodeType !== 1) return;
      var tag = node.tagName.toLowerCase();
      var m = matrixMul(matrix, parseSvgTransform(node.getAttribute('transform')));
      var style = Object.assign({}, inheritedStyle || {}, parseStyleMap(node));
      var cmdSubs=[];
      if (tag === 'path') cmdSubs = parsePathToCommandSubpaths(node.getAttribute('d') || '', m);
      else if (tag === 'rect') cmdSubs = rectToCommandSubpaths(parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('x'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('y'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('width'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('height'),0)).map(function(sp){ return { commands: applyMatrixToCommandList(sp.commands, m), closed: sp.closed }; });
      else if (tag === 'circle') cmdSubs = ellipseToCommandSubpaths(parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('cx'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('cy'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('r'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('r'),0)).map(function(sp){ return { commands: applyMatrixToCommandList(sp.commands, m), closed: sp.closed }; });
      else if (tag === 'ellipse') cmdSubs = ellipseToCommandSubpaths(parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('cx'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('cy'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('rx'),0), parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('ry'),0)).map(function(sp){ return { commands: applyMatrixToCommandList(sp.commands, m), closed: sp.closed }; });
      else if (tag === 'line') cmdSubs = [{ commands: applyMatrixToCommandList([{type:'M',p:{x:parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('x1'),0),y:parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('y1'),0)}},{type:'L',p:{x:parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('x2'),0),y:parseSvgNumber(node.getAttribute('y2'),0)}}], m), closed:false }];
      else if (tag === 'polyline' || tag === 'polygon') cmdSubs = polyPointsToCommandSubpath(polygonPoints(node.getAttribute('points')), tag==='polygon').map(function(sp){ return { commands: applyMatrixToCommandList(sp.commands, m), closed: sp.closed }; });
      if (cmdSubs.length) shapes.push({ style: style, cmdSubpaths: cmdSubs, subpaths: commandSubpathsToLegacySubpaths(cmdSubs) });
      Array.prototype.slice.call(node.childNodes || []).forEach(function(child){ walk(child, m, style); });
    }
    Array.prototype.slice.call(svg.childNodes || []).forEach(function(child){ walk(child, viewM, {}); });
    return { width: outW, height: outH, shapes: shapes };
  }

  function readFileAsText(file){ // FIX v7.1
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      try {
        var reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(){ resolve(String(reader.result || '')); };
        reader.onerror = function(){ reject(reader.error || new Error('Could not read text file.')); };
        reader.readAsText(file);
      } catch(e) { reject(e); }
    });
  }

  function loadImageFromFile(file){ // FIX v7.2
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      try {
        var isSvg = !!(file && ((file.type || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('svg') >= 0 || /\.svg$/i.test(file.name || ''))); // FIX v7.2
        if (!isSvg) { // FIX v7.2
          reject(new Error('This tool only accepts SVG files, including normal SVG and Inkscape SVG.')); // FIX v7.2
          return; // FIX v7.2
        }
        var reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(){
          var dataUrl = reader.result;
          loadImageFromUrl(dataUrl).then(async function(img){
            var svgRaw = '';
            var svgNative = null;
            var targetW = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.viewportRect && App.source.viewportRect.width ? App.source.viewportRect.width : (img.naturalWidth || img.width || 100))); // FIX v7.5
            var targetH = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.viewportRect && App.source.viewportRect.height ? App.source.viewportRect.height : (img.naturalHeight || img.height || 100))); // FIX v7.5
            try {
              svgRaw = await readFileAsText(file);
              svgNative = parseNativeSvg(svgRaw, targetW, targetH); // FIX v7.5: SVG coordinates are normalised to the Set Area so bones and SVG share the same scale.
            } catch(svgErr) {
              log('SVG native parse warning: ' + (svgErr && svgErr.message ? svgErr.message : svgErr));
            }
            resolve({ dataUrl: dataUrl, image: img, fileName: file && file.name ? file.name : 'svg', isSvg: true, svgRaw: svgRaw, svgNative: svgNative, width: targetW, height: targetH }); // FIX v7.5
          }).catch(function(err){ reject(err || new Error('SVG load failed')); });
        };
        reader.onerror = function(){ reject(reader.error || new Error('Could not read SVG file.')); };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
      } catch(e) {
        reject(e);
      }
    });
  }

  function selectedCurveSvgEscape(value){ // FIX v14.4
    return String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
  }

  function selectedCurveCssColor(value, fallback){ // FIX v14.4
    if (value == null || value === '') return fallback;
    try { if (typeof value === 'string') return value; } catch(e){}
    try { if (value && typeof value.toCSS === 'function') return value.toCSS(true); } catch(e){}
    try { if (value && typeof value.toCSS === 'function') return value.toCSS(); } catch(e){}
    try {
      if (value && typeof value.red === 'number' && typeof value.green === 'number' && typeof value.blue === 'number') {
        var r = Math.round(clamp(value.red, 0, 1) * 255);
        var g = Math.round(clamp(value.green, 0, 1) * 255);
        var b = Math.round(clamp(value.blue, 0, 1) * 255);
        var a = typeof value.alpha === 'number' ? clamp(value.alpha, 0, 1) : 1;
        if (a < 1) return 'rgba(' + r + ',' + g + ',' + b + ',' + round(a) + ')';
        return 'rgb(' + r + ',' + g + ',' + b + ')';
      }
    } catch(e){}
    return fallback;
  }

  function selectedCurveNumber(value, fallback){ // FIX v14.4
    var n = Number(value);
    return isFinite(n) ? n : fallback;
  }

  function selectedCurveGetBounds(value){ // FIX v14.4
    if (!value) return null;
    try {
      if (value.bounds) {
        var b = value.bounds;
        var x = selectedCurveNumber(b.x, selectedCurveNumber(b.left, NaN));
        var y = selectedCurveNumber(b.y, selectedCurveNumber(b.top, NaN));
        var w = selectedCurveNumber(b.width, selectedCurveNumber(b.w, NaN));
        var h = selectedCurveNumber(b.height, selectedCurveNumber(b.h, NaN));
        if (isFinite(x) && isFinite(y) && isFinite(w) && isFinite(h) && w > 0 && h > 0) return { x:x, y:y, w:w, h:h, cx:x + w * 0.5, cy:y + h * 0.5 };
      }
    } catch(e){}
    try {
      var ox = selectedCurveNumber(value.x, selectedCurveNumber(value.transformation && value.transformation.x, NaN));
      var oy = selectedCurveNumber(value.y, selectedCurveNumber(value.transformation && value.transformation.y, NaN));
      var ow = selectedCurveNumber(value.width, NaN);
      var oh = selectedCurveNumber(value.height, NaN);
      if (isFinite(ox) && isFinite(oy) && isFinite(ow) && isFinite(oh) && ow > 0 && oh > 0) return { x:ox - ow * 0.5, y:oy - oh * 0.5, w:ow, h:oh, cx:ox, cy:oy };
    } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function selectedCurveFindPaperItem(obj){ // FIX v14.4
    var seen = [];
    function scan(value, depth){
      if (!value || depth > 4) return null;
      if (seen.indexOf(value) >= 0) return null;
      seen.push(value);
      try { if (typeof value.exportSVG === 'function') return value; } catch(e){}
      var keys = ['view','_view','paper','_paper','path','_path','item','_item','paperItem','_paperItem','wickItem','_wickItem','projectItem','_projectItem','itemInstance','_itemInstance'];
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
        try { var found = scan(value[keys[i]], depth + 1); if (found) return found; } catch(e){}
      }
      return null;
    }
    return scan(obj, 0);
  }

  function selectedCurvePaperBounds(item){ // FIX v14.4
    if (!item) return null;
    try {
      var b = item.bounds;
      if (b && isFinite(b.left) && isFinite(b.top) && isFinite(b.width) && isFinite(b.height) && b.width > 0 && b.height > 0) return { x:b.left, y:b.top, w:b.width, h:b.height, cx:b.left + b.width * 0.5, cy:b.top + b.height * 0.5 };
    } catch(e){}
    return null;
  }

  function selectedCurveExtractSvgInner(svgText){ // FIX v14.4
    var raw = String(svgText || '').trim();
    if (!raw) return '';
    if (/^<svg[\s>]/i.test(raw)) {
      try {
        var doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(raw, 'image/svg+xml');
        var svg = doc.documentElement;
        if (svg && /svg/i.test(svg.tagName)) return Array.prototype.slice.call(svg.childNodes || []).map(function(n){ return new XMLSerializer().serializeToString(n); }).join('\n');
      } catch(e){}
      return raw.replace(/^<svg\b[^>]*>/i, '').replace(/<\/svg>\s*$/i, '');
    }
    return raw;
  }

  function selectedCurveWrapSvgContent(innerSvg, bounds, fileName){ // FIX v14.4
    bounds = bounds || { x:0, y:0, w:100, h:100 };
    var w = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(bounds.w || 100));
    var h = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(bounds.h || 100));
    var x = selectedCurveNumber(bounds.x, 0);
    var y = selectedCurveNumber(bounds.y, 0);
    return '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="' + w + '" height="' + h + '" viewBox="0 0 ' + w + ' ' + h + '">\n' + '<title>' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(fileName || 'Selected Wick Curve') + '</title>\n' + '<g transform="translate(' + round(-x) + ' ' + round(-y) + ')">\n' + String(innerSvg || '') + '\n</g>\n</svg>';
  }

  function selectedCurvePointXY(point){ // FIX v14.4
    if (!point) return { x:0, y:0 };
    return { x:selectedCurveNumber(point.x, selectedCurveNumber(point[0], 0)), y:selectedCurveNumber(point.y, selectedCurveNumber(point[1], 0)) };
  }

  function selectedCurveManualPathFromPaperItem(item, bounds){ // FIX v14.4
    if (!item || !item.segments || !item.segments.length) return '';
    bounds = bounds || selectedCurvePaperBounds(item) || { x:0, y:0, w:100, h:100 };
    var segs = Array.prototype.slice.call(item.segments || []);
    var d = [];
    function localPoint(p){ return { x:round(p.x - bounds.x), y:round(p.y - bounds.y) }; }
    var first = localPoint(selectedCurvePointXY(segs[0].point));
    d.push('M ' + first.x + ' ' + first.y);
    for (var i = 1; i < segs.length; i++) {
      var prev = segs[i - 1];
      var cur = segs[i];
      var pp = selectedCurvePointXY(prev.point);
      var cp = selectedCurvePointXY(cur.point);
      var ho = selectedCurvePointXY(prev.handleOut);
      var hi = selectedCurvePointXY(cur.handleIn);
      var hasOut = Math.abs(ho.x) > 0.0001 || Math.abs(ho.y) > 0.0001;
      var hasIn = Math.abs(hi.x) > 0.0001 || Math.abs(hi.y) > 0.0001;
      var end = localPoint(cp);
      if (hasOut || hasIn) {
        var c1 = localPoint({ x:pp.x + ho.x, y:pp.y + ho.y });
        var c2 = localPoint({ x:cp.x + hi.x, y:cp.y + hi.y });
        d.push('C ' + c1.x + ' ' + c1.y + ' ' + c2.x + ' ' + c2.y + ' ' + end.x + ' ' + end.y);
      } else d.push('L ' + end.x + ' ' + end.y);
    }
    try { if (item.closed) d.push('Z'); } catch(e){}
    var fill = 'none';
    var stroke = '#000000';
    var strokeWidth = 1;
    try { fill = selectedCurveCssColor(item.fillColor, 'none'); } catch(e){}
    try { stroke = selectedCurveCssColor(item.strokeColor, '#000000'); } catch(e){}
    try { strokeWidth = selectedCurveNumber(item.strokeWidth, 1); } catch(e){}
    if (!stroke || stroke === 'none') stroke = '#000000';
    return '<path d="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(d.join(' ')) + '" fill="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(fill || 'none') + '" stroke="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(stroke || '#000000') + '" stroke-width="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(strokeWidth) + '" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"/>';
  }

  function selectedCurveManualRectSvg(obj, bounds){ // FIX v14.4
    bounds = bounds || { x:0, y:0, w:100, h:100 };
    var fill = 'none';
    var stroke = '#000000';
    var strokeWidth = 1;
    try { fill = selectedCurveCssColor(obj.fillColor || obj.fill, 'none'); } catch(e){}
    try { stroke = selectedCurveCssColor(obj.strokeColor || obj.stroke, '#000000'); } catch(e){}
    try { strokeWidth = selectedCurveNumber(obj.strokeWidth || obj.stroke_width, 1); } catch(e){}
    return '<rect x="0" y="0" width="' + Math.max(1, round(bounds.w)) + '" height="' + Math.max(1, round(bounds.h)) + '" fill="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(fill || 'none') + '" stroke="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(stroke || '#000000') + '" stroke-width="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(strokeWidth) + '"/>';
  }

  function selectedCurveDensityToMaxStep(value){ // FIX v14.6
    var density = clamp(Number(value || 0), 0, 100);
    return Math.max(2, Math.round(42 - (density * 0.40)));
  }

  function selectedCurveStyleAttributesFromPaperItem(item){ // FIX v14.6
    var fill = 'none';
    var stroke = '#000000';
    var strokeWidth = 1;
    var opacity = 1;
    try { fill = selectedCurveCssColor(item && item.fillColor, 'none'); } catch(e){}
    try { stroke = selectedCurveCssColor(item && item.strokeColor, '#000000'); } catch(e){}
    try { strokeWidth = selectedCurveNumber(item && item.strokeWidth, 1); } catch(e){}
    try { opacity = selectedCurveNumber(item && item.opacity, 1); } catch(e){}
    if (!stroke || stroke === 'none') stroke = '#000000';
    var attrs = ' fill="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(fill || 'none') + '" stroke="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(stroke || '#000000') + '" stroke-width="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(strokeWidth) + '" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"';
    if (isFinite(opacity) && opacity >= 0 && opacity < 1) attrs += ' opacity="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(round(opacity)) + '"';
    return attrs;
  }

  function selectedCurveHasHandle(handle){ // FIX v14.7
    var h = selectedCurvePointXY(handle || { x:0, y:0 });
    return Math.abs(h.x) > 0.0001 || Math.abs(h.y) > 0.0001;
  }

  function selectedCurveBezierPoint(p0, p1, p2, p3, t){ // FIX v14.7
    var mt = 1 - t;
    var mt2 = mt * mt;
    var t2 = t * t;
    return {
      x: (mt2 * mt * p0.x) + (3 * mt2 * t * p1.x) + (3 * mt * t2 * p2.x) + (t2 * t * p3.x),
      y: (mt2 * mt * p0.y) + (3 * mt2 * t * p1.y) + (3 * mt * t2 * p2.y) + (t2 * t * p3.y)
    };
  }

  function selectedCurveSegmentLengthEstimate(p0, p1, p2, p3, isCurve){ // FIX v14.7
    if (!isCurve) return dist(p0, p3);
    var total = 0;
    var prev = p0;
    for (var i = 1; i <= 16; i++) {
      var pt = selectedCurveBezierPoint(p0, p1, p2, p3, i / 16);
      total += dist(prev, pt);
      prev = pt;
    }
    return total;
  }

  function selectedCurvePushSegmentPoints(out, prevSeg, curSeg, maxStep, includeEnd){ // FIX v14.7
    var p0 = selectedCurvePointXY(prevSeg.point);
    var p3 = selectedCurvePointXY(curSeg.point);
    var hOut = selectedCurvePointXY(prevSeg.handleOut || { x:0, y:0 });
    var hIn = selectedCurvePointXY(curSeg.handleIn || { x:0, y:0 });
    var isCurve = selectedCurveHasHandle(prevSeg.handleOut) || selectedCurveHasHandle(curSeg.handleIn);
    var p1 = isCurve ? { x:p0.x + hOut.x, y:p0.y + hOut.y } : p0;
    var p2 = isCurve ? { x:p3.x + hIn.x, y:p3.y + hIn.y } : p3;
    var segLen = selectedCurveSegmentLengthEstimate(p0, p1, p2, p3, isCurve);
    var steps = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(segLen / Math.max(2, Number(maxStep || 8))));
    var last = includeEnd ? steps : steps - 1;
    for (var i = 1; i <= last; i++) {
      var t = i / steps;
      out.push(isCurve ? selectedCurveBezierPoint(p0, p1, p2, p3, t) : { x:lerp(p0.x, p3.x, t), y:lerp(p0.y, p3.y, t) });
    }
  }

  function selectedCurveCornerSafePointsFromPaperPath(item, maxStep){ // FIX v14.7
    var segs = [];
    try { segs = Array.prototype.slice.call(item && item.segments ? item.segments : []); } catch(e) { segs = []; }
    if (!segs.length) return [];
    var pts = [];
    pts.push(selectedCurvePointXY(segs[0].point));
    for (var i = 1; i < segs.length; i++) selectedCurvePushSegmentPoints(pts, segs[i - 1], segs[i], maxStep, true);
    try {
      if (item.closed && segs.length > 1) selectedCurvePushSegmentPoints(pts, segs[segs.length - 1], segs[0], maxStep, false);
    } catch(e){}
    return pts;
  }

  function selectedCurveDensifiedPathFromPaperItem(item, bounds, maxStep){ // FIX v14.7
    if (!item) return '';
    var parts = [];
    function walk(node){
      if (!node) return;
      try {
        if (node.segments && node.segments.length) {
          var pts = selectedCurveCornerSafePointsFromPaperPath(node, maxStep); // FIX v14.7: preserve original anchors and only insert points between them
          if (pts && pts.length) {
            var d = [];
            d.push('M ' + round(pts[0].x) + ' ' + round(pts[0].y));
            for (var i = 1; i < pts.length; i++) d.push('L ' + round(pts[i].x) + ' ' + round(pts[i].y));
            try { if (node.closed) d.push('Z'); } catch(e){}
            parts.push('<path d="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(d.join(' ')) + '"' + selectedCurveStyleAttributesFromPaperItem(node) + ' data-luketools-point-density="' + selectedCurveSvgEscape(App.selectedCurve.pointDensity) + '" data-luketools-corner-safe="true"/>');
          }
          return;
        }
      } catch(pathErr){}
      try {
        if (node.children && node.children.length) {
          Array.prototype.slice.call(node.children || []).forEach(function(child){ walk(child); });
        }
      } catch(childErr){}
    }
    walk(item);
    return parts.join('\n');
  }

  function selectedCurveObjectToSvg(obj){ // FIX v14.4
    if (!obj) throw new Error('No Wick object is selected. Select a Wick curve or path on the stage first.');
    var item = selectedCurveFindPaperItem(obj);
    var bounds = selectedCurvePaperBounds(item) || getObjectStageBounds(obj) || selectedCurveGetBounds(obj);
    if (!bounds || bounds.w <= 0 || bounds.h <= 0) throw new Error('The selected object does not expose usable bounds.');
    var name = String(obj.identifier || obj.name || 'Selected_Wick_Curve');
    var rawExport = '';
    var density = clamp(Number(App.selectedCurve && App.selectedCurve.pointDensity != null ? App.selectedCurve.pointDensity : 50), 0, 100); // FIX v14.6
    var inner = '';
    if (item && density > 0) inner = selectedCurveDensifiedPathFromPaperItem(item, bounds, selectedCurveDensityToMaxStep(density)); // FIX v14.6
    if (!inner && item && typeof item.exportSVG === 'function') {
      try { rawExport = String(item.exportSVG({ asString:true }) || ''); } catch(e){}
      if (!rawExport) { try { rawExport = String(item.exportSVG({ asString:true, precision:3 }) || ''); } catch(e2){} }
    }
    if (!inner) inner = rawExport ? selectedCurveExtractSvgInner(rawExport) : '';
    if (!inner && item && item.segments && item.segments.length) inner = selectedCurveManualPathFromPaperItem(item, bounds);
    if (!inner) inner = selectedCurveManualRectSvg(obj, bounds);
    return { svgRaw:selectedCurveWrapSvgContent(inner, bounds, name), bounds:bounds, fileName:makeValidIdentifier(name, 'Selected_Wick_Curve') + '.svg' };
  }

  function removeOriginalSelectedCurveObject(obj){ // FIX v14.5
    var removed = false;
    var lastErr = null;
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    try {
      if (App.B && typeof App.B.deleteSelectedObject === 'function') {
        App.B.deleteSelectedObject();
        removed = true;
      }
    } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    if (!removed) {
      try {
        if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.deleteSelectedObjects === 'function') {
          App.ed.deleteSelectedObjects();
          removed = true;
        }
      } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    }
    if (!removed) {
      try {
        if (App.project && App.project.selection && typeof App.project.selection.delete === 'function') {
          App.project.selection.delete();
          removed = true;
        }
      } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    }
    if (!removed) {
      try {
        if (obj && typeof obj.remove === 'function') {
          obj.remove();
          removed = true;
        }
      } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    }
    if (!removed) {
      try {
        if (obj && obj.parent && typeof obj.parent.removeChild === 'function') {
          obj.parent.removeChild(obj);
          removed = true;
        }
      } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    }
    if (!removed) {
      try {
        if (obj && obj.parent && Array.isArray(obj.parent.objects)) {
          var idx = obj.parent.objects.indexOf(obj);
          if (idx >= 0) {
            obj.parent.objects.splice(idx, 1);
            removed = true;
          }
        }
      } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    }
    if (!removed) {
      try {
        if (obj && obj.parent && Array.isArray(obj.parent.children)) {
          var idx2 = obj.parent.children.indexOf(obj);
          if (idx2 >= 0) {
            obj.parent.children.splice(idx2, 1);
            removed = true;
          }
        }
      } catch(e) { lastErr = e; }
    }
    if (!removed) throw new Error('Converted the selected Wick curve, but could not remove the original stage object automatically.' + (lastErr && lastErr.message ? ' ' + lastErr.message : ''));
    markDirty();
    return true;
  }

  async function loadSvgTextAsSource(svgRaw, fileName, mode, bounds){ // FIX v14.4
    if (!svgRaw || !/^\s*<svg[\s>]/i.test(String(svgRaw))) throw new Error('Could not build a valid SVG from the selected object.');
    if (bounds) {
      App.source.stagePlacementBounds = { x:bounds.x, y:bounds.y, w:bounds.w, h:bounds.h, cx:bounds.cx, cy:bounds.cy };
      App.source.viewportRect = stageBoundsToViewportRect(bounds) || App.source.viewportRect;
    }
    if (!App.source.viewportRect) App.source.viewportRect = { x:80, y:80, width:100, height:100 };
    var dataUrl = svgTextToDataUrl(svgRaw);
    var img = await loadImageFromUrl(dataUrl);
