    var targetW = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.viewportRect && App.source.viewportRect.width ? App.source.viewportRect.width : (bounds && bounds.w ? bounds.w : (img.naturalWidth || img.width || 100))));
    var targetH = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.viewportRect && App.source.viewportRect.height ? App.source.viewportRect.height : (bounds && bounds.h ? bounds.h : (img.naturalHeight || img.height || 100))));
    var svgNative = null;
    try { svgNative = parseNativeSvg(svgRaw, targetW, targetH); } catch(svgErr) { log('Selected Wick curve SVG native parse warning: ' + (svgErr && svgErr.message ? svgErr.message : svgErr)); }
    applyLoadedSourceImage(dataUrl, img, { fileName:fileName || 'Selected_Wick_Curve.svg', mode:mode || 'selected-wick-curve', label:fileName || 'Selected Wick Curve', svgRaw:svgRaw, svgNative:svgNative, width:targetW, height:targetH, uuid:'selected-wick-curve' });
    if (bounds) {
      App.source.stageBounds = { x:bounds.x, y:bounds.y, w:bounds.w, h:bounds.h, cx:bounds.cx, cy:bounds.cy };
      App.source.stageCenter = { x:bounds.cx, y:bounds.cy };
    }
    if (svgNative && svgNative.shapes && svgNative.shapes.length) {
      log('Selected Wick curve converted to SVG Native source: parsed ' + svgNative.shapes.length + ' vector shape' + (svgNative.shapes.length === 1 ? '' : 's') + '.');
      if (el('selExportMode')) el('selExportMode').value = 'nativeCurve'; // FIX v16.9: native Wick curves are the default commit mode.
    } else log('Selected Wick curve converted to SVG source, but no native vector shapes were parsed.');
  }

  async function useSelectedWickCurveAsSourceInternal(removeOriginal){ // FIX v14.5
    try {
      refreshBridgeRefs();
      try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.captureSelectionNow === 'function') App.B.captureSelectionNow(); } catch(e){}
      var obj = getSelectedObject();
      if (!obj) throw new Error('No Wick object is selected. Select a Wick curve or path on the stage first.');
      var converted = selectedCurveObjectToSvg(obj);
      rememberSelectedCurveSourceTimeline(); // FIX v14.8
      await loadSvgTextAsSource(converted.svgRaw, converted.fileName, 'selected-wick-curve', converted.bounds);
      if (removeOriginal) {
        removeOriginalSelectedCurveObject(obj); // FIX v14.5
        log('Selected Wick curve ingested and original removed from the Wick stage.'); // FIX v14.5
      }
      removeSetAreaOverlay();
      ensureOverlay();
      hideSetAreaVisualFrame();
      fitOverlayToSource();
      renderOverlay();
      updateUI();
    } catch(err) {
      log((removeOriginal ? 'Use Selected Curve And Remove Original failed: ' : 'Use Selected Wick Curve failed: ') + (err && err.message ? err.message : err));
    }
  }

  async function useSelectedWickCurveAsSource(){ // FIX v14.5
    return useSelectedWickCurveAsSourceInternal(false); // FIX v14.5
  }

  async function useSelectedWickCurveAsSourceAndRemoveOriginal(){ // FIX v14.5
    return useSelectedWickCurveAsSourceInternal(true); // FIX v14.5
  }

  async function onImageFileChosen(evt){ // FIX v7.1
    var file = evt && evt.target && evt.target.files && evt.target.files[0] ? evt.target.files[0] : null;
    if (!file) return;
    try {
      var loaded = await loadImageFromFile(file);
      applyLoadedSourceImage(loaded.dataUrl, loaded.image, { fileName: loaded.fileName, mode: 'local-svg', label: loaded.fileName, svgRaw: loaded.svgRaw, svgNative: loaded.svgNative, width: loaded.width, height: loaded.height }); // FIX v7.5
      if (loaded.svgNative && loaded.svgNative.shapes && loaded.svgNative.shapes.length) {
        log('SVG Native Mode ready: parsed ' + loaded.svgNative.shapes.length + ' vector shape' + (loaded.svgNative.shapes.length === 1 ? '' : 's') + ' with preserved curve commands.');
        if (el('selExportMode')) el('selExportMode').value = 'nativeCurve'; // FIX v16.9: native Wick curves are the default commit mode.
      }
    } catch(e) {
      log('SVG load failed: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e));
    }
  }

  function beginSetAreaMode(){ // FIX v6.0
    removeSetAreaOverlay();
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc || !pdoc.body) {
      log('Could not access the Wick editor screen to set an area.');
      return;
    }
    var root = pdoc.createElement('div');
    root.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'set-area');
    root.style.cssText = [
      'position:fixed',
      'left:0',
      'top:0',
      'right:0',
      'bottom:0',
      'z-index:2147483645',
      'cursor:crosshair',
      'background:transparent', // FIX v6.2
      'pointer-events:auto',
      'user-select:none'
    ].join(';');
    var label = pdoc.createElement('div');
    label.textContent = 'Drag to set image area. Press Esc to cancel.';
    label.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;left:18px;top:18px;padding:8px 10px;background:rgba(20,20,20,0.92);color:#fff;border:1px solid #52b1ff;font:12px Arial,sans-serif;pointer-events:none;';
    var box = pdoc.createElement('div');
    box.style.cssText = 'position:fixed;left:0;top:0;width:0;height:0;border:2px solid #52b1ff;background:transparent;box-shadow:0 0 0 1px rgba(82,177,255,0.35) inset;pointer-events:none;display:none;'; // FIX v6.2
    root.appendChild(label);
    root.appendChild(box);
    pdoc.body.appendChild(root);

    App.interaction.setAreaActive = true;
    App.interaction.setAreaRoot = root;
    App.interaction.setAreaBox = box;
    App.interaction.setAreaStart = null;

    function updateBox(clientX, clientY){
      var sx = App.interaction.setAreaStart.x;
      var sy = App.interaction.setAreaStart.y;
      var left = Math.min(sx, clientX);
      var top = Math.min(sy, clientY);
      var width = Math.abs(clientX - sx);
      var height = Math.abs(clientY - sy);
      box.style.display = 'block';
      box.style.left = Math.round(left) + 'px';
      box.style.top = Math.round(top) + 'px';
      box.style.width = Math.round(width) + 'px';
      box.style.height = Math.round(height) + 'px';
    }

    root.addEventListener('mousedown', function(ev){
      if (ev.button !== 0) return;
      ev.preventDefault();
      ev.stopPropagation();
      App.interaction.setAreaStart = { x: ev.clientX, y: ev.clientY };
      updateBox(ev.clientX, ev.clientY);
    }, true);

    App.interaction.setAreaMove = function(ev){
      if (!App.interaction.setAreaStart) return;
      ev.preventDefault();
      ev.stopPropagation();
      updateBox(ev.clientX, ev.clientY);
    };

    App.interaction.setAreaUp = function(ev){
      if (!App.interaction.setAreaStart) return;
      ev.preventDefault();
      ev.stopPropagation();
      var sx = App.interaction.setAreaStart.x;
      var sy = App.interaction.setAreaStart.y;
      var left = Math.min(sx, ev.clientX);
      var top = Math.min(sy, ev.clientY);
      var width = Math.abs(ev.clientX - sx);
      var height = Math.abs(ev.clientY - sy);
      removeSetAreaOverlay();
      if (width < 10 || height < 10) {
        log('Set area cancelled because the drag was too small.');
        updateUI();
        return;
      }
      App.source.viewportRect = { x: left, y: top, width: width, height: height };
      App.source.stagePlacementBounds = getSetAreaStageBounds(); // FIX v8.8: set area becomes stage anchored so Wick zoom and pan can move the overlay correctly without keyframing it.
      if (App.source.image) {
        ensureOverlay();
        fitOverlayToSource();
        renderOverlay();
      }
      updateUI();
      log('Set area: ' + Math.round(width) + ' x ' + Math.round(height) + ' at ' + Math.round(left) + ', ' + Math.round(top) + '.');
      promptLocalImageFile();
    };

    App.interaction.setAreaKey = function(ev){
      if (ev.key === 'Escape') {
        ev.preventDefault();
        ev.stopPropagation();
        removeSetAreaOverlay();
        log('Set area cancelled.');
      }
    };

    pdoc.addEventListener('mousemove', App.interaction.setAreaMove, true);
    pdoc.addEventListener('mouseup', App.interaction.setAreaUp, true);
    pdoc.addEventListener('keydown', App.interaction.setAreaKey, true);
    log('Set Area mode: drag a rectangle on the Wick editor screen.');
  }

  function blobToDataUrl(blob){ // FIX v5.5
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      try {
        var reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(){ resolve(reader.result); };
        reader.onerror = function(){ reject(reader.error || new Error('FileReader failed')); };
        reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
      } catch(e) {
        reject(e);
      }
    });
  }

  async function collectImageCandidatesAsync(obj){ // FIX v5.5
    var urls = [];
    var seenUrls = {};
    var seenObjs = [];

    function addUrl(v){
      if (typeof v !== 'string' || !v) return;
      if (seenUrls[v]) return;
      if (/^data:image\//i.test(v) || /^blob:/i.test(v) || /^https?:/i.test(v) || /^file:/i.test(v)) {
        seenUrls[v] = true;
        urls.push(v);
      }
    }

    async function scan(value, depth){
      if (value == null || depth > 3) return;
      if (typeof value === 'string') {
        addUrl(value);
        return;
      }
      if (typeof Blob !== 'undefined' && (value instanceof Blob || value instanceof File)) {
        try { addUrl(await blobToDataUrl(value)); } catch(e){}
        return;
      }
      if (typeof HTMLImageElement !== 'undefined' && value instanceof HTMLImageElement) {
        try { addUrl(value.currentSrc || value.src); } catch(e){}
        return;
      }
      if (Array.isArray(value)) {
        for (var i = 0; i < value.length; i++) await scan(value[i], depth + 1);
        return;
      }
      if (typeof value !== 'object') return;
      if (seenObjs.indexOf(value) >= 0) return;
      seenObjs.push(value);

      var directKeys = [
        'src','source','imageData','dataUrl','dataURL','dataUri','dataURI','href','url','currentSrc',
        'asset','linkedAsset','clipAsset','image','img','file','blob','contents','raw','assetData'
      ];
      for (var k = 0; k < directKeys.length; k++) {
        var key = directKeys[k];
        try { if (value[key] != null) await scan(value[key], depth + 1); } catch(e){}
      }

      try {
        var keys = Object.keys(value);
        for (var j = 0; j < keys.length; j++) {
          var dynKey = keys[j];
          if (/src|url|data|image|asset|file|blob/i.test(dynKey)) {
            try { await scan(value[dynKey], depth + 1); } catch(e){}
          }
        }
      } catch(e){}
    }

    await scan(obj, 0);

    try {
      if (App.project && App.project.assets && App.project.assets.length) {
        for (var ai = 0; ai < App.project.assets.length; ai++) {
          var a = App.project.assets[ai];
          var match = false;
          try { if (obj && obj.assetUUID && a.uuid === obj.assetUUID) match = true; } catch(e){}
          try { if (obj && obj.assetId && a.uuid === obj.assetId) match = true; } catch(e){}
          try { if (obj && obj.assetIdentifier && a.identifier === obj.assetIdentifier) match = true; } catch(e){}
          try { if (obj && obj.identifier && a.identifier === obj.identifier) match = true; } catch(e){}
          try { if (obj && obj.uuid && a.uuid === obj.uuid) match = true; } catch(e){}
          if (match) await scan(a, 0);
        }
      }
    } catch(e){}

    return urls;
  }

  async function getImageSrcCandidates(obj){ // FIX v5.5
    return await collectImageCandidatesAsync(obj);
  }

  function loadImageFromUrl(url){
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      var img = new Image();
      img.onload = function(){ resolve(img); };
      img.onerror = function(){ reject(new Error('SVG load failed')); };
      img.src = url;
    });
  }

  function captureSelectionFromStageCanvas(bounds, fit){
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      try {
        fit = fit || getFittedStageRect();
        if (!fit || !fit.canvas || !bounds) return reject(new Error('Missing fit or bounds'));
        var vp = stageBoundsToViewportRect(bounds);
        if (!vp) return reject(new Error('Could not map bounds to viewport'));
        var c = fit.canvas;
        var cRect = fit.canvasRect;
        var sx = (vp.x - cRect.left) * (c.width / cRect.width);
        var sy = (vp.y - cRect.top) * (c.height / cRect.height);
        var sw = vp.width * (c.width / cRect.width);
        var sh = vp.height * (c.height / cRect.height);
        sx = Math.max(0, sx); sy = Math.max(0, sy);
        sw = Math.max(1, sw); sh = Math.max(1, sh);
        var out = document.createElement('canvas');
        out.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(bounds.w));
        out.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(bounds.h));
        var ctx = out.getContext('2d', { alpha: true, willReadFrequently: true }); // FIX v5.5
        ctx.clearRect(0,0,out.width,out.height);
        ctx.drawImage(c, sx, sy, sw, sh, 0, 0, out.width, out.height);
        try { // FIX v5.5: emergency background cleanup for fallback stage crops
          var id = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, out.width, out.height);
          var px = id.data;
          var samples = [
            [0,0],[out.width-1,0],[0,out.height-1],[out.width-1,out.height-1]
          ];
          var bg = [];
          for (var si = 0; si < samples.length; si++) {
            var sx0 = samples[si][0], sy0 = samples[si][1];
            var ii = (sy0 * out.width + sx0) * 4;
            bg.push([px[ii], px[ii+1], px[ii+2]]);
          }
          function nearBg(r,g,b){
            for (var bi = 0; bi < bg.length; bi++) {
              var br = bg[bi][0], bgc = bg[bi][1], bb = bg[bi][2];
              if (Math.abs(r-br) <= 12 && Math.abs(g-bgc) <= 12 && Math.abs(b-bb) <= 12) return true;
            }
            return false;
          }
          for (var p = 0; p < px.length; p += 4) {
            if (nearBg(px[p], px[p+1], px[p+2])) px[p+3] = 0;
          }
          ctx.putImageData(id, 0, 0);
        } catch(e){}
        resolve({ dataUrl: out.toDataURL('image/png'), width: out.width, height: out.height, mode: 'stage-crop' });
      } catch(e) {
        reject(e);
      }
    });
  }

  async function captureSelectedImage(){
    if (!refreshBridgeRefs()) {
      log('Bridge or editor not available.');
      return;
    }
    var obj = getSelectedObject();
    var info = getSelectionInfo();
    if (!obj) {
      log('No selected object found. Select an image on the stage first.');
      return;
    }
    var bounds = getObjectStageBounds(obj);
    if (!bounds) {
      log('Could not determine selected object bounds.');
      return;
    }
    var fit = getFittedStageRect();
    if (!fit) {
      log('Could not find stage canvas.');
      return;
    }

    App.source.selectedIdentifier = info && (info.identifier || info.name) || obj.identifier || obj.name || 'SelectedObject';
    App.source.selectedUUID = info && info.uuid || obj.uuid || '';
    App.source.stageBounds = bounds;
    App.source.stageCenter = { x: bounds.cx, y: bounds.cy };
    App.source.stageRotation = Number(obj.rotation || 0) || 0;

    var data = null;
    var candidates = await getImageSrcCandidates(obj); // FIX v5.5
    if (candidates.length) {
      for (var i = 0; i < candidates.length; i++) {
        try {
          var img = await loadImageFromUrl(candidates[i]);
          data = { dataUrl: candidates[i], width: img.naturalWidth || img.width, height: img.naturalHeight || img.height, mode: 'asset' };
          break;
        } catch(e){}
      }
    }
    if (!data) {
      try {
        data = await captureSelectionFromStageCanvas(bounds, fit);
        if (data) data.mode = 'stage-crop'; // FIX v5.5
        log('WARNING: Raw PNG asset data was not found. The tool fell back to a stage crop, which can destroy transparency. Re select the original PNG image on stage if this happens.'); // FIX v5.5
      } catch(err) {
        log('Failed to capture image: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err));
        return;
      }
    }
    if (!data || !data.dataUrl) {
      log('No image data captured.');
      return;
    }

    try {
      var image = await loadImageFromUrl(data.dataUrl);
      App.source.dataUrl = data.dataUrl;
      App.source.embeddedDataUrl = ''; // FIX v5.2
      App.source.captureMode = data.mode || ''; // FIX v5.5
      App.source.image = image;
      App.source.width = data.width || image.naturalWidth || image.width;
      App.source.height = data.height || image.naturalHeight || image.height;
      buildAlphaMask();
      App.source.viewportRect = stageBoundsToViewportRect(bounds);
      ensureOverlay();
      fitOverlayToSource();
      clearAnimationData(false);
      syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
      renderOverlay();
      log('Captured source image using ' + data.mode + '.'); // FIX v5.5
    } catch(e) {
      log('Captured image but failed to load preview: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e));
    }
    updateUI();
  }

  function clearAnimationData(clearBones){
    App.keyframes = {};
    App.currentFrame = 1;
    if (clearBones) {
      App.bones = [];
      App.nextBoneId = 1;
      App.selectedBoneId = null;
    }
    updateUI();
  }

  function getWickStageClipElement(){ // FIX v8.9
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc) return null;
    var selectors = [
      '#wick-canvas-container',
      '.wick-canvas-container',
      '#canvas-container',
      '.canvas-container',
      '#wick-canvas',
      '.wick-canvas',
      'canvas.wick-canvas',
      'canvas'
    ];
    for (var i = 0; i < selectors.length; i++) {
      try {
        var elx = pdoc.querySelector(selectors[i]);
        if (elx) {
          if (elx.tagName && elx.tagName.toLowerCase() === 'canvas' && elx.parentElement) return elx.parentElement;
          return elx;
        }
      } catch(e){}
    }
    return pdoc.body;
  }

  function getWickStageClipRect(){ // FIX v8.9
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    var stageEl = getWickStageClipElement();
    if (!pdoc || !stageEl) return { left:0, top:0, width:window.innerWidth || 800, height:window.innerHeight || 600 };
    try {
      var r = stageEl.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (r && r.width > 10 && r.height > 10) return { left:r.left, top:r.top, width:r.width, height:r.height };
    } catch(e){}
    return { left:0, top:0, width:pdoc.documentElement.clientWidth || 800, height:pdoc.documentElement.clientHeight || 600 };
  }

  function updateOverlayClipHost(){ // FIX v8.9
    if (!App.overlay.clipHost) return null;
    var r = getWickStageClipRect();
    App.overlay.clipHost.style.left = Math.round(r.left) + 'px';
    App.overlay.clipHost.style.top = Math.round(r.top) + 'px';
    App.overlay.clipHost.style.width = Math.max(20, Math.round(r.width)) + 'px';
    App.overlay.clipHost.style.height = Math.max(20, Math.round(r.height)) + 'px';
    try { getWickNavigationViewportRect(); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.8
    return r;
  }

  function ensureOverlay(){
    if (App.overlay.root) return;
    var pdoc = window.parent.document;
    var clipHost = pdoc.createElement('div'); // FIX v8.9
    clipHost.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay', App.interaction.overlayOwnerId); // FIX v8.9
    clipHost.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'stage-clip-host'); // FIX v8.9
    clipHost.style.cssText = [ // FIX v8.9
      'position:fixed',
      'left:0px',
      'top:0px',
      'width:100px',
      'height:100px',
      'border:0',
      'background:transparent',
      'z-index:950', // FIX v10.0: BoneWarp stage layer unchanged below raised Wick controls
      'overflow:hidden',
      'pointer-events:none',
      'user-select:none',
      'contain:layout paint'
    ].join(';');
    var root = pdoc.createElement('div');
    root.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay', App.interaction.overlayOwnerId);
    root.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'stage');
    root.style.cssText = [
      'position:absolute', // FIX v8.9: positioned inside clipped Wick stage host
      'left:20px',
      'top:20px',
      'width:320px',
      'height:240px',
      'border:0', // FIX v8.0
      'background:transparent', // FIX v6.2
      'z-index:1', // FIX v8.9
      'box-shadow:none', // FIX v8.0
      'overflow:visible', // FIX v8.0
      'pointer-events:auto',
      'user-select:none'
    ].join(';');
    var svgLayer = pdoc.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'svg'); // FIX v7.5
    svgLayer.style.cssText = 'position:absolute;left:0;top:0;width:100%;height:100%;display:block;pointer-events:none;overflow:visible;'; // FIX v7.5
    svgLayer.setAttribute('xmlns', 'http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'); // FIX v7.5
    root.appendChild(svgLayer); // FIX v7.5
    var canvas = pdoc.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.style.cssText = 'position:absolute;left:0;top:0;width:100%;height:100%;display:block;cursor:crosshair;overflow:visible;'; // FIX v8.0
    root.appendChild(canvas);
    clipHost.appendChild(root); // FIX v8.9
    pdoc.body.appendChild(clipHost); // FIX v8.9
    App.overlay.clipHost = clipHost; // FIX v8.9
    updateOverlayClipHost(); // FIX v8.9
    try { getWickNavigationViewportRect(); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.8
    App.overlay.root = root;
    App.overlay.svgLayer = svgLayer; // FIX v7.5
    App.overlay.canvas = canvas;
    App.overlay.ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    App.overlay.active = true;
    if (App.source && App.source.image) hideSetAreaVisualFrame(); // FIX v7.8

    canvas.addEventListener('mousedown', onOverlayMouseDown);
    pdoc.addEventListener('mousemove', onOverlayMouseMove);
    pdoc.addEventListener('mouseup', onOverlayMouseUp);
    pdoc.addEventListener('keydown', onParentKeyDown, true);
    pdoc.addEventListener('keyup', onParentKeyUp, true);
  }

  function removeOverlay(){
    try {
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (pdoc) {
        try { pdoc.removeEventListener('mousemove', onOverlayMouseMove); } catch(e){}
        try { pdoc.removeEventListener('mouseup', onOverlayMouseUp); } catch(e){}
        try { pdoc.removeEventListener('keydown', onParentKeyDown, true); } catch(e){}
        try { pdoc.removeEventListener('keyup', onParentKeyUp, true); } catch(e){}
      }
      if (App.overlay.clipHost && App.overlay.clipHost.parentNode) App.overlay.clipHost.parentNode.removeChild(App.overlay.clipHost); // FIX v8.9
      else if (App.overlay.root && App.overlay.root.parentNode) App.overlay.root.parentNode.removeChild(App.overlay.root);
      if (App.overlay.timelineRoot && App.overlay.timelineRoot.parentNode) App.overlay.timelineRoot.parentNode.removeChild(App.overlay.timelineRoot);
      if (pdoc) {
        var stale = Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('[data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay="' + App.interaction.overlayOwnerId + '"]'));
        stale.forEach(function(node){ try { if (node && node.parentNode) node.parentNode.removeChild(node); } catch(e){} });
      }
    } catch(e){}
    App.overlay.root = null;
    App.overlay.clipHost = null; // FIX v8.9
    App.overlay.canvas = null;
    App.overlay.svgLayer = null; // FIX v7.5
    App.overlay.ctx = null;
    App.overlay.timelineRoot = null;
    App.overlay.timelineCanvas = null;
    App.overlay.timelineCtx = null;
    App.overlay.active = false;
    try { updateUI(); } catch(e){}
  }

  function cleanupToolOverlays(){ // FIX v9.7
    if (App.interaction.cleanupDone) return; // FIX v9.7
    App.interaction.cleanupDone = true; // FIX v9.7
    try { stop(); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { removeSetAreaOverlay(); } catch(e){} // FIX v6.0
    try { if (App.wickFollowTimer) clearInterval(App.wickFollowTimer); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { if (App.closeWatchTimer) clearInterval(App.closeWatchTimer); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { if (App.playTimer) clearInterval(App.playTimer); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { if (App.playRaf) cancelAnimationFrame(App.playRaf); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { if (App.interaction.closeObserver) App.interaction.closeObserver.disconnect(); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { removeParentCloseCleanup(); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.7
    try { removeProxyOverlay(false); } catch(e){} // FIX v10.2
    App.wickFollowTimer = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.closeWatchTimer = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.playTimer = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.playRaf = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.interaction.closeObserver = null; // FIX v9.7
    removeOverlay(); // FIX v9.7
    try { // FIX v14.0: cleanup only temporary LukeTool UI DOM. Do not remove committed Wick clips or any rendered Wick project content.
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (pdoc) {
        var selectors = [
          '[data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay]',
          '[data-luketools-bonewarp-kind="set-area"]',
          '[data-luketools-bonewarp-kind="stage-clip-host"]',
          '[data-luketools-bonewarp-kind="stage-overlay-root"]',
          '[data-luketools-bonewarp-kind="proxy-keyframe-canvas"]',
          '[data-luketools-bonewarp-kind="proxy-keyframe-hit"]',
          '[id^="ltbw_nav_cut_"]',
          '#ltbw-proxy-keyframe-canvas',
          '.luketools-bonewarp-overlay',
          '.ltbw-stage-clip-host'
        ].join(',');
        Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll(selectors)).forEach(function(node){
          try { if (node && node.parentNode) node.parentNode.removeChild(node); } catch(removeErr){}
        });
      }
    } catch(e){}
    App.overlay.root = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.overlay.clipHost = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.overlay.canvas = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.overlay.svgLayer = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.overlay.ctx = null; // FIX v9.7
    App.overlay.active = false; // FIX v9.7
  }

  function removeParentCloseCleanup(){ // FIX v9.7
    try {
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (pdoc && App.interaction.parentCloseHandler) {
        pdoc.removeEventListener('mousedown', App.interaction.parentCloseHandler, true);
        pdoc.removeEventListener('click', App.interaction.parentCloseHandler, true);
      }
      if (App.interaction.unloadHandler) {
        window.removeEventListener('beforeunload', App.interaction.unloadHandler, true);
        window.removeEventListener('pagehide', App.interaction.unloadHandler, true);
      }
    } catch(e){}
    App.interaction.parentCloseHandler = null;
    App.interaction.unloadHandler = null;
  }

  function installParentCloseCleanup(){ // FIX v9.7
    try {
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (!pdoc || App.interaction.parentCloseHandler) return;
      App.interaction.parentCloseHandler = function(evt){
        try {
          var target = evt && evt.target ? evt.target : null;
          if (!target || !target.closest) return;
          var clickable = target.closest('button,[role="button"],.close,.Close,.modal-close,.tool-close,.luketools-close,[aria-label],[title]');
          if (!clickable) return;
          var label = ((clickable.getAttribute('aria-label') || '') + ' ' + (clickable.getAttribute('title') || '') + ' ' + (clickable.textContent || '')).trim().toLowerCase();
          var looksLikeClose = label === 'x' || label === '×' || label.indexOf('close') >= 0 || label.indexOf('hide') >= 0;
          if (!looksLikeClose) return;
          var frame = window.frameElement;
          var panel = frame ? frame.parentElement : null;
          var nearPanel = false;
          var node = clickable;
          for (var i = 0; node && i < 8; i++, node = node.parentElement) {
            if (node === panel || node === (panel && panel.parentElement) || node === (panel && panel.parentElement && panel.parentElement.parentElement)) {
              nearPanel = true;
              break;
            }
          }
          if (nearPanel || label.indexOf('luke') >= 0 || label.indexOf('tool') >= 0 || label === 'x' || label === '×') {
            setTimeout(cleanupToolOverlays, 0);
          }
        } catch(e){}
      };
      pdoc.addEventListener('mousedown', App.interaction.parentCloseHandler, true);
      pdoc.addEventListener('click', App.interaction.parentCloseHandler, true);
      App.interaction.unloadHandler = function(){ cleanupToolOverlays(); };
      window.addEventListener('beforeunload', App.interaction.unloadHandler, true);
      window.addEventListener('pagehide', App.interaction.unloadHandler, true);
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function ensureTimelineOverlay(){
    // FIX v4.3: no separate warp timeline overlay. The tool now uses Wick's existing timeline only.
    if (App.overlay.timelineRoot && App.overlay.timelineRoot.parentNode) {
      try { App.overlay.timelineRoot.parentNode.removeChild(App.overlay.timelineRoot); } catch(e){}
    }
    App.overlay.timelineRoot = null;
    App.overlay.timelineCanvas = null;
    App.overlay.timelineCtx = null;
  }

  function getPreviewBoundsForPose(pose){ // FIX v8.0
    var baseW = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.width) || 1); // FIX v8.0
    var baseH = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.height) || 1); // FIX v8.0
    var out = { minX: 0, minY: 0, maxX: baseW, maxY: baseH, width: baseW, height: baseH, offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 }; // FIX v8.0
    pose = pose || getRestPose(); // FIX v8.0
    function addPoint(p, extra){ // FIX v8.0
      if (!p) return; // FIX v8.0
      extra = Number(extra || 0); // FIX v8.0
      out.minX = Math.min(out.minX, p.x - extra); // FIX v8.0
      out.minY = Math.min(out.minY, p.y - extra); // FIX v8.0
      out.maxX = Math.max(out.maxX, p.x + extra); // FIX v8.0
      out.maxY = Math.max(out.maxY, p.y + extra); // FIX v8.0
    }
    try {
      var b = getVisibleWarpBoundsForPose(pose); // FIX v8.0
      addPoint({ x: b.minX, y: b.minY }, 0); // FIX v8.0
      addPoint({ x: b.maxX, y: b.maxY }, 0); // FIX v8.0
    } catch(e){}
    try {
      App.bones.forEach(function(bone){ // FIX v8.0
        var pb = getBonePoseLike(bone, pose); // FIX v8.0
        var envExtra = Math.max(36, getBoneEnvStart(pb), getBoneEnvEnd(pb)); // FIX v8.0
        addPoint(pb.head, envExtra); // FIX v8.0
        addPoint(pb.tail, envExtra); // FIX v8.0
        var geom = getEnvelopeGeometry(pb); // FIX v8.0
        addPoint(geom.headPos, 28); // FIX v8.0
        addPoint(geom.headNeg, 28); // FIX v8.0
        addPoint(geom.tailPos, 28); // FIX v8.0
        addPoint(geom.tailNeg, 28); // FIX v8.0
      });
    } catch(e){}
    var pad = 42; // FIX v8.0: large enough for handles, labels, envelopes and dragged bones.
    out.minX = Math.floor(out.minX - pad); // FIX v8.0
    out.minY = Math.floor(out.minY - pad); // FIX v8.0
    out.maxX = Math.ceil(out.maxX + pad); // FIX v8.0
    out.maxY = Math.ceil(out.maxY + pad); // FIX v8.0
    out.width = Math.max(1, out.maxX - out.minX); // FIX v8.0
    out.height = Math.max(1, out.maxY - out.minY); // FIX v8.0
    out.offsetX = -out.minX; // FIX v8.0
    out.offsetY = -out.minY; // FIX v8.0
    return out; // FIX v8.0
  }

  function localBoundsToViewportRect(bounds){ // FIX v8.8
    bounds = bounds || { minX:0, minY:0, width:App.source.width, height:App.source.height };
    var stageBase = App.source.stagePlacementBounds || null;
    if (stageBase) {
      var sx = stageBase.w / Math.max(1, App.source.width);
      var sy = stageBase.h / Math.max(1, App.source.height);
      var stageRect = {
        x: stageBase.x + (bounds.minX || 0) * sx,
        y: stageBase.y + (bounds.minY || 0) * sy,
        w: Math.max(1, (bounds.width || App.source.width) * sx),
        h: Math.max(1, (bounds.height || App.source.height) * sy)
      };
      return stageBoundsToViewportRect(stageRect);
    }
    var vp = App.source.viewportRect || { x:50, y:50, width: App.source.width, height: App.source.height };
    var vx = vp.width / Math.max(1, App.source.width);
    var vy = vp.height / Math.max(1, App.source.height);
    return {
      x: vp.x + (bounds.minX || 0) * vx,
      y: vp.y + (bounds.minY || 0) * vy,
      width: Math.max(20, (bounds.width || App.source.width) * vx),
      height: Math.max(20, (bounds.height || App.source.height) * vy)
    };
  }

  function applyOverlayViewportForBounds(bounds){ // FIX v8.8
    if (!App.overlay.root || !App.source.image) return;
    bounds = bounds || App.overlay.previewBounds || { minX:0, minY:0, width:App.source.width, height:App.source.height, offsetX:0, offsetY:0 };
    var rect = localBoundsToViewportRect(bounds);
    if (!rect) return;
    var hostRect = updateOverlayClipHost() || { left:0, top:0 }; // FIX v8.9
    App.overlay.root.style.left = Math.round(rect.x - hostRect.left) + 'px'; // FIX v8.9
    App.overlay.root.style.top = Math.round(rect.y - hostRect.top) + 'px'; // FIX v8.9
    App.overlay.root.style.width = Math.max(20, Math.round(rect.width)) + 'px';
    App.overlay.root.style.height = Math.max(20, Math.round(rect.height)) + 'px';
    resizeOverlayCanvas();
  }

  function fitOverlayToSource(){
    if (!App.overlay.root || !App.source.image) return;
    App.overlay.previewBounds = App.overlay.previewBounds || { minX:0, minY:0, maxX:App.source.width, maxY:App.source.height, width:App.source.width, height:App.source.height, offsetX:0, offsetY:0 }; // FIX v7.0
    applyOverlayViewportForBounds(App.overlay.previewBounds); // FIX v7.0
  }

  function resizeOverlayCanvas(){
    if (!App.overlay.canvas || !App.overlay.root || !App.source.image) return;
    var rect = App.overlay.root.getBoundingClientRect();
    var b = App.overlay.previewBounds || { width: App.source.width, height: App.source.height }; // FIX v7.0
    App.overlay.canvas.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(b.width)); // FIX v7.0
    App.overlay.canvas.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(b.height)); // FIX v7.0
    App.overlay.canvas.style.width = rect.width + 'px';
    App.overlay.canvas.style.height = rect.height + 'px';
    if (App.overlay.svgLayer) { // FIX v7.5
      App.overlay.svgLayer.setAttribute('width', String(Math.max(1, Math.round(b.width))));
      App.overlay.svgLayer.setAttribute('height', String(Math.max(1, Math.round(b.height))));
      App.overlay.svgLayer.setAttribute('viewBox', '0 0 ' + Math.max(1, Math.round(b.width)) + ' ' + Math.max(1, Math.round(b.height)));
    }
    App.overlay.root.style.opacity = String(App.overlay.opacity);
  }

  function getOverlayRect(){
    if (!App.overlay.root) return null;
    return App.overlay.root.getBoundingClientRect();
  }

  function clientToOverlayLocal(clientX, clientY){
    var rect = getOverlayRect();
    if (!rect || !App.overlay.canvas) return { x:0, y:0 };
    var b = App.overlay.previewBounds || { offsetX:0, offsetY:0 }; // FIX v7.0
    return {
      x: (clientX - rect.left) / rect.width * App.overlay.canvas.width - (b.offsetX || 0), // FIX v7.0
      y: (clientY - rect.top) / rect.height * App.overlay.canvas.height - (b.offsetY || 0) // FIX v7.0
    };
  }

  function renderBoneList(){
    var list = el('boneList');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = '';
    if (!App.bones.length) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="boneItem"><span class="small">No bones</span></div>';
      return;
    }
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      var div = document.createElement('div');
      div.className = 'boneItem' + (b.id === App.selectedBoneId ? ' active' : '');
      div.innerHTML = '<span>' + escapeHtml(b.name) + '</span><span class="small">' + escapeHtml(boneTypeLabel(b)) + '  parent ' + escapeHtml(getBoneName(b.parentId)) + '  env ' + Math.round(getBoneEnvStart(b)) + '/' + Math.round(getBoneEnvEnd(b)) + '  s ' + round(b.strength) + '</span>'; // FIX v17.0
      div.addEventListener('click', function(){ App.selectedBoneId = b.id; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
      list.appendChild(div);
    });
  }

  function escapeHtml(s){
    return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(ch){ return ({'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'})[ch]; });
  }

  function getBoneById(id){
    id = id == null || id === '' ? null : Number(id);
    for (var i = 0; i < App.bones.length; i++) {
      if (App.bones[i].id === id) return App.bones[i];
    }
    return null;
  }

  function getBoneName(id){
    var b = getBoneById(id);
    return b ? b.name : 'None';
  }

  function getChildBones(parentId){
    return App.bones.filter(function(b){ return Number(b.parentId || 0) === Number(parentId || 0); });
  }

  function boneHasChildren(boneId){ // FIX v4.8
    return getChildBones(boneId).length > 0; // FIX v4.8
  }

  function getDescendantBones(parentId){
    var out = [];
    function walk(id){
      getChildBones(id).forEach(function(child){
        out.push(child);
        walk(child.id);
      });
    }
    walk(parentId);
    return out;
  }

  function isDescendantOf(testId, possibleParentId){
    var children = getDescendantBones(possibleParentId);
    for (var i = 0; i < children.length; i++) {
      if (children[i].id === Number(testId)) return true;
    }
    return false;
  }


  function getFrameBoneById(id){ // FIX v13.2
    id = Number(id || 0);
    return App.frameBones.filter(function(fb){ return Number(fb.id) === id; })[0] || null;
  }

  function getSelectedFrameBone(){ // FIX v13.2
    return getFrameBoneById(App.selectedFrameBoneId);
  }

  function boneLocalFromPoint(bone, point){ // FIX v13.2
    if (!bone) return { u: 0, v: 0 };
    var len = Math.max(1, getLockedBoneLength(bone));
    var dir = normalize({ x: bone.tail.x - bone.head.x, y: bone.tail.y - bone.head.y });
    var perp = { x: -dir.y, y: dir.x };
    var rel = { x: point.x - bone.head.x, y: point.y - bone.head.y };
    return { u: rel.x * dir.x + rel.y * dir.y, v: rel.x * perp.x + rel.y * perp.y, length: len };
  }

  function frameBonePointFromPose(fb, pose){ // FIX v13.2
    if (!fb) return { x: 0, y: 0, angle: 0 };
    var p = fb.point ? clone(fb.point) : { x: 0, y: 0 };
    var angle = 0;
    var bone = getBoneById(fb.attachedBoneId);
    if (bone && pose) {
      var pb = getBonePoseLike(bone, pose);
      var dir = normalize({ x: pb.tail.x - pb.head.x, y: pb.tail.y - pb.head.y });
      var perp = { x: -dir.y, y: dir.x };
      var loc = fb.local || boneLocalFromPoint(bone, p);
      p = { x: pb.head.x + dir.x * loc.u + perp.x * loc.v, y: pb.head.y + dir.y * loc.u + perp.y * loc.v };
      angle = Math.atan2(dir.y, dir.x);
    }
    return { x: p.x, y: p.y, angle: angle };
  }

  function addFrameBoneAtPoint(point, attachBoneId){ // FIX v13.2
    var bone = attachBoneId ? getBoneById(attachBoneId) : getSelectedBone();
    var fb = {
      id: App.nextFrameBoneId++,
      name: 'Frame Bone ' + (App.nextFrameBoneId - 1),
      attachedBoneId: bone ? bone.id : null,
      point: clone(point),
      local: bone ? boneLocalFromPoint(bone, point) : null,
      frameCount: 1,
      scale: 1, // FIX v13.6
      rotationDeg: 0, // FIX v13.6
      frames: {}
    };
    App.frameBones.push(fb);
    App.selectedFrameBoneId = fb.id;
    App.frameBonePinMode = false;
    ensureProxyLayerForCreatedFrameBone(fb); // FIX v13.7: Frame Bones also get a visible Wick proxy key layer immediately
    updateFrameBoneUI();
    renderOverlay();
    log('Added ' + fb.name + (bone ? ' attached to ' + bone.name : ' pinned without attached bone') + '.');
    return fb;
  }

  function addFrameBoneFromMode(){ // FIX v13.2
    var mode = App.frameBoneCreateMode || 'attach';
    var bone = getSelectedBone();
    if (mode === 'pin') {
      App.frameBonePinMode = true;
      App.interaction.addBoneMode = false;
      log('Frame Bone pin mode: click on the SVG to place the frame bone.');
      updateFrameBoneUI();
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    if (!bone) { log('Select a normal bone before attaching a Frame Bone.'); return; }
    addFrameBoneAtPoint(clone(bone.tail), bone.id);
  }

  function deleteSelectedFrameBone(){ // FIX v13.2
    var id = Number(App.selectedFrameBoneId || 0);
    if (!id) return;
    App.frameBones = App.frameBones.filter(function(fb){ return Number(fb.id) !== id; });
    Object.keys(App.frameBoneKeys || {}).forEach(function(fr){
      if (App.frameBoneKeys[fr]) delete App.frameBoneKeys[fr][id];
      if (App.frameBoneKeys[fr] && Object.keys(App.frameBoneKeys[fr]).length === 0) delete App.frameBoneKeys[fr];
    });
    removeProxyLayerForFrameBoneId(id); // FIX v13.7
    App.selectedFrameBoneId = App.frameBones.length ? App.frameBones[0].id : null;
    updateFrameBoneUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function applySelectedFrameBoneCount(){ // FIX v13.2
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb) return;
    var n = clamp(parseInt(el('numFrameBoneFrameCount').value, 10) || 1, 1, 99);
    fb.frameCount = n;
    Object.keys(fb.frames || {}).forEach(function(k){ if (Number(k) > n) delete fb.frames[k]; });
    updateFrameBoneUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function selectedFrameBoneSlot(){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    var max = fb ? Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1)) : 99;
    var stored = el('fileFrameBoneSvgLoader') ? Number(el('fileFrameBoneSvgLoader').getAttribute('data-slot') || 0) : 0;
    return clamp(stored || 1, 1, max);
  }

  function frameBoneSlotTitle(slot){ // FIX v13.6
    return String(slot).padStart(3, '0');
  }

  function setSelectedFrameBoneKeyToSlot(slot){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb) { log('No frame bone selected.'); return; }
    slot = clamp(Number(slot || 1), 1, Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1)));
    if (!App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame]) App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame] = {};
    App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame][fb.id] = slot;
    ensureProxyLayerForCreatedFrameBone(fb); // FIX v13.7
    scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v13.7
    updateFrameBoneUI();
    renderOverlay();
    log('Frame Bone key set on Wick frame ' + App.currentFrame + ': ' + fb.name + ' uses internal SVG frame ' + frameBoneSlotTitle(slot) + '.');
  }

  function selectedFrameBoneKeySlot(){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    var max = fb ? Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1)) : 99;
    return clamp(frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, App.currentFrame), 1, max);
  }

  function promptFrameBoneSvgFileForSlot(slot){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb) { log('No frame bone selected.'); return; }
    var inp = el('fileFrameBoneSvgLoader');
    if (!inp) return;
    slot = clamp(Number(slot || 1), 1, Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1)));
    inp.setAttribute('data-slot', String(slot));
    try { inp.value = ''; } catch(e){}
    inp.click();
  }

  function promptFrameBoneSvgFile(){ // FIX v13.6 compatibility
    promptFrameBoneSvgFileForSlot(1);
  }

  function promptLoadAllFrameBoneSvgs(){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb) { log('No frame bone selected.'); return; }
    var inp = el('fileFrameBoneSvgAllLoader');
    if (!inp) return;
    try { inp.value = ''; } catch(e){}
    inp.click();
  }

  function loadFrameBoneSvgIntoSlot(fb, slot, file){ // FIX v13.6
    if (!fb || !file) return Promise.resolve();
    slot = clamp(Number(slot || 1), 1, Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1)));
    return readFileAsText(file).then(function(raw){
      return loadImageFromFile(file).then(function(loaded){
        fb.frames[slot] = {
          fileName: file.name || ('frame_' + frameBoneSlotTitle(slot) + '.svg'),
          raw: raw,
          dataUrl: loaded.dataUrl,
          width: loaded.image ? (loaded.image.naturalWidth || loaded.image.width || 80) : 80,
          height: loaded.image ? (loaded.image.naturalHeight || loaded.image.height || 80) : 80
        };
      });
    });
  }

  function onFrameBoneSvgFileChosen(file){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb || !file) return;
    var slot = selectedFrameBoneSlot();
    loadFrameBoneSvgIntoSlot(fb, slot, file).then(function(){
      updateFrameBoneUI();
      renderOverlay();
      log('Loaded SVG into ' + fb.name + ' slot ' + frameBoneSlotTitle(slot) + '.');
    }).catch(function(e){ log('Frame Bone SVG load failed: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e)); });
  }

  function slotNumberFromFileName(name, fallback){ // FIX v13.6
    var base = String(name || '');
    var m = base.match(/(?:^|[^0-9])(\d{1,4})(?=\D*$)/);
    if (!m) m = base.match(/(\d{1,4})/);
    var n = m ? Number(m[1]) : Number(fallback || 1);
    return isFinite(n) && n > 0 ? n : Number(fallback || 1);
  }

  function onFrameBoneSvgAllFilesChosen(files){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb || !files || !files.length) return;
    var list = Array.prototype.slice.call(files).filter(function(f){ return f && /\.svg$/i.test(f.name || ''); });
    list.sort(function(a,b){
      var an = slotNumberFromFileName(a.name, 9999);
      var bn = slotNumberFromFileName(b.name, 9999);
      return an === bn ? String(a.name).localeCompare(String(b.name)) : an - bn;
    });
    var tasks = [];
    list.forEach(function(file, idx){
      var namedSlot = slotNumberFromFileName(file.name, idx + 1);
      var slot = clamp(namedSlot, 1, Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1)));
      tasks.push(loadFrameBoneSvgIntoSlot(fb, slot, file));
    });
    Promise.all(tasks).then(function(){
      updateFrameBoneUI();
      renderOverlay();
      log('Loaded ' + tasks.length + ' SVG frame bone image' + (tasks.length === 1 ? '' : 's') + ' into ' + fb.name + '.');
    }).catch(function(e){ log('Load All Frame Bone SVGs failed: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e)); });
  }

  function setSelectedFrameBoneKey(){ // FIX v13.6 compatibility
    setSelectedFrameBoneKeyToSlot(selectedFrameBoneKeySlot());
  }

  function clearSelectedFrameBoneKey(){ // FIX v13.2
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb || !App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame]) return;
    delete App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame][fb.id];
    if (Object.keys(App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame]).length === 0) delete App.frameBoneKeys[App.currentFrame];
    scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v13.7
    updateFrameBoneUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, frameNum){ // FIX v13.6
    if (!fb) return 1;
    frameNum = clamp(Math.round(frameNum || App.currentFrame || 1), 1, App.frameCount);
    if (App.frameBoneKeys[frameNum] && App.frameBoneKeys[frameNum][fb.id]) return clamp(Number(App.frameBoneKeys[frameNum][fb.id]), 1, Math.max(1, fb.frameCount || 1));
    var keys = Object.keys(App.frameBoneKeys || {}).map(Number).filter(function(fr){ return App.frameBoneKeys[fr] && App.frameBoneKeys[fr][fb.id]; }).sort(function(a,b){ return a-b; });
    var prev = null;
    keys.forEach(function(fr){ if (fr <= frameNum) prev = fr; });
    if (prev !== null) return clamp(Number(App.frameBoneKeys[prev][fb.id]), 1, Math.max(1, fb.frameCount || 1));
    return 1;
  }

  function frameBoneScale(fb){ // FIX v13.6
    var s = Number(fb && fb.scale);
    return isFinite(s) && s > 0 ? s : 1;
  }

  function frameBoneRotationRad(fb){ // FIX v13.6
    var d = Number(fb && fb.rotationDeg);
    return (isFinite(d) ? d : 0) * Math.PI / 180;
  }

  function applySelectedFrameBoneTransform(){ // FIX v13.6
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    if (!fb) return;
    var scaleNode = el('numFrameBoneScale');
    var rotNode = el('numFrameBoneRotation');
    fb.scale = clamp(Number(scaleNode ? scaleNode.value : 1) || 1, 0.01, 20);
    fb.rotationDeg = clamp(Number(rotNode ? rotNode.value : 0) || 0, -360, 360);
    updateFrameBoneUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function frameBoneSvgMarkupForFrame(fb, frameNum, pose, ox, oy){ // FIX v13.6
    var slot = frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, frameNum);
    var data = fb && fb.frames ? fb.frames[slot] : null;
    if (!data || !data.dataUrl) return '';
    var fp = frameBonePointFromPose(fb, pose);
    var s = frameBoneScale(fb);
    var w = Math.max(1, Number(data.width || 80)) * s;
    var h = Math.max(1, Number(data.height || 80)) * s;
    var cx = fp.x + (ox || 0);
    var cy = fp.y + (oy || 0);
    var angleDeg = (fp.angle + frameBoneRotationRad(fb)) * 180 / Math.PI;
    return '<image href="' + escapeXmlAttr(data.dataUrl) + '" x="' + round(cx - w * 0.5) + '" y="' + round(cy - h * 0.5) + '" width="' + round(w) + '" height="' + round(h) + '" transform="rotate(' + round(angleDeg) + ' ' + round(cx) + ' ' + round(cy) + ')" />';
  }

  function buildFrameBoneSvgMarkup(frameNum, pose, ox, oy){ // FIX v13.2
    return (App.frameBones || []).map(function(fb){ return frameBoneSvgMarkupForFrame(fb, frameNum, pose, ox, oy); }).join('');
  }

  function drawFrameBonesOnContext(ctx, pose){ // FIX v13.6
    (App.frameBones || []).forEach(function(fb){
      var fp = frameBonePointFromPose(fb, pose);
      var active = Number(fb.id) === Number(App.selectedFrameBoneId || 0);
      var slot = frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, App.currentFrame);
      var data = fb.frames ? fb.frames[slot] : null;
      ctx.save();
      ctx.translate(fp.x, fp.y);
      ctx.rotate((fp.angle || 0) + frameBoneRotationRad(fb));
      ctx.scale(frameBoneScale(fb), frameBoneScale(fb));
      if (data && data.dataUrl && data.imageCache && data.imageCache.complete) {
        var w = Math.max(1, Number(data.width || 80));
        var h = Math.max(1, Number(data.height || 80));
        try { ctx.drawImage(data.imageCache, -w * 0.5, -h * 0.5, w, h); } catch(e){}
      }
      ctx.fillStyle = active ? 'rgba(255, 230, 70, 0.16)' : 'rgba(70, 210, 255, 0.12)';
      ctx.strokeStyle = active ? '#ffe646' : '#48d9ff';
      ctx.lineWidth = active ? 2.5 / frameBoneScale(fb) : 1.5 / frameBoneScale(fb);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.rect(-18, -18, 36, 36);
      ctx.fill(); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(-24, 0); ctx.lineTo(24, 0); ctx.moveTo(0, -24); ctx.lineTo(0, 24); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();
      ctx.save();
      ctx.font = 'bold 10px Arial';
      ctx.lineWidth = 2;
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.85)';
      ctx.strokeText(fb.name + ' ' + frameBoneSlotTitle(slot), fp.x + 8, fp.y - 20);
      ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
      ctx.fillText(fb.name + ' ' + frameBoneSlotTitle(slot), fp.x + 8, fp.y - 20);
      ctx.restore();
    });
  }

  function ensureFrameBoneImageCache(data){ // FIX v13.6
    if (!data || !data.dataUrl || data.imageCache) return;
    var img = new Image();
    img.onload = function(){ renderOverlay(); };
    img.src = data.dataUrl;
    data.imageCache = img;
  }

  function makeFrameBoneSlotCard(fb, slot, mode){ // FIX v13.6
    var card = document.createElement('div');
    var currentSlot = frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, App.currentFrame);
    var data = fb.frames ? fb.frames[slot] : null;
    var hasImage = !!(data && data.dataUrl);
    card.className = 'frameSlotCard' + (Number(slot) === Number(currentSlot) ? ' active' : '') + (hasImage ? ' keyed' : '');
    var title = document.createElement('div');
    title.className = 'frameSlotTitle';
    title.innerHTML = '<span>' + frameBoneSlotTitle(slot) + '</span><span>' + (hasImage ? escapeHtml(data.fileName || 'SVG') : 'blank') + '</span>';
    var thumb = document.createElement('div');
    thumb.className = 'frameSlotThumb';
    if (hasImage) {
      var img = document.createElement('img');
      img.src = data.dataUrl;
      thumb.appendChild(img);
    } else {
      thumb.textContent = 'Blank image area';
    }
    card.appendChild(title);
    card.appendChild(thumb);
    if (mode === 'animate') {
      card.title = 'Click to key this image at Wick frame ' + App.currentFrame;
      card.addEventListener('click', function(){ setSelectedFrameBoneKeyToSlot(slot); });
    } else {
      var btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.className = 'softBtn softBtnSecondary frameSlotButton';
      btn.textContent = 'Load SVG';
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(ev){ ev.stopPropagation(); promptFrameBoneSvgFileForSlot(slot); });
      card.appendChild(btn);
      card.addEventListener('click', function(){ App.selectedFrameBoneId = fb.id; updateFrameBoneUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    }
    return card;
  }

  function renderFrameBoneSlots(containerId, mode){ // FIX v13.6
    var container = el(containerId);
    if (!container) return;
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    container.innerHTML = '';
    if (!fb) { container.textContent = 'No selected frame bone'; return; }
    var count = Math.max(1, Number(fb.frameCount || 1));
    for (var slot = 1; slot <= count; slot++) {
      var data = fb.frames ? fb.frames[slot] : null;
      if (data) ensureFrameBoneImageCache(data);
      container.appendChild(makeFrameBoneSlotCard(fb, slot, mode));
    }
  }

  function updateFrameBoneUI(){ // FIX v13.6
    if (el('selFrameBoneCreateMode')) el('selFrameBoneCreateMode').value = App.frameBoneCreateMode || 'attach';
    if (el('btnAddFrameBoneAttach')) el('btnAddFrameBoneAttach').classList.toggle('active', !App.frameBonePinMode && (App.frameBoneCreateMode || 'attach') === 'attach');
    if (el('btnAddFrameBonePin')) el('btnAddFrameBonePin').classList.toggle('active', !!App.frameBonePinMode || (App.frameBoneCreateMode || 'attach') === 'pin');
    if (el('projectSaveInfo')) el('projectSaveInfo').textContent = 'Source ' + (App.source.fileName || 'none') + '   bones ' + App.bones.length + '   frame bones ' + App.frameBones.length + '   keyed frames ' + Object.keys(App.keyframes || {}).length + '.';
    var fb = getSelectedFrameBone();
    var selectedText = fb ? (fb.name + ' attached=' + getBoneName(fb.attachedBoneId) + ' frames=' + (fb.frameCount || 1) + ' current=' + frameBoneSlotTitle(frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, App.currentFrame))) : (App.frameBonePinMode ? 'Pin mode active: click on SVG' : 'None');
    if (el('selectedFrameBoneInfo')) el('selectedFrameBoneInfo').textContent = selectedText;
    if (el('animateFrameBoneInfo')) el('animateFrameBoneInfo').textContent = fb ? ('Current Wick frame ' + App.currentFrame + ' will use slot ' + frameBoneSlotTitle(frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, App.currentFrame)) + ' unless you click a different image below.') : 'No selected frame bone';
    if (fb && el('numFrameBoneFrameCount') && document.activeElement !== el('numFrameBoneFrameCount')) el('numFrameBoneFrameCount').value = String(fb.frameCount || 1);
    if (fb && el('numFrameBoneScale') && document.activeElement !== el('numFrameBoneScale')) el('numFrameBoneScale').value = String(frameBoneScale(fb));
    if (fb && el('numFrameBoneRotation') && document.activeElement !== el('numFrameBoneRotation')) el('numFrameBoneRotation').value = String(Number(fb.rotationDeg || 0));
    renderFrameBoneSlots('frameBoneSlots', 'setup');
    renderFrameBoneSlots('frameBoneAnimateSlots', 'animate');
    if (el('frameBoneList')) {
      if (!App.frameBones.length) el('frameBoneList').innerHTML = 'No frame bones';
      else {
        el('frameBoneList').innerHTML = '';
        App.frameBones.forEach(function(item){
          var div = document.createElement('div');
          div.className = 'boneItem' + (Number(item.id) === Number(App.selectedFrameBoneId || 0) ? ' active' : '');
          div.innerHTML = '<span>' + escapeHtml(item.name) + '</span><span>bone ' + escapeHtml(getBoneName(item.attachedBoneId)) + '  svg slots ' + Object.keys(item.frames || {}).length + '/' + (item.frameCount || 1) + '</span>';
          div.addEventListener('click', function(){ App.selectedFrameBoneId = item.id; updateFrameBoneUI(); renderOverlay(); });
          el('frameBoneList').appendChild(div);
        });
      }
    }
  }

  function safeJsonClone(obj){
    return obj == null ? obj : JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj));
  }

  function svgTextToDataUrl(svgText){
    return 'data:image/svg+xml;charset=utf-8,' + encodeURIComponent(String(svgText || ''));
  }

  function downloadTextFile(filename, textContent, mimeType){
    var blob = new Blob([String(textContent || '')], { type: mimeType || 'application/json' });
    var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = filename || ('BoneWarp_' + Date.now() + '.json');
    document.body.appendChild(a);
    a.click();
    setTimeout(function(){ try { document.body.removeChild(a); } catch(e){} try { URL.revokeObjectURL(url); } catch(e){} }, 250);
  }

  function buildRigProjectState(){
    return {
      app: 'LukeTools_BoneWarp_Stamp', version: '14.6', savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      source: {
        fileName: App.source.fileName || '', captureMode: App.source.captureMode || 'local-file', selectedIdentifier: App.source.selectedIdentifier || '', selectedUUID: App.source.selectedUUID || '',
        width: Number(App.source.width || 0), height: Number(App.source.height || 0), svgRaw: App.source.svgRaw || '', dataUrl: App.source.dataUrl || App.source.embeddedDataUrl || '',
        stagePlacementBounds: safeJsonClone(App.source.stagePlacementBounds), viewportRect: safeJsonClone(App.source.viewportRect), alphaThreshold: Number(App.source.alphaThreshold || 254)
      },
      flags: safeJsonClone(App.flags), rig: safeJsonClone(App.rig), smooth: safeJsonClone(App.smooth), selectedCurve: safeJsonClone(App.selectedCurve), grid: safeJsonClone(App.grid), // FIX v14.6
      bones: safeJsonClone(App.bones), nextBoneId: Number(App.nextBoneId || 1), selectedBoneId: App.selectedBoneId == null ? null : Number(App.selectedBoneId),
      frameBones: safeJsonClone(App.frameBones), nextFrameBoneId: Number(App.nextFrameBoneId || 1), selectedFrameBoneId: App.selectedFrameBoneId == null ? null : Number(App.selectedFrameBoneId), frameBoneCreateMode: App.frameBoneCreateMode || 'attach', frameBoneKeys: safeJsonClone(App.frameBoneKeys),
      frameCount: Number(App.frameCount || 1), fps: Number(App.fps || 12), currentFrame: Number(App.currentFrame || 1), keyframes: safeJsonClone(App.keyframes)
    };
  }

  function saveRigProjectState(){
    var data = buildRigProjectState();
    var baseName = (App.source.fileName || 'BoneWarp_Project').replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '').replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9_\-]+/g, '_');
    downloadTextFile(baseName + '_BoneWarp_v15_5.json', JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), 'application/json');
    log('Saved Bone Warp project file.');
    updateFrameBoneUI();
  }

  function promptLoadRigProject(){
    var inp = el('fileRigProjectLoader');
    if (!inp) return;
    try { inp.value = ''; } catch(e){}
    inp.click();
  }

  async function loadRigProjectState(data){
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object') throw new Error('Invalid project data.');
    (App.bones || []).map(function(b){ return Number(b.id); }).forEach(function(id){ try { removeProxyLayerForBoneId(id); } catch(e){} });
    App.bones = []; App.keyframes = {}; App.selectedBoneId = null; App.nextBoneId = 1;
    App.frameBones = []; App.frameBoneKeys = {}; App.selectedFrameBoneId = null; App.nextFrameBoneId = 1; App.frameBonePinMode = false; App.frameBoneCreateMode = 'attach'; App.currentFrame = 1;
    if (data.grid) App.grid = Object.assign({}, App.grid, safeJsonClone(data.grid));
    if (data.flags) App.flags = Object.assign({}, App.flags, safeJsonClone(data.flags));
    if (data.rig) App.rig = Object.assign({}, App.rig, safeJsonClone(data.rig));
    if (data.smooth) App.smooth = Object.assign({}, App.smooth, safeJsonClone(data.smooth));
    if (data.selectedCurve) App.selectedCurve = Object.assign({}, App.selectedCurve, safeJsonClone(data.selectedCurve)); // FIX v14.6
    var src = data.source || {};
    App.source.stagePlacementBounds = safeJsonClone(src.stagePlacementBounds) || null;
    App.source.viewportRect = safeJsonClone(src.viewportRect) || null;
    App.source.alphaThreshold = Number(src.alphaThreshold || 254);
    if (src.svgRaw || src.dataUrl) {
      var sourceDataUrl = src.dataUrl || (src.svgRaw ? svgTextToDataUrl(src.svgRaw) : '');
      var img = await loadImageFromUrl(sourceDataUrl);
      var targetW = Math.max(1, Number(src.width || img.naturalWidth || img.width || 1));
      var targetH = Math.max(1, Number(src.height || img.naturalHeight || img.height || 1));
      var svgNative = src.svgRaw ? parseNativeSvg(src.svgRaw, targetW, targetH) : null;
      applyLoadedSourceImage(sourceDataUrl, img, { fileName: src.fileName || 'loaded_svg', mode: src.captureMode || 'local-file', label: src.selectedIdentifier || (src.fileName || 'LoadedImage'), uuid: src.selectedUUID || 'local-file', svgRaw: src.svgRaw || '', svgNative: svgNative, width: targetW, height: targetH });
      App.source.stagePlacementBounds = safeJsonClone(src.stagePlacementBounds) || App.source.stagePlacementBounds;
      App.source.viewportRect = safeJsonClone(src.viewportRect) || App.source.viewportRect;
      App.source.alphaThreshold = Number(src.alphaThreshold || App.source.alphaThreshold || 254);
      buildAlphaMask();
    } else {
      removeOverlay(); App.source.dataUrl = ''; App.source.embeddedDataUrl = ''; App.source.image = null; App.source.width = 0; App.source.height = 0; App.source.fileName = ''; App.source.captureMode = ''; App.source.svgRaw = ''; App.source.svgNative = null; App.source.selectedIdentifier = ''; App.source.selectedUUID = '';
    }
    App.bones = safeJsonClone(data.bones || []);
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){ b.type = normaliseBoneType(b.type); }); // FIX v17.0
    App.nextBoneId = Number(data.nextBoneId || ((App.bones || []).reduce(function(maxId, item){ return Math.max(maxId, Number(item.id || 0)); }, 0) + 1) || 1);
    App.selectedBoneId = data.selectedBoneId == null ? (App.bones[0] ? Number(App.bones[0].id) : null) : Number(data.selectedBoneId);
    App.frameBones = safeJsonClone(data.frameBones || []);
    App.nextFrameBoneId = Number(data.nextFrameBoneId || ((App.frameBones || []).reduce(function(maxId, item){ return Math.max(maxId, Number(item.id || 0)); }, 0) + 1) || 1);
    App.selectedFrameBoneId = data.selectedFrameBoneId == null ? (App.frameBones[0] ? Number(App.frameBones[0].id) : null) : Number(data.selectedFrameBoneId);
    App.frameBoneCreateMode = data.frameBoneCreateMode === 'pin' ? 'pin' : 'attach'; App.frameBoneKeys = safeJsonClone(data.frameBoneKeys || {}); App.keyframes = safeJsonClone(data.keyframes || {});
    App.frameCount = Math.max(1, Number(data.frameCount || App.frameCount || 1)); App.fps = clamp(Number(data.fps || App.fps || 12), 1, 60); App.currentFrame = clamp(Number(data.currentFrame || 1), 1, App.frameCount);
    enforceAllRestChains(); Object.keys(App.keyframes || {}).forEach(function(fr){ if (App.keyframes[fr]) enforceAllPoseChains(App.keyframes[fr]); });
    if (App.source.image) { ensureOverlay(); hideSetAreaVisualFrame(); fitOverlayToSource(); }
    try { syncProxyLayersToBones(true); } catch(e){}
    scheduleProxyFrame(); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); markDirty();
  }

  async function onRigProjectFileChosen(file){
    if (!file) return;
    try { var raw = await readFileAsText(file); var data = JSON.parse(raw); await loadRigProjectState(data); log('Loaded Bone Warp project file: ' + (file.name || 'unnamed file') + '.'); updateFrameBoneUI(); }
    catch(e) { log('Project load failed: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e)); }
  }

  function updateParentSelect(){
    var sel = el('selBoneParent');
    if (!sel) return;
    var b = getSelectedBone();
    sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">None</option>';
    if (!b) {
      sel.disabled = true;
      return;
    }
    sel.disabled = false;
    App.bones.forEach(function(candidate){
      if (candidate.id === b.id) return;
      if (isDescendantOf(candidate.id, b.id)) return;
      var opt = document.createElement('option');
      opt.value = String(candidate.id);
      opt.textContent = candidate.name;
      sel.appendChild(opt);
    });
    sel.value = b.parentId ? String(b.parentId) : '';
  }

  function setSelectedBoneParent(parentId){
    var b = getSelectedBone();
    if (!b) return;
    parentId = parentId ? Number(parentId) : null;
    if (parentId === b.id) return;
    if (parentId && isDescendantOf(parentId, b.id)) {
      log('Parent blocked because it would create a loop.');
      updateParentSelect();
      return;
    }
    var oldHead = clone(b.head);
    var oldTail = clone(b.tail);
    b.parentId = parentId;
    if (parentId) {
      var parent = getBoneById(parentId);
      if (parent) {
        var dx = parent.tail.x - b.head.x;
        var dy = parent.tail.y - b.head.y;
        b.head.x += dx;
        b.head.y += dy;
        b.tail.x += dx;
        b.tail.y += dy;
        var descendants = captureDescendantStateForBone(b.id, null);
        applyDescendantTransformToRest(descendants, { head: oldHead, tail: oldTail }, { head: clone(b.head), tail: clone(b.tail) });
      }
    }
    enforceAllRestChains();
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }


  function buildAlphaMask(){
    App.source.alphaMask = null;
    App.source.opaqueBounds = null;
    if (!App.source.image || !App.source.width || !App.source.height) return;
    try {
      var c = document.createElement('canvas');
      c.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width));
      c.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height));
      var ctx = c.getContext('2d');
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, c.width, c.height);
      ctx.drawImage(App.source.image, 0, 0, c.width, c.height);
      var img = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, c.width, c.height);
      var minX = c.width, minY = c.height, maxX = -1, maxY = -1;
      var th = App.source.alphaThreshold || 8;
      for (var y = 0; y < c.height; y++) {
        for (var x = 0; x < c.width; x++) {
          var a = img.data[(y * c.width + x) * 4 + 3];
          if (a >= th) {
            if (x < minX) minX = x;
            if (y < minY) minY = y;
            if (x > maxX) maxX = x;
            if (y > maxY) maxY = y;
          }
        }
      }
      App.source.alphaMask = { width: c.width, height: c.height, data: img.data };
      if (maxX >= minX && maxY >= minY) App.source.opaqueBounds = { x:minX, y:minY, w:maxX-minX+1, h:maxY-minY+1 };
    } catch(e) {
      App.source.alphaMask = null;
      App.source.opaqueBounds = null;
    }
  }

  function alphaAt(x, y){
    if (!App.rig.meshOpaqueOnly) return 255;
    var m = App.source.alphaMask;
    if (!m || !m.data) return 255;
    var ix = clamp(Math.round(x), 0, m.width - 1);
    var iy = clamp(Math.round(y), 0, m.height - 1);
    return m.data[(iy * m.width + ix) * 4 + 3] || 0;
  }

  function isOpaqueAt(x, y){
    return alphaAt(x, y) >= (App.source.alphaThreshold || 8);
  }

  function getMeshBounds(){ // FIX v4.9
    if (App.rig.meshOpaqueOnly && App.source.opaqueBounds) return clone(App.source.opaqueBounds); // FIX v4.9
    return { x: 0, y: 0, w: App.source.width, h: App.source.height }; // FIX v4.9
  }

  function triangleHasOpaqueContent(a, b, c){
    if (!App.rig.meshOpaqueOnly) return true;
    var samples = [
      a, b, c,
      { x:(a.x + b.x) * 0.5, y:(a.y + b.y) * 0.5 },
      { x:(b.x + c.x) * 0.5, y:(b.y + c.y) * 0.5 },
      { x:(c.x + a.x) * 0.5, y:(c.y + a.y) * 0.5 },
      { x:(a.x + b.x + c.x) / 3, y:(a.y + b.y + c.y) / 3 },
      { x:a.x * 0.6 + b.x * 0.2 + c.x * 0.2, y:a.y * 0.6 + b.y * 0.2 + c.y * 0.2 },
      { x:a.x * 0.2 + b.x * 0.6 + c.x * 0.2, y:a.y * 0.2 + b.y * 0.6 + c.y * 0.2 },
      { x:a.x * 0.2 + b.x * 0.2 + c.x * 0.6, y:a.y * 0.2 + b.y * 0.2 + c.y * 0.6 }
    ];
    for (var i = 0; i < samples.length; i++) {
      if (isOpaqueAt(samples[i].x, samples[i].y)) return true; // FIX v4.9: use image opacity to include any triangle that touches opaque pixels
    }
    return false; // FIX v4.9
  }


  function segmentHasOpaqueContent(a, b){
    if (!App.rig.meshOpaqueOnly) return true;
    var steps = 8;
    for (var i = 0; i <= steps; i++) {
      var t = i / steps;
      if (isOpaqueAt(lerp(a.x, b.x, t), lerp(a.y, b.y, t))) return true; // FIX v4.9: draw mesh segments when they touch opaque pixels
    }
    return false; // FIX v4.9
  }


  function getSelectedBone(){
    for (var i = 0; i < App.bones.length; i++) {
      if (App.bones[i].id === App.selectedBoneId) return App.bones[i];
    }
    return null;
  }

  function getSelectedBoneProp(key, fallback){
    var b = getSelectedBone();
    return b ? b[key] : fallback;
  }

  function getBoneEnvStart(item){
    if (!item) return 90;
    if (item.envStart != null) return item.envStart;
    if (item.radius != null) return item.radius;
    return 90;
  }

  function getBoneEnvEnd(item){
    if (!item) return 90;
    if (item.envEnd != null) return item.envEnd;
    if (item.radius != null) return item.radius;
    return 90;
  }

  function ensurePoseEnvelopeValues(poseBone, bone){
    if (!poseBone) return;
    if (poseBone.envStart == null) poseBone.envStart = getBoneEnvStart(bone);
    if (poseBone.envEnd == null) poseBone.envEnd = getBoneEnvEnd(bone);
  }

  function getBonePoseLike(bone, pose){
    var pb = (pose && poseHasBone(pose, bone.id)) ? pose[bone.id] : null;
    if (pb) ensurePoseEnvelopeValues(pb, bone);
    return {
      head: clone(pb ? pb.head : bone.head),
      tail: clone(pb ? pb.tail : bone.tail),
      envStart: getBoneEnvStart(pb || bone),
      envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(pb || bone)
    };
  }

  function getEnvelopeGeometry(boneLike){
    var head = boneLike.head;
    var tail = boneLike.tail;
    var dir = normalize({ x: tail.x - head.x, y: tail.y - head.y });
    var perp = { x: -dir.y, y: dir.x };
    var s = Math.max(2, getBoneEnvStart(boneLike));
    var e = Math.max(2, getBoneEnvEnd(boneLike));
    return {
      headPos: { x: head.x + perp.x * s, y: head.y + perp.y * s },
      headNeg: { x: head.x - perp.x * s, y: head.y - perp.y * s },
      tailPos: { x: tail.x + perp.x * e, y: tail.y + perp.y * e },
      tailNeg: { x: tail.x - perp.x * e, y: tail.y - perp.y * e },
      perp: perp
    };
  }

  function envelopeWidthFromLocalPoint(startBone, local, whichEnd){
    var head = startBone.head;
    var tail = startBone.tail;
    var dir = normalize({ x: tail.x - head.x, y: tail.y - head.y });
    var perp = { x: -dir.y, y: dir.x };
    var anchor = whichEnd === 'head' ? head : tail;
    var rel = { x: local.x - anchor.x, y: local.y - anchor.y };
    var width = Math.abs(rel.x * perp.x + rel.y * perp.y);
    return clamp(width, 2, 500);
  }

  function ensureWeightMapForBone(bone){
    if (!bone || !App.source.width || !App.source.height) return null;
    var w = App.source.width, h = App.source.height;
    if (!bone.weightMap || bone.weightMap.width !== w || bone.weightMap.height !== h) {
      bone.weightMap = {
        width: w,
        height: h,
        data: new Uint8ClampedArray(w * h),
        canvas: document.createElement('canvas'),
        dirty: true
      };
      bone.weightMap.canvas.width = w;
      bone.weightMap.canvas.height = h;
      bone.weightMap.data.fill(255);
    }
    return bone.weightMap;
  }

  function clearWeightMapForBone(bone){
    if (!bone) return;
    bone.weightMap = null;
  }

  function sampleWeightMap(bone, x, y){
    if (!bone || !bone.weightMap || !bone.weightMap.data) return 1;
    var wm = bone.weightMap;
    var ix = clamp(Math.round(x), 0, wm.width - 1);
    var iy = clamp(Math.round(y), 0, wm.height - 1);
    return (wm.data[iy * wm.width + ix] || 0) / 255;
  }

  function rebuildWeightMapCanvas(bone){
    if (!bone || !bone.weightMap || !bone.weightMap.canvas) return;
    var wm = bone.weightMap;
    if (!wm.dirty) return;
    var ctx = wm.canvas.getContext('2d');
    var img = ctx.createImageData(wm.width, wm.height);
    for (var i = 0; i < wm.data.length; i++) {
      var v = wm.data[i] / 255;
      var show = 1 - v;
      var o = i * 4;
      img.data[o] = 255;
      img.data[o + 1] = 80;
      img.data[o + 2] = 40;
      img.data[o + 3] = Math.round(show * 180);
    }
    ctx.putImageData(img, 0, 0);
    wm.dirty = false;
  }

  function paintWeightStampAt(local){
    var bone = getSelectedBone();
    if (!bone || !App.source.image) return false;
    var wm = ensureWeightMapForBone(bone);
    if (!wm) return false;
    var size = Math.max(1, App.paint.brushSize);
    var radius = size * 0.5;
    var x0 = Math.max(0, Math.floor(local.x - radius - 1));
    var y0 = Math.max(0, Math.floor(local.y - radius - 1));
    var x1 = Math.min(wm.width - 1, Math.ceil(local.x + radius + 1));
    var y1 = Math.min(wm.height - 1, Math.ceil(local.y + radius + 1));
    var changed = false;
    for (var y = y0; y <= y1; y++) {
      for (var x = x0; x <= x1; x++) {
        var dx = x - local.x;
        var dy = y - local.y;
        var d = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy);
        if (d > radius) continue;
        var t = 1 - (d / Math.max(1, radius));
        var falloff = t * t;
        var idx = y * wm.width + x;
        var current = wm.data[idx] / 255;
        var next = App.paint.action === 'erase'
          ? current * (1 - App.paint.brushStrength * falloff)
          : current + (1 - current) * App.paint.brushStrength * falloff;
        next = clamp(next, 0, 1);
        var nextByte = Math.round(next * 255);
        if (nextByte !== wm.data[idx]) {
          wm.data[idx] = nextByte;
          changed = true;
        }
      }
    }
    if (changed) wm.dirty = true;
    return changed;
  }

  function paintWeightStroke(fromLocal, toLocal){
    if (!fromLocal || !toLocal) return;
    var step = Math.max(1, App.paint.brushSize * 0.35);
    var d = dist(fromLocal, toLocal);
    var count = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(d / step));
    for (var i = 0; i <= count; i++) {
      var t = count <= 0 ? 0 : i / count;
      paintWeightStampAt({ x: lerp(fromLocal.x, toLocal.x, t), y: lerp(fromLocal.y, toLocal.y, t) });
    }
  }

  function drawWeightPaintOverlay(ctx, bone){
    if (!App.paint.showOverlay || !bone || !bone.weightMap) return;
    rebuildWeightMapCanvas(bone);
    ctx.save();
    ctx.globalAlpha = App.paint.enabled ? 0.8 : 0.55;
    ctx.drawImage(bone.weightMap.canvas, 0, 0);
    ctx.restore();
  }

  function nearestBoneEndpoint(point, ignoreId){
    var best = null;
    App.bones.forEach(function(bone){
      if (ignoreId && bone.id === ignoreId) return;
      var endpoints = [
        { bone: bone, type: 'head', point: bone.head },
        { bone: bone, type: 'tail', point: bone.tail }
      ];
      endpoints.forEach(function(ep){
        var d = dist(point, ep.point);
        if (!best || d < best.distance) best = { bone: ep.bone, type: ep.type, point: ep.point, distance: d };
      });
    });
    return best;
  }

  function autoConnectNewBone(a, b){
    var out = { head: clone(a), tail: clone(b), parentId: App.selectedBoneId || null, connected: false, connectedTo: null };
    if (!App.rig.autoConnect || !App.bones.length) {
      if (out.parentId) {
        var fallbackParent = getBoneById(out.parentId);
        if (fallbackParent) {
          var dx0 = fallbackParent.tail.x - out.head.x;
          var dy0 = fallbackParent.tail.y - out.head.y;
          out.head.x += dx0;
          out.head.y += dy0;
          out.tail.x += dx0;
          out.tail.y += dy0;
          out.connected = true;
          out.connectedTo = { bone: fallbackParent, type: 'tail', point: fallbackParent.tail, distance: 0 };
        }
      }
      return out;
    }
    var maxD = Math.max(1, App.rig.connectDistance || 18);
    var headHit = nearestBoneEndpoint(a, null);
    var tailHit = nearestBoneEndpoint(b, null);

    // A real IK chain means child.head shares the exact same coordinate as parent.tail.
    if (headHit && headHit.distance <= maxD && headHit.type === 'tail') {
      out.head = clone(headHit.point);
      out.parentId = headHit.bone.id;
      out.connected = true;
      out.connectedTo = headHit;
    } else if (tailHit && tailHit.distance <= maxD && tailHit.type === 'tail') {
      // User drew backwards. Flip it so the new bone head is connected to parent tail.
      out.head = clone(tailHit.point);
      out.tail = clone(a);
      out.parentId = tailHit.bone.id;
      out.connected = true;
      out.connectedTo = tailHit;
    } else if (App.selectedBoneId) {
      var selectedParent = getBoneById(App.selectedBoneId);
      if (selectedParent) {
        var dx = selectedParent.tail.x - out.head.x;
        var dy = selectedParent.tail.y - out.head.y;
        out.head.x += dx;
        out.head.y += dy;
        out.tail.x += dx;
        out.tail.y += dy;
        out.parentId = selectedParent.id;
        out.connected = true;
        out.connectedTo = { bone: selectedParent, type: 'tail', point: selectedParent.tail, distance: 0 };
      }
    }

    if (out.connected && out.connectedTo) log('Chain connected new bone head to ' + out.connectedTo.bone.name + ' tail.');
    if (dist(out.head, out.tail) < 5) out.tail = { x: out.head.x + 20, y: out.head.y };
    return out;
  }


  function addBone(a, b){
    var connected = autoConnectNewBone(a, b);
    var defaultEnvelope = 32; // FIX v7.7: keep new bones at a sensible default envelope size instead of scaling huge
    var bone = {
      id: App.nextBoneId++,
      name: 'Bone ' + (App.nextBoneId - 1),
      parentId: connected.parentId,
      head: { x: connected.head.x, y: connected.head.y },
      tail: { x: connected.tail.x, y: connected.tail.y },
      restLength: Math.max(1, dist(connected.head, connected.tail)), // FIX v4.7: locked bone length
      radius: defaultEnvelope, // FIX v7.7
      envStart: defaultEnvelope, // FIX v7.7
      envEnd: defaultEnvelope, // FIX v7.7
      strength: 1,
      type: normaliseBoneType(App.newBoneType) // FIX v17.0
    };
    App.bones.push(bone);
    App.selectedBoneId = bone.id;
    enforceAllRestChains();
    // FIX v12.4: creating a new bone must not add that bone to every existing animation keyframe.
    // The bone stays at rest until the user actually moves that bone in Animate mode.
    ensureProxyLayerForCreatedBone(bone); // FIX v10.9: create the real Wick proxy layer immediately when the bone is created
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }


  function deleteSelectedBone(){
    if (!App.selectedBoneId) {
      log('Select a bone first. Delete Bone only removes the currently selected bone.'); // FIX v13.3
      return;
    }
    var deletedId = App.selectedBoneId;
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      if (Number(b.parentId || 0) === Number(deletedId)) b.parentId = null;
    });
    App.bones = App.bones.filter(function(b){ return b.id !== deletedId; });
    removeProxyLayerForBoneId(deletedId); // FIX v10.9: remove the matching Wick proxy layer when the bone is deleted
    Object.keys(App.keyframes).forEach(function(fr){
      if (App.keyframes[fr] && App.keyframes[fr][deletedId]) delete App.keyframes[fr][deletedId];
      if (App.keyframes[fr] && Object.keys(App.keyframes[fr]).length === 0) delete App.keyframes[fr]; // FIX v13.3
    });
    App.selectedBoneId = null; // FIX v13.3: do not auto select another bone after delete. The next delete requires the user to select another bone.
    App.interaction.boneId = null; // FIX v13.3
    App.interaction.hoverBoneId = null; // FIX v13.3
    App.interaction.hoverHandle = ''; // FIX v13.3
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones') App.interaction.addBoneMode = true; // FIX v13.2
    log('Deleted selected bone. Select another bone before using Delete Bone again.'); // FIX v13.3
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function clearBones(){
    App.bones = [];
    App.keyframes = {};
    App.frameBones = []; // FIX v13.2
    App.frameBoneKeys = {}; // FIX v13.2
    App.selectedFrameBoneId = null; // FIX v13.2
    App.nextFrameBoneId = 1; // FIX v13.2
    App.selectedBoneId = null;
    App.nextBoneId = 1;
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones') App.interaction.addBoneMode = true; // FIX v13.2
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function renameSelectedBone(){
    var b = getSelectedBone();
    if (!b) return;
    b.name = (el('inpBoneName').value || '').trim() || b.name;
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function setSelectedBoneType(value){ // FIX v17.0
    App.newBoneType = normaliseBoneType(value);
    var b = getSelectedBone();
    if (b) {
      b.type = App.newBoneType;
