      if (isStretchyBone(b)) b.restLength = boneLengthFromPoseItem(b);
      else setItemTailToLockedLength(b, b);
      updateUI();
      renderOverlay();
      scheduleProxyFrame();
    }
  }

  function boneLengthFromPoseItem(item){
    if (!item || !item.head || !item.tail) return 1;
    return Math.max(1, dist(item.head, item.tail));
  }

  function getLockedBoneLength(bone){ // FIX v4.7
    if (!bone) return 1;
    if (typeof bone.restLength !== 'number' || !isFinite(bone.restLength) || bone.restLength <= 0) {
      bone.restLength = boneLengthFromPoseItem(bone);
    }
    return Math.max(1, bone.restLength);
  }

  function getBoneLengthForItem(bone, item){ // FIX v17.0
    if (isStretchyBone(bone) && item && item.head && item.tail) return boneLengthFromPoseItem(item);
    return getLockedBoneLength(bone);
  }

  function setItemTailToLockedLength(item, bone){ // FIX v4.7
    if (!item || !item.head || !item.tail || !bone) return;
    if (isStretchyBone(bone)) { // FIX v17.0: stretchy bones keep their current tail distance instead of being forced back to rest length.
      item.angle = Math.atan2(item.tail.y - item.head.y, item.tail.x - item.head.x);
      if (item === bone) bone.restLength = boneLengthFromPoseItem(bone);
      return;
    }
    var length = getLockedBoneLength(bone);
    if (typeof item.angle === 'number' && isFinite(item.angle)) { // FIX v8.6: keep explicit full rotation angle when present
      item.tail = tailFromAngle(item.head, item.angle, length);
      return;
    }
    var dir = normalize({ x: item.tail.x - item.head.x, y: item.tail.y - item.head.y });
    item.tail = { x: item.head.x + dir.x * length, y: item.head.y + dir.y * length };
    item.angle = Math.atan2(item.tail.y - item.head.y, item.tail.x - item.head.x); // FIX v8.6
  }

  function enforceAllBoneRestLengths(){ // FIX v4.7
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){ setItemTailToLockedLength(b, b); });
  }

  function enforcePoseBoneLengths(pose){ // FIX v4.7
    if (!pose) return;
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      if (!pose[b.id]) pose[b.id] = { head: clone(b.head), tail: clone(b.tail) };
      setItemTailToLockedLength(pose[b.id], b);
    });
  }

  function translatePoseItem(item, dx, dy){
    item.head.x += dx;
    item.head.y += dy;
    item.tail.x += dx;
    item.tail.y += dy;
  }

  function enforceChildConnectionRest(parentId){
    var parent = getBoneById(parentId);
    if (!parent) return;
    getChildBones(parentId).forEach(function(child){
      var old = { head: clone(child.head), tail: clone(child.tail) };
      var dx = parent.tail.x - child.head.x;
      var dy = parent.tail.y - child.head.y;
      child.head.x += dx;
      child.head.y += dy;
      child.tail.x += dx;
      child.tail.y += dy;
      setItemTailToLockedLength(child, child); // FIX v4.7
      var descendants = captureDescendantStateForBone(child.id, null);
      applyDescendantTransformToRest(descendants, old, { head: clone(child.head), tail: clone(child.tail) });
      enforceChildConnectionRest(child.id);
    });
  }

  function enforceAllRestChains(){
    enforceAllBoneRestLengths(); // FIX v4.7
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      if (!b.parentId) enforceChildConnectionRest(b.id);
    });
    enforceAllBoneRestLengths(); // FIX v4.7
  }

  function getParentAngleForBoneFromPose(bone, pose){ // FIX v13.0: child keys use angle relative to their parent, not world angle
    if (!bone || !bone.parentId) return 0;
    var parentBone = getBoneById(bone.parentId);
    if (!parentBone) return 0;
    var parentItem = poseHasBone(pose, parentBone.id) ? pose[parentBone.id] : parentBone;
    return angleOfItem(parentItem);
  }

  function getLocalAngleForBoneItem(bone, item, parentItem){ // FIX v13.0
    if (!bone || !bone.parentId) return angleOfItem(item);
    if (item && typeof item.localAngle === 'number' && isFinite(item.localAngle)) return item.localAngle;
    var parentAngle = parentItem ? angleOfItem(parentItem) : getParentAngleForBoneFromPose(bone, null);
    return angleOfItem(item) - parentAngle;
  }

  function writeLocalAngleForBoneItem(bone, item, pose){ // FIX v13.0
    if (!bone || !item) return item;
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(item, bone);
    if (bone.parentId) item.localAngle = angleOfItem(item) - getParentAngleForBoneFromPose(bone, pose);
    else delete item.localAngle;
    return item;
  }

  function enforceChildConnectionPose(pose, parentId, sourcePose){ // FIX v12.9: child bones stay physically connected to the parent tail while preserving local rotation offset
    if (!pose) return;
    var parentBone = getBoneById(parentId);
    if (!parentBone) return;
    if (!pose[parentId]) pose[parentId] = { head: clone(parentBone.head), tail: clone(parentBone.tail) };
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(pose[parentId], parentBone);
    var source = sourcePose || pose;
    var sourceParent = poseHasBone(source, parentId) ? clone(source[parentId]) : clone(pose[parentId]);
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(sourceParent, parentBone);
    var parentFinalAngle = angleOfItem(pose[parentId]);
    var parentSourceAngle = angleOfItem(sourceParent);
    getChildBones(parentId).forEach(function(child){
      var sourceChild = poseHasBone(source, child.id) ? clone(source[child.id]) : (poseHasBone(pose, child.id) ? clone(pose[child.id]) : { head: clone(child.head), tail: clone(child.tail) });
      copyEnvAndAngleFallback(sourceChild, child);
      var childLocalAngle = getLocalAngleForBoneItem(child, sourceChild, sourceParent); // FIX v13.0: use keyed local angle relative to parent when present
      var finalAngle = parentFinalAngle + childLocalAngle; // FIX v13.0
      pose[child.id] = {
        head: clone(pose[parentId].tail), // FIX v12.9: hard lock child head to parent tail
        tail: tailFromAngle(pose[parentId].tail, finalAngle, getBoneLengthForItem(child, sourceChild)), // FIX v17.0
        angle: finalAngle,
        localAngle: childLocalAngle, // FIX v13.0
        envStart: getBoneEnvStart(sourceChild),
        envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(sourceChild)
      };
      copyEnvAndAngleFallback(pose[child.id], child);
      enforceChildConnectionPose(pose, child.id, source);
    });
  }

  function enforceAllPoseChains(pose, sourcePose){ // FIX v12.8: preserve child local pose while parents animate
    if (!pose) return;
    enforcePoseBoneLengths(pose); // FIX v4.7
    var source = sourcePose || clone(pose);
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      if (!b.parentId) enforceChildConnectionPose(pose, b.id, source);
    });
    enforcePoseBoneLengths(pose); // FIX v4.7
  }

  function getRestPose(){
    enforceAllBoneRestLengths(); // FIX v4.7
    var pose = {};
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      pose[b.id] = { head: clone(b.head), tail: clone(b.tail), angle: Math.atan2(b.tail.y - b.head.y, b.tail.x - b.head.x), envStart: getBoneEnvStart(b), envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(b) }; // FIX v8.6
    });
    return pose;
  }

  function poseHasBone(pose, boneId){
    return !!(pose && pose[boneId] && pose[boneId].head && pose[boneId].tail);
  }

  function getSortedKeyFrames(){
    return Object.keys(App.keyframes).map(function(v){ return Number(v); }).filter(function(v){ return !isNaN(v); }).sort(function(a,b){ return a-b; });
  }

  function keyFramesForBoneId(boneId){ // FIX v12.4
    return Object.keys(App.keyframes).map(function(v){ return Number(v); }).filter(function(f){
      return !isNaN(f) && App.keyframes[f] && App.keyframes[f][boneId];
    }).sort(function(a,b){ return a-b; });
  }

  function restPoseItemForBone(b){ // FIX v13.0
    var item = { head: clone(b.head), tail: clone(b.tail), angle: Math.atan2(b.tail.y - b.head.y, b.tail.x - b.head.x), envStart: getBoneEnvStart(b), envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(b) };
    if (b && b.parentId) {
      var parent = getBoneById(b.parentId);
      if (parent) item.localAngle = item.angle - Math.atan2(parent.tail.y - parent.head.y, parent.tail.x - parent.head.x);
    }
    return item;
  }

  function interpolateBonePoseItem(b, pA, pB, t){ // FIX v12.4
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(pA, b);
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(pB, b);
    var interpHead = { x: lerp(pA.head.x, pB.head.x, t), y: lerp(pA.head.y, pB.head.y, t) };
    var interpAngle = lerp(pA.angle, pB.angle, t);
    var interpLocalAngle = null; // FIX v13.0
    if (b && b.parentId) {
      var rest = restPoseItemForBone(b);
      var aLocal = (typeof pA.localAngle === 'number' && isFinite(pA.localAngle)) ? pA.localAngle : (typeof rest.localAngle === 'number' ? rest.localAngle : 0);
      var bLocal = (typeof pB.localAngle === 'number' && isFinite(pB.localAngle)) ? pB.localAngle : (typeof rest.localAngle === 'number' ? rest.localAngle : 0);
      interpLocalAngle = lerp(aLocal, bLocal, t);
    }
    var interpLength = isStretchyBone(b) ? lerp(boneLengthFromPoseItem(pA), boneLengthFromPoseItem(pB), t) : getLockedBoneLength(b); // FIX v17.0
    var result = {
      head: interpHead,
      tail: tailFromAngle(interpHead, interpAngle, interpLength),
      angle: interpAngle,
      envStart: lerp(getBoneEnvStart(pA), getBoneEnvStart(pB), t),
      envEnd: lerp(getBoneEnvEnd(pA), getBoneEnvEnd(pB), t)
    };
    if (interpLocalAngle !== null) result.localAngle = interpLocalAngle; // FIX v13.0
    return result;
  }

  function getPoseForFrame(frame){ // FIX v12.4
    frame = clamp(Math.round(frame), 1, App.frameCount);
    var out = {};
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      var boneKeys = keyFramesForBoneId(b.id);
      var rest = restPoseItemForBone(b);
      if (!boneKeys.length) { out[b.id] = rest; return; }
      var prev = null, next = null;
      for (var i = 0; i < boneKeys.length; i++) {
        if (boneKeys[i] <= frame) prev = boneKeys[i];
        if (boneKeys[i] >= frame) { next = boneKeys[i]; break; }
      }
      if (prev !== null && prev === frame && App.keyframes[prev] && App.keyframes[prev][b.id]) {
        out[b.id] = clone(App.keyframes[prev][b.id]); copyEnvAndAngleFallback(out[b.id], b); return;
      }
      if (prev !== null && next !== null && prev !== next) {
        out[b.id] = interpolateBonePoseItem(b, clone(App.keyframes[prev][b.id]), clone(App.keyframes[next][b.id]), (frame - prev) / (next - prev)); return;
      }
      if (prev !== null && App.keyframes[prev] && App.keyframes[prev][b.id]) { out[b.id] = clone(App.keyframes[prev][b.id]); copyEnvAndAngleFallback(out[b.id], b); return; }
      if (next !== null && App.keyframes[next] && App.keyframes[next][b.id]) { out[b.id] = clone(App.keyframes[next][b.id]); copyEnvAndAngleFallback(out[b.id], b); return; }
      out[b.id] = rest;
    });
    ensurePoseAngles(out);
    var rawPoseForChain = clone(out); // FIX v12.8: keep the independently keyed pose so children can inherit parent motion without holding the same world angle
    enforceAllPoseChains(out, rawPoseForChain);
    ensurePoseAngles(out);
    return out;
  }


  function captureDescendantStateForBone(boneId, pose){ // FIX v12.6: restored missing chain helper used by pose enforcement and drag setup
    return getDescendantBones(boneId).map(function(child){
      var source = pose && poseHasBone(pose, child.id) ? pose[child.id] : { head: child.head, tail: child.tail };
      return { id: child.id, head: clone(source.head), tail: clone(source.tail) };
    });
  }

  function transformPointFromBoneChange(point, oldBone, newBone){ // FIX v12.6: restored descendant transform helper
    var oh = oldBone.head;
    var ot = oldBone.tail;
    var nh = newBone.head;
    var nt = newBone.tail;
    var oldDir = normalize({ x: ot.x - oh.x, y: ot.y - oh.y });
    var newDir = normalize({ x: nt.x - nh.x, y: nt.y - nh.y });
    var oldPerp = { x: -oldDir.y, y: oldDir.x };
    var newPerp = { x: -newDir.y, y: newDir.x };
    var rel = { x: point.x - oh.x, y: point.y - oh.y };
    var u = rel.x * oldDir.x + rel.y * oldDir.y;
    var v = rel.x * oldPerp.x + rel.y * oldPerp.y;
    var scale = 1;
    return {
      x: nh.x + newDir.x * u * scale + newPerp.x * v * scale,
      y: nh.y + newDir.y * u * scale + newPerp.y * v * scale
    };
  }

  function getCurrentBonePoseForTransform(bone, pose){ // FIX v12.6
    if (pose && poseHasBone(pose, bone.id)) return pose[bone.id];
    return { head: clone(bone.head), tail: clone(bone.tail) };
  }

  function applyDescendantTransformToRest(startDescendants, oldParentBone, newParentBone){ // FIX v12.6
    startDescendants.forEach(function(item){
      var b = getBoneById(item.id);
      if (!b) return;
      b.head = transformPointFromBoneChange(item.head, oldParentBone, newParentBone);
      b.tail = transformPointFromBoneChange(item.tail, oldParentBone, newParentBone);
      b.angle = Math.atan2(b.tail.y - b.head.y, b.tail.x - b.head.x);
    });
  }

  function applyDescendantTransformToPose(pose, startDescendants, oldParentBone, newParentBone){ // FIX v12.6
    startDescendants.forEach(function(item){
      var b = getBoneById(item.id);
      if (!b) return;
      if (!pose[item.id]) pose[item.id] = { head: clone(b.head), tail: clone(b.tail) };
      pose[item.id].head = transformPointFromBoneChange(item.head, oldParentBone, newParentBone);
      pose[item.id].tail = transformPointFromBoneChange(item.tail, oldParentBone, newParentBone);
      pose[item.id].angle = Math.atan2(pose[item.id].tail.y - pose[item.id].head.y, pose[item.id].tail.x - pose[item.id].head.x);
      pose[item.id].envStart = getBoneEnvStart(b);
      pose[item.id].envEnd = getBoneEnvEnd(b);
    });
  }

  function solveIKOnPose(pose, boneId, target){
    var chain = getBoneChainToRoot(boneId);
    if (!chain.length) return;
    chain.forEach(function(b){
      if (!pose[b.id]) pose[b.id] = { head: clone(b.head), tail: clone(b.tail) };
    });

    var joints = [];
    var lengths = [];
    for (var i = 0; i < chain.length; i++) {
      var pb = pose[chain[i].id];
      if (i === 0) joints.push(clone(pb.head));
      joints.push(clone(pb.tail));
      lengths.push(getLockedBoneLength(chain[i])); // FIX v4.7: IK uses locked rest length, not stretched pose length
    }

    var root = clone(joints[0]);
    var totalLength = lengths.reduce(function(a, b){ return a + b; }, 0);
    var rootToTarget = dist(root, target);

    if (App.rig.mode === 'splineIk') {
      solveSplineIKJoints(joints, lengths, root, target);
    } else if (rootToTarget >= totalLength) {
      var dir = normalize({ x: target.x - root.x, y: target.y - root.y });
      joints[0] = clone(root);
      for (var ui = 0; ui < lengths.length; ui++) {
        joints[ui + 1] = {
          x: joints[ui].x + dir.x * lengths[ui],
          y: joints[ui].y + dir.y * lengths[ui]
        };
      }
    } else {
      var tolerance = 0.5;
      for (var iter = 0; iter < 18; iter++) {
        joints[joints.length - 1] = clone(target);
        for (var bi = joints.length - 2; bi >= 0; bi--) {
          var backwardDir = normalize({ x: joints[bi].x - joints[bi + 1].x, y: joints[bi].y - joints[bi + 1].y });
          joints[bi] = {
            x: joints[bi + 1].x + backwardDir.x * lengths[bi],
            y: joints[bi + 1].y + backwardDir.y * lengths[bi]
          };
        }
        joints[0] = clone(root);
        for (var fi = 0; fi < joints.length - 1; fi++) {
          var forwardDir = normalize({ x: joints[fi + 1].x - joints[fi].x, y: joints[fi + 1].y - joints[fi].y });
          joints[fi + 1] = {
            x: joints[fi].x + forwardDir.x * lengths[fi],
            y: joints[fi].y + forwardDir.y * lengths[fi]
          };
        }
        if (dist(joints[joints.length - 1], target) <= tolerance) break;
      }
    }

    for (var ci = 0; ci < chain.length; ci++) {
      pose[chain[ci].id] = { head: clone(joints[ci]), tail: clone(joints[ci + 1]), angle: Math.atan2(joints[ci + 1].y - joints[ci].y, joints[ci + 1].x - joints[ci].x), envStart: getBoneEnvStart(chain[ci]), envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(chain[ci]) }; // FIX v8.6
    }
    enforceAllPoseChains(pose);
  }


  function solveIKOnRest(boneId, target){
    var pose = getRestPose();
    solveIKOnPose(pose, boneId, target);
    Object.keys(pose).forEach(function(id){
      var b = getBoneById(Number(id));
      if (!b) return;
      b.head = clone(pose[id].head);
      b.tail = clone(pose[id].tail);
    });
    enforceAllRestChains();
  }


  function ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame(){ // FIX v12.4
    if (!App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]) App.keyframes[App.currentFrame] = {};
    ensurePoseAngles(App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]);
    return App.keyframes[App.currentFrame];
  }

  function ensureEditableBoneKeyAtCurrentFrame(boneId, sourcePose){ // FIX v12.4
    var bone = getBoneById(Number(boneId));
    if (!bone) return null;
    var framePose = ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame();
    if (!framePose[bone.id]) {
      var pose = sourcePose || getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame);
      framePose[bone.id] = poseHasBone(pose, bone.id) ? clone(pose[bone.id]) : restPoseItemForBone(bone);
    }
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(framePose[bone.id], bone);
    writeLocalAngleForBoneItem(bone, framePose[bone.id], sourcePose || getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame)); // FIX v13.0
    return framePose[bone.id];
  }

  function removeEmptyKeyFrame(frame){ // FIX v12.4
    if (App.keyframes[frame] && Object.keys(App.keyframes[frame]).length === 0) delete App.keyframes[frame];
  }

  function setCurrentKeyForBoneFromPose(boneId, pose){ // FIX v12.4
    var bone = getBoneById(Number(boneId));
    if (!bone) return;
    var sourcePose = pose || getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame);
    if (!App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]) App.keyframes[App.currentFrame] = {};
    App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][bone.id] = poseHasBone(sourcePose, bone.id) ? clone(sourcePose[bone.id]) : restPoseItemForBone(bone);
    copyEnvAndAngleFallback(App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][bone.id], bone);
    writeLocalAngleForBoneItem(bone, App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][bone.id], sourcePose); // FIX v13.0
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
    syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame();
  }

  function setCurrentKeyFromPose(pose){ // FIX v12.4
    if (!App.selectedBoneId) { log('Select a bone before setting a key.'); return; }
    setCurrentKeyForBoneFromPose(App.selectedBoneId, pose || getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame));
  }

  function clearCurrentKey(){ // FIX v12.4
    if (App.selectedBoneId && App.keyframes[App.currentFrame] && App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][App.selectedBoneId]) {
      delete App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][App.selectedBoneId];
      removeEmptyKeyFrame(App.currentFrame);
    } else {
      delete App.keyframes[App.currentFrame];
    }
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
    syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v10.9
  }

  function resetCurrentToRest(){ // FIX v12.4
    if (!App.selectedBoneId) { log('Select a bone before resetting a key.'); return; }
    var bone = getBoneById(App.selectedBoneId);
    if (!bone) return;
    if (!App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]) App.keyframes[App.currentFrame] = {};
    App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][bone.id] = restPoseItemForBone(bone);
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
    syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v10.9
  }

  function copyPreviousPose(){
    var keys = getSortedKeyFrames().filter(function(f){ return f < App.currentFrame; });
    if (!keys.length) {
      log('No previous keyframe found.');
      return;
    }
    App.keyframes[App.currentFrame] = clone(App.keyframes[keys[keys.length - 1]]);
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
    syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v10.9
  }

  function frameFromScrubClientX(clientX){ // FIX v8.3
    var ind = el('wickFrameIndicator'); // FIX v8.3
    if (!ind) return App.currentFrame; // FIX v8.3
    var rect = ind.getBoundingClientRect(); // FIX v8.3
    var pct = rect.width <= 0 ? 0 : clamp((clientX - rect.left) / rect.width, 0, 1); // FIX v8.3
    return clamp(Math.round(1 + pct * Math.max(0, App.frameCount - 1)), 1, App.frameCount); // FIX v8.3
  }

  function scrubToClientX(clientX, pushToWick){ // FIX v8.3
    syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline(); // FIX v8.3
    setCurrentFrame(frameFromScrubClientX(clientX), !!pushToWick); // FIX v8.3
  }

  function startFrameIndicatorScrub(e){ // FIX v8.3
    var ind = el('wickFrameIndicator'); // FIX v8.3
    if (!ind) return; // FIX v8.3
    if (App.playing) stop(false); // FIX v8.3
    App.scrubbingFrameIndicator = true; // FIX v8.3
    App.scrubWasFollowing = !!App.flags.followWick; // FIX v8.3
    App.flags.followWick = false; // FIX v8.3
    var evt = e.touches && e.touches.length ? e.touches[0] : e; // FIX v8.3
    if (e.preventDefault) e.preventDefault(); // FIX v8.3
    scrubToClientX(evt.clientX, false); // FIX v8.5: tool scrubber must not push Wick timeline
    function move(ev){ // FIX v8.3
      var mev = ev.touches && ev.touches.length ? ev.touches[0] : ev; // FIX v8.3
      if (ev.preventDefault) ev.preventDefault(); // FIX v8.3
      scrubToClientX(mev.clientX, false); // FIX v8.5
    }
    function up(ev){ // FIX v8.3
      var uev = ev.changedTouches && ev.changedTouches.length ? ev.changedTouches[0] : ev; // FIX v8.3
      if (ev.preventDefault) ev.preventDefault(); // FIX v8.3
      scrubToClientX(uev.clientX, false); // FIX v8.5
      App.scrubbingFrameIndicator = false; // FIX v8.3
      App.flags.followWick = !!App.scrubWasFollowing; // FIX v8.3
      App.scrubWasFollowing = null; // FIX v8.3
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', move, true); // FIX v8.3
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', up, true); // FIX v8.3
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', move, true); // FIX v8.3
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', up, true); // FIX v8.3
      updateUI(); // FIX v8.3
    }
    window.addEventListener('mousemove', move, true); // FIX v8.3
    window.addEventListener('mouseup', up, true); // FIX v8.3
    window.addEventListener('touchmove', move, true); // FIX v8.3
    window.addEventListener('touchend', up, true); // FIX v8.3
  }

  function setCurrentFrame(frame, pushToWick){
    App.currentFrame = clamp(Math.round(frame), 1, App.frameCount);
    if (pushToWick) setWickTimelineFrame(App.currentFrame);
    updateUI();
    renderOverlay();
    syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v10.9
  }

  function setWickTimelineFrame(frame){ // FIX v8.4
    frame = clamp(Math.round(Number(frame) || 1), 1, App.frameCount || 1); // FIX v8.4
    var tl = getSelectedTimeline();
    try { if (tl) tl.playheadPosition = frame; } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (tl) tl._playheadPosition = frame; } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.project) App.project.currentFrameNumber = frame; } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.project) App.project.playheadPosition = frame; } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.gotoFrame === 'function') App.ed.gotoFrame(frame); } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.project) App.ed.project.currentFrameNumber = frame; } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.render === 'function') App.ed.render(); } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.refresh === 'function') App.ed.refresh(); } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.setCurrentFrame === 'function') App.B.setCurrentFrame(frame); } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.B && typeof App.B.refreshCanvas === 'function') App.B.refreshCanvas(); } catch(e){} // FIX v8.4
    markDirty();
  }

  function syncFromWickTimeline(){
    if (!App.flags.followWick) return;
    syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
    var tl = getSelectedTimeline();
    var viewSig = getStageViewSignature(); // FIX v8.8
    var viewChanged = viewSig && viewSig !== App.lastStageViewSignature; // FIX v8.8
    App.lastStageViewSignature = viewSig || App.lastStageViewSignature; // FIX v8.8
    if (!tl) {
      if (viewChanged) renderOverlay(); // FIX v8.8
      return;
    }
    var pos = 1;
    try { pos = Number(tl.playheadPosition || App.project.currentFrameNumber || 1); } catch(e){}
    pos = clamp(Math.round(pos), 1, App.frameCount);
    if (pos !== App.currentFrame || viewChanged) { // FIX v8.8: Wick pan and zoom change the display only, not keyframes.
      App.currentFrame = pos;
      updateUI();
      renderOverlay();
      syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v10.9
    }
  }

  function startFollowWick(){
    if (App.wickFollowTimer) clearInterval(App.wickFollowTimer);
    App.wickFollowTimer = setInterval(syncFromWickTimeline, 120);
  }

  function play(){
    stop(false); // FIX v8.2
    syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline(); // FIX v8.2
    App.playing = true;
    App.playWasFollowing = !!App.flags.followWick; // FIX v8.2
    App.flags.followWick = false; // FIX v8.2: follow Wick was resetting the preview frame during playback.
    var frameDuration = 1000 / Math.max(1, App.fps);
    var lastTime = 0;
    function tick(now){
      if (!App.playing) return;
      if (!lastTime) lastTime = now;
      if (now - lastTime >= frameDuration) {
        lastTime = now;
        var n = App.currentFrame + 1;
        if (n > App.frameCount) n = 1;
        setCurrentFrame(n, false); // FIX v8.5: tool preview play must not drive Wick timeline
        updateUI();
        renderOverlay();
      }
      App.playRaf = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    }
    App.playRaf = requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    updateUI();
  }

  function stop(restoreFollow){
    App.playing = false;
    if (App.playTimer) clearInterval(App.playTimer);
    App.playTimer = null;
    if (App.playRaf) cancelAnimationFrame(App.playRaf); // FIX v8.2
    App.playRaf = null; // FIX v8.2
    if (restoreFollow !== false && App.playWasFollowing != null) { // FIX v8.2
      App.flags.followWick = !!App.playWasFollowing;
      App.playWasFollowing = null;
    }
    updateUI();
  }

  function pointToSegmentDistance(p, a, b){
    var abx = b.x - a.x, aby = b.y - a.y;
    var apx = p.x - a.x, apy = p.y - a.y;
    var ab2 = abx*abx + aby*aby;
    if (ab2 <= 0.000001) return { d: dist(p, a), t: 0, closest: { x:a.x, y:a.y } };
    var t = clamp((apx*abx + apy*aby) / ab2, 0, 1);
    var cx = a.x + abx*t, cy = a.y + aby*t;
    var dx = p.x - cx, dy = p.y - cy;
    return { d: Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy), t: t, closest: { x:cx, y:cy } };
  }

  function normalize(v){
    var len = Math.sqrt(v.x*v.x + v.y*v.y) || 1;
    return { x: v.x/len, y: v.y/len, len: len };
  }

  function tailFromRotationOnly(startBone, target, lockedLength){ // FIX v4.7
    var length = Math.max(1, lockedLength || startBone.restLength || dist(startBone.head, startBone.tail));
    var dir = normalize({ x: target.x - startBone.head.x, y: target.y - startBone.head.y });
    return { x: startBone.head.x + dir.x * length, y: startBone.head.y + dir.y * length };
  }

  function angleOfItem(item){ // FIX v8.6
    if (!item || !item.head || !item.tail) return 0;
    if (typeof item.angle === 'number' && isFinite(item.angle)) return item.angle;
    return Math.atan2(item.tail.y - item.head.y, item.tail.x - item.head.x);
  }

  function rawAngleOfPoints(head, point){ // FIX v8.6
    return Math.atan2(point.y - head.y, point.x - head.x);
  }

  function wrappedAngleDelta(fromAngle, toAngle){ // FIX v8.6
    var d = toAngle - fromAngle;
    while (d > Math.PI) d -= Math.PI * 2;
    while (d < -Math.PI) d += Math.PI * 2;
    return d;
  }

  function tailFromAngle(head, angle, lockedLength){ // FIX v8.6
    var length = Math.max(1, lockedLength || 1);
    return { x: head.x + Math.cos(angle) * length, y: head.y + Math.sin(angle) * length };
  }

  function setPoseItemAngleAndTail(item, angle, lockedLength){ // FIX v8.6
    if (!item || !item.head) return;
    item.angle = angle;
    item.tail = tailFromAngle(item.head, angle, lockedLength || dist(item.head, item.tail));
  }

  function ensurePoseAngles(pose){ // FIX v8.6
    if (!pose) return pose;
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      if (!pose[b.id]) return;
      if (typeof pose[b.id].angle !== 'number' || !isFinite(pose[b.id].angle)) pose[b.id].angle = Math.atan2(pose[b.id].tail.y - pose[b.id].head.y, pose[b.id].tail.x - pose[b.id].head.x);
    });
    return pose;
  }

  function copyEnvAndAngleFallback(item, bone){ // FIX v13.0
    if (!item) return item;
    ensurePoseEnvelopeValues(item, bone);
    if (typeof item.angle !== 'number' || !isFinite(item.angle)) item.angle = Math.atan2(item.tail.y - item.head.y, item.tail.x - item.head.x);
    if (bone && bone.parentId) {
      if (typeof item.localAngle !== 'number' || !isFinite(item.localAngle)) {
        var parent = getBoneById(bone.parentId);
        if (parent) item.localAngle = item.angle - Math.atan2(parent.tail.y - parent.head.y, parent.tail.x - parent.head.x);
      }
    } else if (item.localAngle != null) {
      delete item.localAngle;
    }
    return item;
  }

  function movedFarEnough(a, b){ // FIX v4.7
    return !!(a && b && dist(a, b) >= 8);
  }

  function skinPointByPose(p, pose){
    if (!App.bones.length) return { x:p.x, y:p.y };
    var sumW = 0;
    var sumX = 0;
    var sumY = 0;
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      var rest = { head: b.head, tail: b.tail };
      var cur = poseHasBone(pose, b.id) ? pose[b.id] : rest;
      var distInfo = pointToSegmentDistance(p, rest.head, rest.tail);
      var envStart = getBoneEnvStart(cur);
      var envEnd = getBoneEnvEnd(cur);
      var radius = Math.max(1, lerp(envStart, envEnd, distInfo.t)); // FIX v6.3: envelope width varies from head to tail
      if (distInfo.d > radius) return;
      var w = 1 - (distInfo.d / radius);
      w = w * w * (b.strength || 1);
      w *= sampleWeightMap(b, p.x, p.y); // FIX v6.4: per bone weight painting multiplies local influence
      var restDirV = { x: rest.tail.x - rest.head.x, y: rest.tail.y - rest.head.y };
      var curDirV = { x: cur.tail.x - cur.head.x, y: cur.tail.y - cur.head.y };
      var restDir = normalize(restDirV);
      var curDir = normalize(curDirV);
      var restPerp = { x: -restDir.y, y: restDir.x };
      var curPerp = { x: -curDir.y, y: curDir.x };
      var rel = { x: p.x - rest.head.x, y: p.y - rest.head.y };
      var u = rel.x * restDir.x + rel.y * restDir.y;
      var v = rel.x * restPerp.x + rel.y * restPerp.y;
      var restLen = Math.max(0.0001, Math.sqrt(restDirV.x * restDirV.x + restDirV.y * restDirV.y)); // FIX v17.1
      var curLen = Math.max(0.0001, Math.sqrt(curDirV.x * curDirV.x + curDirV.y * curDirV.y)); // FIX v17.1
      var scaleU = isStretchyBone(b) ? (curLen / restLen) : 1; // FIX v17.1: stretchy bones pull curve points along the bone axis as the tail stretches.
      var scaleV = 1; // FIX v17.1: do not thicken or squash the curve sideways when a stretchy bone changes length.
      var tx = cur.head.x + curDir.x * u * scaleU + curPerp.x * v * scaleV; // FIX v17.1
      var ty = cur.head.y + curDir.y * u * scaleU + curPerp.y * v * scaleV; // FIX v17.1
      sumX += tx * w;
      sumY += ty * w;
      sumW += w;
    });
    if (sumW <= 0.00001) return { x:p.x, y:p.y };
    return { x: sumX / sumW, y: sumY / sumW };
  }

  function buildRestVertices(){
    var cols = App.grid.cols;
    var rows = App.grid.rows;
    var bounds = getMeshBounds(); // FIX v4.9
    var verts = [];
    for (var y = 0; y <= rows; y++) {
      for (var x = 0; x <= cols; x++) {
        verts.push({
          x: bounds.x + (x / cols) * bounds.w, // FIX v4.9: mesh is built over the opaque image bounds instead of the full image area
          y: bounds.y + (y / rows) * bounds.h // FIX v4.9
        });
      }
    }
    return verts;
  }

  function buildWarpedVertices(pose){
    var rest = buildRestVertices();
    return rest.map(function(p){ return skinPointByPose(p, pose); });
  }

  function vertexIndex(x, y){ return y * (App.grid.cols + 1) + x; }

  function expandTriangleAroundCentroid(a, b, c, amount){ // FIX v6.1
    var cx = (a.x + b.x + c.x) / 3; // FIX v6.1
    var cy = (a.y + b.y + c.y) / 3; // FIX v6.1
    function pullOut(p){ // FIX v6.1
      var dx = p.x - cx; // FIX v6.1
      var dy = p.y - cy; // FIX v6.1
      var len = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) || 1; // FIX v6.1
      return { x: p.x + (dx / len) * amount, y: p.y + (dy / len) * amount }; // FIX v6.1
    }
    return [pullOut(a), pullOut(b), pullOut(c)]; // FIX v6.1
  }

  function drawImageTriangle(ctx, img, sx0, sy0, sx1, sy1, sx2, sy2, dx0, dy0, dx1, dy1, dx2, dy2){
    var denom = sx0*(sy1 - sy2) + sx1*(sy2 - sy0) + sx2*(sy0 - sy1);
    if (Math.abs(denom) < 0.00001) return;
    var a = (dx0*(sy1 - sy2) + dx1*(sy2 - sy0) + dx2*(sy0 - sy1)) / denom;
    var b = (dy0*(sy1 - sy2) + dy1*(sy2 - sy0) + dy2*(sy0 - sy1)) / denom;
    var c = (dx0*(sx2 - sx1) + dx1*(sx0 - sx2) + dx2*(sx1 - sx0)) / denom;
    var d = (dy0*(sx2 - sx1) + dy1*(sx0 - sx2) + dy2*(sx1 - sx0)) / denom;
    var e = (dx0*(sx1*sy2 - sx2*sy1) + dx1*(sx2*sy0 - sx0*sy2) + dx2*(sx0*sy1 - sx1*sy0)) / denom;
    var f = (dy0*(sx1*sy2 - sx2*sy1) + dy1*(sx2*sy0 - sx0*sy2) + dy2*(sx0*sy1 - sx1*sy0)) / denom;
    var grown = expandTriangleAroundCentroid( // FIX v6.1
      { x: dx0, y: dy0 }, // FIX v6.1
      { x: dx1, y: dy1 }, // FIX v6.1
      { x: dx2, y: dy2 }, // FIX v6.1
      1.1 // FIX v6.1: overlaps neighbouring triangles slightly so mesh seams do not stamp as transparent lines
    );
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(grown[0].x, grown[0].y); // FIX v6.1
    ctx.lineTo(grown[1].x, grown[1].y); // FIX v6.1
    ctx.lineTo(grown[2].x, grown[2].y); // FIX v6.1
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.clip();
    ctx.imageSmoothingEnabled = true; // FIX v6.1
    ctx.setTransform(a, b, c, d, e, f);
    ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
    ctx.restore();
  }

  function renderWarpToContext(ctx, pose, renderOpts){
    renderOpts = renderOpts || {}; // FIX v6.9
    if (App.source.svgNative && App.source.svgNative.shapes && App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) { // FIX v7.5
      renderNativeSvgToContext(ctx, pose, renderOpts); // FIX v7.5: SVG source is drawn as vector curves, not as image mesh.
      return; // FIX v7.5
    }
    var img = App.source.image;
    if (!img) return;
    var w = Number(renderOpts.canvasWidth || App.source.width || 0); // FIX v6.9
    var h = Number(renderOpts.canvasHeight || App.source.height || 0); // FIX v6.9
    var ox = Number(renderOpts.offsetX || 0); // FIX v6.9
    var oy = Number(renderOpts.offsetY || 0); // FIX v6.9
    var rest = buildRestVertices();
    var warped = buildWarpedVertices(pose);
    ctx.save();
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);

    if (App.flags.showImage) {
      for (var y = 0; y < App.grid.rows; y++) {
        for (var x = 0; x < App.grid.cols; x++) {
          var i00 = vertexIndex(x, y);
          var i10 = vertexIndex(x+1, y);
          var i01 = vertexIndex(x, y+1);
          var i11 = vertexIndex(x+1, y+1);
          var s00 = rest[i00], s10 = rest[i10], s01 = rest[i01], s11 = rest[i11];
          var d00 = warped[i00], d10 = warped[i10], d01 = warped[i01], d11 = warped[i11];
          if (triangleHasOpaqueContent(s00, s10, s11)) drawImageTriangle(ctx, img, s00.x, s00.y, s10.x, s10.y, s11.x, s11.y, d00.x + ox, d00.y + oy, d10.x + ox, d10.y + oy, d11.x + ox, d11.y + oy); // FIX v6.9
          if (triangleHasOpaqueContent(s00, s11, s01)) drawImageTriangle(ctx, img, s00.x, s00.y, s11.x, s11.y, s01.x, s01.y, d00.x + ox, d00.y + oy, d11.x + ox, d11.y + oy, d01.x + ox, d01.y + oy); // FIX v6.9
        }
      }
    }

    if (App.flags.showMesh) {
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(83, 207, 255, 0.18)'; // FIX v6.6
      ctx.lineWidth = 1;
      for (var yy = 0; yy <= App.grid.rows; yy++) {
        ctx.beginPath();
        for (var xx = 0; xx <= App.grid.cols; xx++) {
          var vi = vertexIndex(xx, yy);
          var pt = warped[vi];
          var rpt = rest[vi];
          if (xx === 0) ctx.moveTo(pt.x + ox, pt.y + oy);
          else {
            var pvi = vertexIndex(xx - 1, yy);
            if (segmentHasOpaqueContent(rest[pvi], rpt)) ctx.lineTo(pt.x + ox, pt.y + oy);
            else ctx.moveTo(pt.x + ox, pt.y + oy);
          }
        }
        ctx.stroke();
      }
      for (var xx2 = 0; xx2 <= App.grid.cols; xx2++) {
        ctx.beginPath();
        for (var yy2 = 0; yy2 <= App.grid.rows; yy2++) {
          var vi2 = vertexIndex(xx2, yy2);
          var pt2 = warped[vi2];
          var rpt2 = rest[vi2];
          if (yy2 === 0) ctx.moveTo(pt2.x + ox, pt2.y + oy);
          else {
            var pvi2 = vertexIndex(xx2, yy2 - 1);
            if (segmentHasOpaqueContent(rest[pvi2], rpt2)) ctx.lineTo(pt2.x + ox, pt2.y + oy);
            else ctx.moveTo(pt2.x + ox, pt2.y + oy);
          }
        }
        ctx.stroke();
      }
    }
    ctx.restore();
  }

  function drawParentLinks(ctx, pose){
    ctx.save();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 211, 90, 0.55)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
    ctx.setLineDash([6, 5]);
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      if (!b.parentId) return;
      var parent = getBoneById(b.parentId);
      if (!parent) return;
      var pp = poseHasBone(pose, parent.id) ? pose[parent.id] : { head: parent.head, tail: parent.tail };
      var cp = poseHasBone(pose, b.id) ? pose[b.id] : { head: b.head, tail: b.tail };
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(pp.tail.x, pp.tail.y);
      ctx.lineTo(cp.head.x, cp.head.y);
      ctx.stroke();
    });
    ctx.restore();
  }

  function drawEnvelopeOnContext(ctx, bone, poseBone, active, hover){
    var head = poseBone.head;
    var tail = poseBone.tail;
    var s = Math.max(2, getBoneEnvStart(poseBone));
    var e = Math.max(2, getBoneEnvEnd(poseBone));
    var dir = normalize({ x: tail.x - head.x, y: tail.y - head.y });
    var perp = { x: -dir.y, y: dir.x };

    var headPos = { x: head.x + perp.x * s, y: head.y + perp.y * s };
    var headNeg = { x: head.x - perp.x * s, y: head.y - perp.y * s };
    var tailPos = { x: tail.x + perp.x * e, y: tail.y + perp.y * e };
    var tailNeg = { x: tail.x - perp.x * e, y: tail.y - perp.y * e };

    ctx.save();

    // FIX v6.6: draw a clean influence envelope using two circular caps plus a simple connecting body.
    // This avoids the messy crossing arc artefacts from the previous variable radius capsule path.
    ctx.fillStyle = active ? 'rgba(150, 78, 255, 0.10)' : 'rgba(150, 78, 255, 0.045)';
    ctx.strokeStyle = hover ? 'rgba(255, 176, 64, 0.95)' : (active ? 'rgba(180, 110, 255, 0.95)' : 'rgba(140, 95, 255, 0.50)');
    ctx.lineWidth = active ? 2.5 : 1.5;

    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(headPos.x, headPos.y);
    ctx.lineTo(tailPos.x, tailPos.y);
    ctx.lineTo(tailNeg.x, tailNeg.y);
    ctx.lineTo(headNeg.x, headNeg.y);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.stroke();

    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(head.x, head.y, s, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.stroke();

    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.arc(tail.x, tail.y, e, 0, Math.PI * 2);
    ctx.fill();
    ctx.stroke();

    var showHandles = active || hover;
    if (showHandles) {
      [
        { p: headPos, handle: 'envHeadPos' },
        { p: headNeg, handle: 'envHeadNeg' },
        { p: tailPos, handle: 'envTailPos' },
        { p: tailNeg, handle: 'envTailNeg' }
      ].forEach(function(item){
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.arc(item.p.x, item.p.y, 5, 0, Math.PI * 2); // FIX v8.1: envelope handles reduced to about one third size
        ctx.fillStyle = (App.interaction.hoverHandle === item.handle || App.interaction.dragType === item.handle) ? '#ffff00' : '#c77cff'; // FIX v6.6
        ctx.fill();
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
        ctx.lineWidth = 2; // FIX v8.1
        ctx.stroke();
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#22113a';
        ctx.lineWidth = 1; // FIX v8.1
        ctx.stroke();
      });
    }
    ctx.restore();
  }

  function drawBoneOnContext(ctx, bone, poseBone, active, hover, localMode){
    var head = localMode ? bone.head : poseBone.head;
    var tail = localMode ? bone.tail : poseBone.tail;
    ctx.save();

    // FIX v6.6: stronger bone visibility.
    ctx.lineCap = 'round';
    ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.78)';
    ctx.lineWidth = active ? 4 : 3.5; // FIX v8.1: bone line reduced to about one third size
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(head.x, head.y);
    ctx.lineTo(tail.x, tail.y);
    ctx.stroke();

    ctx.strokeStyle = active ? '#ffe05c' : (hover ? '#ff9f5a' : '#38d6ff');
    ctx.lineWidth = active ? 2.5 : 2; // FIX v8.1
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(head.x, head.y);
    ctx.lineTo(tail.x, tail.y);
    ctx.stroke();

    function circle(x,y, fill, r){
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(x, y, r, 0, Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle = fill;
      ctx.fill();
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#ffffff';
      ctx.lineWidth = 2; // FIX v8.1
      ctx.stroke();
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#00131f';
      ctx.lineWidth = 1; // FIX v8.1
      ctx.stroke();
    }
    circle(head.x, head.y, active ? '#ffff00' : '#31c7ff', active ? 6 : 5); // FIX v8.1: head handle reduced to about one third size
    circle(tail.x, tail.y, active ? '#ffb000' : '#00ffd0', active ? 6 : 5); // FIX v8.1: tail handle reduced to about one third size

    ctx.font = active ? 'bold 11px Arial' : 'bold 10px Arial'; // FIX v8.1
    var tx = ((head.x + tail.x) * 0.5) + 6;
    var ty = ((head.y + tail.y) * 0.5) - 6;
    ctx.lineWidth = 2; // FIX v8.1
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.8)';
    ctx.strokeText(bone.name, tx, ty);
    ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
    ctx.fillText(bone.name, tx, ty);
    ctx.restore();
  }


  function getStageNavFallbackViewportRect(){ // FIX v9.6
    var hostRect = App.overlay && App.overlay.clipHost ? App.overlay.clipHost.getBoundingClientRect() : getWickStageClipRect(); // FIX v9.6
    if (!hostRect) return null; // FIX v9.6
    var w = Math.min(390, Math.max(260, hostRect.width * 0.34)); // FIX v9.6
    var h = 96; // FIX v9.6
    return { // FIX v9.6
      left: hostRect.left + hostRect.width - w - 10, // FIX v9.6
      top: hostRect.top + hostRect.height - h - 10, // FIX v9.6
      width: w, // FIX v9.6
      height: h // FIX v9.6
    }; // FIX v9.6
  }

  function getWickNavigationViewportRect(){ // FIX v9.6
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null; // FIX v9.6
    var hostRect = App.overlay && App.overlay.clipHost ? App.overlay.clipHost.getBoundingClientRect() : getWickStageClipRect(); // FIX v9.6
    if (!pdoc || !hostRect) return getStageNavFallbackViewportRect(); // FIX v9.6
    var best = null; // FIX v9.6
    var bestScore = -Infinity; // FIX v9.6
    var nodes = []; // FIX v9.6
    try { nodes = Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('div,button,section,nav')); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.6
    nodes.forEach(function(n){ // FIX v9.6
      try { // FIX v9.6
        if (!n || n === App.overlay.clipHost || (App.overlay.clipHost && App.overlay.clipHost.contains(n))) return; // FIX v9.6
        var r = n.getBoundingClientRect(); // FIX v9.6
        if (!r || r.width < 80 || r.height < 28 || r.width > 520 || r.height > 150) return; // FIX v9.6
        var cs = pdoc.defaultView.getComputedStyle(n); // FIX v9.6
        if (!cs || cs.display === 'none' || cs.visibility === 'hidden' || Number(cs.opacity || 1) <= 0.05) return; // FIX v9.6
        var overlapsStage = r.right > hostRect.left && r.left < hostRect.right && r.bottom > hostRect.top && r.top < hostRect.bottom; // FIX v9.6
        if (!overlapsStage) return; // FIX v9.6
        var nearBottom = Math.abs(r.bottom - hostRect.bottom); // FIX v9.6
        var nearRight = Math.abs(r.right - hostRect.right); // FIX v9.6
        var score = 0; // FIX v9.6
        if (nearBottom < 140) score += 120 - nearBottom; // FIX v9.6
        if (nearRight < 180) score += 90 - nearRight * 0.4; // FIX v9.6
        if (String(n.className || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('zoom') >= 0) score += 40; // FIX v9.6
        if (String(n.className || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('stage') >= 0) score += 20; // FIX v9.6
        if (String(n.textContent || '').trim().length < 6) score += 8; // FIX v9.6
        if (score > bestScore) { // FIX v9.6
          bestScore = score; // FIX v9.6
          best = { left:r.left, top:r.top, width:r.width, height:r.height, node:n }; // FIX v9.6
        } // FIX v9.6
      } catch(e){} // FIX v9.6
    }); // FIX v9.6
    if (!best || bestScore < 15) return getStageNavFallbackViewportRect(); // FIX v9.6
    try { raiseWickNavigationControls(best.node); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.8
    return best; // FIX v9.6
  }

  function raiseWickNavigationControls(navNode){ // FIX v9.8
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null; // FIX v9.8
    if (!pdoc) return; // FIX v9.8
    var node = navNode || null; // FIX v9.8
    if (!node) { // FIX v9.8
      try { // FIX v9.8
        var guess = getWickNavigationViewportRect(); // FIX v9.8
        node = guess && guess.node ? guess.node : null; // FIX v9.8
      } catch(e){} // FIX v9.8
    } // FIX v9.8
    if (!node || !node.style) return; // FIX v9.8
    try { node.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-raised-nav', '1'); } catch(e){} // FIX v9.8
    try { // FIX v9.8
      var currentPosition = pdoc.defaultView.getComputedStyle(node).position; // FIX v9.8
      if (!currentPosition || currentPosition === 'static') node.style.position = 'relative'; // FIX v9.8
      node.style.zIndex = '960'; // FIX v10.1: above BoneWarp stage layer at 950, below LukeTools panel
      node.style.pointerEvents = 'auto'; // FIX v9.8
      node.style.isolation = 'isolate'; // FIX v9.8
    } catch(e){} // FIX v9.8
    // FIX v10.1: Do not climb parent nodes or change the Set Area / stage layer stack.
    // Only the detected Wick navigation control itself is raised, and only to 960 so it stays below the LukeTools panel.
  }

  function getNavigationExclusionLocalRect(){ // FIX v9.6
    if (!App.overlay || !App.overlay.root || !App.overlay.canvas) return null; // FIX v9.6
    var rootRect = App.overlay.root.getBoundingClientRect(); // FIX v9.6
    var nav = getWickNavigationViewportRect(); // FIX v9.6
    if (!rootRect || !nav || rootRect.width <= 0 || rootRect.height <= 0) return null; // FIX v9.6
    var canvasW = Math.max(1, App.overlay.canvas.width || 1); // FIX v9.6
    var canvasH = Math.max(1, App.overlay.canvas.height || 1); // FIX v9.6
    var pad = 12; // FIX v9.6
    var x = ((nav.left - pad) - rootRect.left) / rootRect.width * canvasW; // FIX v9.6
    var y = ((nav.top - pad) - rootRect.top) / rootRect.height * canvasH; // FIX v9.6
    var w = (nav.width + pad * 2) / rootRect.width * canvasW; // FIX v9.6
    var h = (nav.height + pad * 2) / rootRect.height * canvasH; // FIX v9.6
    var ix = Math.max(0, Math.floor(x)); // FIX v9.6
    var iy = Math.max(0, Math.floor(y)); // FIX v9.6
    var ax = Math.min(canvasW, Math.ceil(x + w)); // FIX v9.6
    var ay = Math.min(canvasH, Math.ceil(y + h)); // FIX v9.6
    if (ax <= 0 || ay <= 0 || ix >= canvasW || iy >= canvasH || ax <= ix || ay <= iy) return null; // FIX v9.6
    return { x:ix, y:iy, width:ax - ix, height:ay - iy, canvasW:canvasW, canvasH:canvasH }; // FIX v9.6
  }

  function buildSvgPreviewClipWrapper(innerMarkup){ // FIX v9.8
    // FIX v9.8: no SVG cutout. Raise the real Wick navigation controls above BoneWarp instead.
    try { getWickNavigationViewportRect(); } catch(e){}
    return innerMarkup;
  }

  function clearNavigationExclusionOnCanvas(ctx){ // FIX v9.8
    // FIX v9.8: no cutout. The native Wick navigation controls are raised above BoneWarp instead.
    try { getWickNavigationViewportRect(); } catch(e){}
  }

  function buildNativeSvgPreviewMarkup(pose, ox, oy){ // FIX v7.5
    if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) return '';
    var body = [];
    var nativeOriginX = 0; // FIX v15.1: preview is drawn in overlay space, so do not use commit origin offsets here.
    var nativeOriginY = 0; // FIX v15.1: prevents ReferenceError during overlay mouse movement.
    App.source.svgNative.shapes.forEach(function(shape){
      var d = '';
      if (shape.cmdSubpaths && shape.cmdSubpaths.length) {
        shape.cmdSubpaths.forEach(function(sp){
          var warpedCmds = (sp.commands || []).map(function(cmd){
            var out = { type: cmd.type };
            if (cmd.p) { var pp = skinPointByPose(cmd.p, pose); out.p = { x: pp.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: pp.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; } // FIX v15.0
            if (cmd.c1) { var pc1 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c1, pose); out.c1 = { x: pc1.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: pc1.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; } // FIX v15.0
            if (cmd.c2) { var pc2 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c2, pose); out.c2 = { x: pc2.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: pc2.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; } // FIX v15.0
            return out;
          });
          warpedCmds = smoothNativeCommandsForOutput(warpedCmds); // FIX v8.7
          d += pathCommandsToD(warpedCmds) + ' ';
        });
      } else if (shape.subpaths && shape.subpaths.length) {
        shape.subpaths.forEach(function(sp){
          var warped = sp.points.map(function(p){ var q = skinPointByPose(p, pose); return { x: q.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: q.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; }); // FIX v15.0
          d += pointsToSubpath(warped, sp.closed) + ' ';
        });
      }
      if (d.trim()) body.push('<path d="' + escapeXmlAttr(d.trim()) + '"' + styleMapToAttrs(shape.style) + ' />');
    });
    body.push(buildFrameBoneSvgMarkup(App.currentFrame, pose, ox || 0, oy || 0)); // FIX v13.2
    return body.join('');
  }

  function updateNativeSvgPreviewLayer(pose, ox, oy){ // FIX v7.5
    if (!App.overlay.svgLayer) return false;
    if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) {
      App.overlay.svgLayer.innerHTML = '';
      App.overlay.svgLayer.style.display = 'none';
      return false;
    }
    App.overlay.svgLayer.style.display = 'block';
    App.overlay.svgLayer.innerHTML = buildSvgPreviewClipWrapper(buildNativeSvgPreviewMarkup(pose, ox || 0, oy || 0)); // FIX v9.6
    return true;
  }

  function renderOverlay(){
    if (!App.overlay.canvas || !App.source.image) return;

    var pose;
    if (isRestBoneEditContext()) { // FIX v16.6
      pose = getRestPose();
    } else {
      pose = getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame);
    }

    App.overlay.previewBounds = getPreviewBoundsForPose(pose); // FIX v7.0
    applyOverlayViewportForBounds(App.overlay.previewBounds); // FIX v7.0

    var ctx = App.overlay.ctx;
    var w = App.overlay.canvas.width;
    var h = App.overlay.canvas.height;
    var ox = App.overlay.previewBounds ? App.overlay.previewBounds.offsetX || 0 : 0; // FIX v7.0
    var oy = App.overlay.previewBounds ? App.overlay.previewBounds.offsetY || 0 : 0; // FIX v7.0
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, w, h);

    var nativePreview = updateNativeSvgPreviewLayer(pose, ox, oy); // FIX v7.5
    if (!nativePreview) { // FIX v7.5
      renderWarpToContext(ctx, pose, { canvasWidth: w, canvasHeight: h, offsetX: ox, offsetY: oy }); // FIX v7.0
    }

    ctx.save(); // FIX v7.0
    ctx.translate(ox, oy); // FIX v7.0

    if (App.flags.showBones) {
      var selected = getSelectedBone();
      if (selected) drawWeightPaintOverlay(ctx, selected);
      App.bones.forEach(function(b){
        var pb = getBonePoseLike(b, pose);
        drawEnvelopeOnContext(ctx, b, pb, b.id === App.selectedBoneId, b.id === App.interaction.hoverBoneId);
      });
      drawParentLinks(ctx, pose);
      App.bones.forEach(function(b){
        var pb = getBonePoseLike(b, pose);
        drawBoneOnContext(ctx, b, pb, b.id === App.selectedBoneId, b.id === App.interaction.hoverBoneId, App.activeTab === 'bones' || App.activeTab === 'editbone'); // FIX v16.6
      });
      drawFrameBonesOnContext(ctx, pose); // FIX v13.2
    }

    if (App.paint.enabled && App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.interaction.hoverLocal) {
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = App.paint.action === 'erase' ? 'rgba(255,100,60,0.95)' : 'rgba(110,255,140,0.95)';
      ctx.lineWidth = 1.5;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.arc(App.interaction.hoverLocal.x, App.interaction.hoverLocal.y, Math.max(1, App.paint.brushSize * 0.5), 0, Math.PI * 2);
      ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    if (App.interaction.addBoneMode && App.interaction.dragging && App.interaction.dragType === 'createBone' && App.interaction.startLocal) {
      var a = App.interaction.startLocal;
      var b = App.interaction.currentLocal || a;
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#00ff95'; // FIX v6.7
      ctx.lineWidth = 7; // FIX v6.7
      ctx.lineCap = 'round'; // FIX v6.7
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(a.x, a.y); ctx.lineTo(b.x, b.y); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#00131f'; // FIX v6.7
      ctx.lineWidth = 2; // FIX v6.7
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(a.x, a.y); ctx.lineTo(b.x, b.y); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();
    }

    ctx.restore(); // FIX v7.0
    clearNavigationExclusionOnCanvas(ctx); // FIX v9.6: invisible cutout over the Wick navigation controls without drawing an ugly cover
    updateUI();
  }

  function hitTestBone(localPoint){
    var best = null;
    var pose = isRestBoneEditContext() ? getRestPose() : getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame); // FIX v16.6
    App.bones.forEach(function(b){
      var pb = getBonePoseLike(b, pose);
      var head = isRestBoneEditContext() ? b.head : pb.head; // FIX v16.6
      var tail = isRestBoneEditContext() ? b.tail : pb.tail; // FIX v16.6
      var dh = dist(localPoint, head);
      var dt = dist(localPoint, tail);
      if (dh <= 10) { // FIX v8.1: smaller visible handles use smaller hit radius
        best = { boneId: b.id, type: 'head', d: dh };
        return;
      }
      if (dt <= 10) { // FIX v8.1: smaller visible handles use smaller hit radius
        best = { boneId: b.id, type: 'tail', d: dt };
        return;
      }
      var geom = getEnvelopeGeometry(pb);
      [
        { p: geom.headPos, type: 'envHeadPos' },
        { p: geom.headNeg, type: 'envHeadNeg' },
        { p: geom.tailPos, type: 'envTailPos' },
        { p: geom.tailNeg, type: 'envTailNeg' }
      ].forEach(function(item){
        var dd = dist(localPoint, item.p);
        if (dd <= 10 && (!best || dd < best.d)) best = { boneId: b.id, type: item.type, d: dd }; // FIX v8.1
      });
      var seg = pointToSegmentDistance(localPoint, head, tail);
      if (seg.d <= 6) { // FIX v8.1
        if (!best || seg.d < best.d) best = { boneId: b.id, type: 'line', d: seg.d };
      }
    });
    return best;
  }

  function resolveSharedJointHit(hit){ // FIX v5.0
    if (!hit) return hit; // FIX v5.0
    if (hit.type === 'head') { // FIX v5.0
      var childBone = getBoneById(hit.boneId); // FIX v5.0
      if (childBone && childBone.parentId) { // FIX v5.0
        var parentBone = getBoneById(childBone.parentId); // FIX v5.0
        if (parentBone) { // FIX v5.0
          return { boneId: parentBone.id, type: 'tail', d: hit.d, redirectedFromChildId: childBone.id }; // FIX v5.0
        } // FIX v5.0
      } // FIX v5.0
    } // FIX v5.0
    return hit; // FIX v5.0
  }

  function onOverlayMouseDown(e){
    if (!App.source.image) return;
    var local = clientToOverlayLocal(e.clientX, e.clientY);
    App.interaction.hoverLocal = local;
    App.interaction.shift = !!e.shiftKey;
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.paint.enabled && getSelectedBone()) {
      App.interaction.dragging = true;
      App.interaction.dragType = 'paintWeight';
      App.interaction.lastPaintLocal = local;
      paintWeightStampAt(local);
      updateUI();
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.frameBonePinMode) { // FIX v13.2
      var attach = getSelectedBone();
      addFrameBoneAtPoint(local, attach ? attach.id : null);
      App.interaction.addBoneMode = true;
      return;
    }
    var rawHit = hitTestBone(local); // FIX v5.0
    if (rawHit && !editBoneModeAllowsDragType(rawHit.type)) rawHit = null; // FIX v16.6: Edit Bone mode does not edit envelope, Edit Envelope mode does not move bone position.
    var hit = rawHit; // FIX v5.0
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.interaction.addBoneMode) { // FIX v4.7
      if (rawHit) { // FIX v5.0
        App.selectedBoneId = rawHit.boneId; // FIX v5.0
        App.interaction.dragging = true;
        App.interaction.dragType = 'maybeCreateBoneFromExisting';
        App.interaction.boneId = rawHit.boneId; // FIX v5.0
        App.interaction.startLocal = local;
        App.interaction.currentLocal = local;
        updateUI();
        renderOverlay();
        return;
      }
      App.interaction.dragging = true;
      App.interaction.dragType = 'createBone';
      App.interaction.startLocal = local;
      App.interaction.currentLocal = local;
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    hit = resolveSharedJointHit(rawHit); // FIX v5.0: shared child heads are actually the parent tail joint
    if (hit && !isRestBoneEditContext() && !isAnimateKeyContext()) return; // FIX v16.6: clicking bones outside Bones, Edit Bone, or Animate must not create keys or edits.
    if (hit) {
      App.selectedBoneId = hit.boneId;
      App.interaction.dragging = true;
      App.interaction.dragType = hit.type;
      App.interaction.boneId = hit.boneId;
      App.interaction.startLocal = local;
      // FIX v11.3: capture BEFORE ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame bakes all bones in
      App.interaction.preExistingKeyFrame = !!App.keyframes[App.currentFrame];
      App.interaction.preKeyedBoneIds = App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]
        ? Object.keys(App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]).map(Number) : [];
      var makeKey = isAnimateKeyContext(); // FIX v16.6
      var restEdit = isRestBoneEditContext(); // FIX v16.6
      var fullPoseAtFrame = makeKey ? getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame) : null; // FIX v16.6
      App.interaction.startPose = makeKey ? ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame() : null; // FIX v16.6
      var bone = getSelectedBone();
      var curPose = makeKey ? ensureEditableBoneKeyAtCurrentFrame(hit.boneId, fullPoseAtFrame) : null; // FIX v16.6: only Animate creates a key.
      var startPB = restEdit ? bone : curPose;
      if (startPB && makeKey) ensurePoseEnvelopeValues(startPB, bone);
      App.interaction.startBone = {
        head: clone(restEdit ? bone.head : curPose.head),
        tail: clone(restEdit ? bone.tail : curPose.tail),
        angle: angleOfItem(restEdit ? bone : curPose), // FIX v16.6
        prevPointerAngle: rawAngleOfPoints(restEdit ? bone.head : curPose.head, local), // FIX v16.6
        cumulativeAngle: angleOfItem(restEdit ? bone : curPose), // FIX v16.6
        envStart: getBoneEnvStart(startPB || bone), // FIX v6.3
        envEnd: getBoneEnvEnd(startPB || bone), // FIX v6.3
        restLength: getLockedBoneLength(bone) // FIX v4.7
      };
      App.interaction.startDescendants = restEdit ? captureDescendantStateForBone(hit.boneId, null) : []; // FIX v16.6
      updateUI();
      renderOverlay();
    }
  }

  function applyShiftConstraint(start, current){
    var dx = current.x - start.x;
    var dy = current.y - start.y;
    if (Math.abs(dx) >= Math.abs(dy)) return { x: current.x, y: start.y };
    return { x: start.x, y: current.y };
  }

  function updateContinuousDragAngleForBone(currentPoint, headPoint){ // FIX v8.6
    if (!App.interaction.startBone) return 0;
    var pointerAngle = rawAngleOfPoints(headPoint, currentPoint);
    var previousPointerAngle = typeof App.interaction.startBone.prevPointerAngle === 'number' ? App.interaction.startBone.prevPointerAngle : pointerAngle;
    var delta = wrappedAngleDelta(previousPointerAngle, pointerAngle);
    App.interaction.startBone.cumulativeAngle = (typeof App.interaction.startBone.cumulativeAngle === 'number' ? App.interaction.startBone.cumulativeAngle : angleOfItem(App.interaction.startBone)) + delta;
    App.interaction.startBone.prevPointerAngle = pointerAngle;
    return App.interaction.startBone.cumulativeAngle;
  }

  function onOverlayMouseMove(e){
    if (!App.overlay.canvas || !App.source.image) return;
    var local = clientToOverlayLocal(e.clientX, e.clientY);
    App.interaction.hoverLocal = local;
    App.interaction.shift = !!e.shiftKey;
    if (!App.interaction.dragging) {
      var hit = hitTestBone(local);
      App.interaction.hoverBoneId = hit ? hit.boneId : null;
      App.interaction.hoverHandle = hit ? hit.type : '';
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    if (App.interaction.dragType === 'paintWeight') {
      paintWeightStroke(App.interaction.lastPaintLocal || local, local);
      App.interaction.lastPaintLocal = local;
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.interaction.dragType === 'maybeCreateBoneFromExisting') { // FIX v4.7
      App.interaction.currentLocal = App.interaction.shift ? applyShiftConstraint(App.interaction.startLocal, local) : local;
      if (movedFarEnough(App.interaction.startLocal, App.interaction.currentLocal)) {
        App.interaction.dragType = 'createBone';
      }
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.interaction.dragType === 'createBone') {
      App.interaction.currentLocal = App.interaction.shift ? applyShiftConstraint(App.interaction.startLocal, local) : local;
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }
    var bone = getSelectedBone();
    if (!bone) return;
    var start = App.interaction.startLocal;
    var cur = App.interaction.shift ? applyShiftConstraint(start, local) : local;
    var dx = cur.x - start.x;
    var dy = cur.y - start.y;
    var oldParentBone = App.interaction.startBone;

    if (App.interaction.dragType === 'envHeadPos' || App.interaction.dragType === 'envHeadNeg' || App.interaction.dragType === 'envTailPos' || App.interaction.dragType === 'envTailNeg') { // FIX v6.3
      var whichEnd = (App.interaction.dragType.indexOf('Head') !== -1) ? 'head' : 'tail';
      var envWidth = envelopeWidthFromLocalPoint(App.interaction.startBone, cur, whichEnd);
      if (isRestBoneEditContext()) { // FIX v16.6
        if (whichEnd === 'head') bone.envStart = envWidth;
        else bone.envEnd = envWidth;
        bone.radius = Math.max(getBoneEnvStart(bone), getBoneEnvEnd(bone));
      } else if (isAnimateKeyContext()) { // FIX v16.6
        var envPose = ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame(); // FIX v12.4
        if (!envPose[bone.id]) envPose[bone.id] = ensureEditableBoneKeyAtCurrentFrame(bone.id); // FIX v12.4
        ensurePoseEnvelopeValues(envPose[bone.id], bone);
        if (whichEnd === 'head') envPose[bone.id].envStart = envWidth;
        else envPose[bone.id].envEnd = envWidth;
      } else return; // FIX v16.6
      updateUI();
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }

    if ((App.rig.mode === 'chainIk' || App.rig.mode === 'splineIk') && App.interaction.dragType === 'tail' && !boneHasChildren(bone.id)) { // FIX v4.8: only end bones should run IK as end effectors
      if (isRestBoneEditContext()) { // FIX v16.6
        solveIKOnRest(bone.id, cur);
      } else if (isAnimateKeyContext()) { // FIX v16.6
        var ikPose = getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame); // FIX v12.4
        solveIKOnPose(ikPose, bone.id, cur);
        ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame()[bone.id] = clone(ikPose[bone.id]); // FIX v12.4: only commit the moved end bone key
      } else return; // FIX v16.6
      renderOverlay();
      return;
    }

    if (isRestBoneEditContext()) { // FIX v16.6
      if (App.interaction.dragType === 'head') {
        bone.head.x = App.interaction.startBone.head.x + dx; // FIX v4.7: head drag translates the whole bone
        bone.head.y = App.interaction.startBone.head.y + dy; // FIX v4.7
        bone.tail.x = App.interaction.startBone.tail.x + dx; // FIX v4.7
        bone.tail.y = App.interaction.startBone.tail.y + dy; // FIX v4.7
        bone.angle = App.interaction.startBone.angle; // FIX v8.6
      } else if (App.interaction.dragType === 'tail') {
        var restAngle = updateContinuousDragAngleForBone(cur, App.interaction.startBone.head); // FIX v8.6
        if (isStretchyBone(bone)) { // FIX v17.0
          bone.tail = clone(cur);
          bone.angle = Math.atan2(bone.tail.y - bone.head.y, bone.tail.x - bone.head.x);
          bone.restLength = boneLengthFromPoseItem(bone);
        } else {
          bone.tail = tailFromAngle(bone.head, restAngle, getLockedBoneLength(bone)); // FIX v8.6
          bone.angle = restAngle; // FIX v8.6
        }
      } else {
        bone.head.x = App.interaction.startBone.head.x + dx;
        bone.head.y = App.interaction.startBone.head.y + dy;
        bone.tail.x = App.interaction.startBone.tail.x + dx;
        bone.tail.y = App.interaction.startBone.tail.y + dy;
        bone.angle = App.interaction.startBone.angle; // FIX v8.6
      }
      setItemTailToLockedLength(bone, bone); // FIX v4.7
      var newParentBone = { head: clone(bone.head), tail: clone(bone.tail) };
      applyDescendantTransformToRest(App.interaction.startDescendants || [], oldParentBone, newParentBone);
      enforceAllRestChains();
    } else if (isAnimateKeyContext()) { // FIX v16.6
      var pose = ensureEditablePoseAtCurrentFrame(); // FIX v12.4 sparse
      var pb = ensureEditableBoneKeyAtCurrentFrame(bone.id); // FIX v12.4 only the moved bone is keyed
      if (!pb) return;
      if (App.interaction.dragType === 'head') {
        pb.head.x = App.interaction.startBone.head.x + dx; // FIX v4.7: head drag translates the whole pose bone
        pb.head.y = App.interaction.startBone.head.y + dy; // FIX v4.7
        pb.tail.x = App.interaction.startBone.tail.x + dx; // FIX v4.7
        pb.tail.y = App.interaction.startBone.tail.y + dy; // FIX v4.7
        pb.angle = App.interaction.startBone.angle; // FIX v8.6
      } else if (App.interaction.dragType === 'tail') {
        var poseAngle = updateContinuousDragAngleForBone(cur, App.interaction.startBone.head); // FIX v8.6
        if (isStretchyBone(bone)) { // FIX v17.0
          pb.tail = clone(cur);
          pb.angle = Math.atan2(pb.tail.y - pb.head.y, pb.tail.x - pb.head.x);
        } else {
          pb.tail = tailFromAngle(pb.head, poseAngle, getLockedBoneLength(bone)); // FIX v8.6
          pb.angle = poseAngle; // FIX v8.6
        }
      } else {
        pb.head.x = App.interaction.startBone.head.x + dx;
        pb.head.y = App.interaction.startBone.head.y + dy;
        pb.tail.x = App.interaction.startBone.tail.x + dx;
        pb.tail.y = App.interaction.startBone.tail.y + dy;
        pb.angle = App.interaction.startBone.angle; // FIX v8.6
      }
      setItemTailToLockedLength(pb, bone); // FIX v12.4
      copyEnvAndAngleFallback(pb, bone); // FIX v12.4
      writeLocalAngleForBoneItem(bone, pb, getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame)); // FIX v13.0: store child key angle relative to parent
    } else { return; } // FIX v16.6
    renderOverlay();
  }

  function onOverlayMouseUp(e){
    if (!App.interaction.dragging) return;
    if (App.activeTab === 'bones' && App.interaction.dragType === 'createBone') {
      var a = App.interaction.startLocal;
      var b = App.interaction.currentLocal || a;
      if (movedFarEnough(a, b)) addBone(a, b); // FIX v4.7
    }
    if (App.interaction.dragType === 'maybeCreateBoneFromExisting') {
      // FIX v4.7: selecting an existing bone in add mode does not create a new bone unless the user drags away.
    }
    // FIX v12.4: after animated drag, keep only existing keys plus the one bone the user actually moved.
    if (isAnimateKeyContext() && App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]) { // FIX v16.6
      var movedBoneId = App.interaction.boneId;
      var preKeyed = App.interaction.preKeyedBoneIds || [];
      var wasPreExisting = App.interaction.preExistingKeyFrame;
      Object.keys(App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]).forEach(function(idStr){
        var id = Number(idStr);
        var wasKeyed = preKeyed.indexOf(id) !== -1;
        var wasMoved = (id === movedBoneId);
        if (!wasKeyed && !wasMoved) delete App.keyframes[App.currentFrame][id];
      });
      if (!wasPreExisting && Object.keys(App.keyframes[App.currentFrame]).length === 0) delete App.keyframes[App.currentFrame];
    }
    App.interaction.dragging = false;
    App.interaction.dragType = '';
    App.interaction.boneId = null;
    App.interaction.startLocal = null;
    App.interaction.startPose = null;
    App.interaction.startBone = null;
    App.interaction.startDescendants = [];
    App.interaction.lastPaintLocal = null;
    App.interaction.preKeyedBoneIds = [];
    App.interaction.preExistingKeyFrame = false;
    renderOverlay();
    scheduleProxyFrame(); // FIX v11.3: refresh proxy after key strip
  }

  function onParentKeyDown(e){
    App.interaction.shift = !!e.shiftKey;
  }

  function onParentKeyUp(e){
    App.interaction.shift = !!e.shiftKey;
  }

  function proxyG(){ // FIX v10.2
    try { return (window.parent && window.parent.Wick && window.parent.Wick.GUIElement) ? window.parent.Wick.GUIElement : {}; } catch(e){ return {}; }
  }

  function proxyCellWidth(){ var g = proxyG(); return Number(g.GRID_DEFAULT_CELL_WIDTH || g.GRID_NORMAL_CELL_WIDTH || 38); } // FIX v10.2
  function proxyCellHeight(){ var g = proxyG(); return Number(g.GRID_DEFAULT_CELL_HEIGHT || g.GRID_NORMAL_CELL_HEIGHT || 42); } // FIX v10.2
  function proxyLayerColumnWidth(){ var g = proxyG(); return Number(g.LAYERS_CONTAINER_WIDTH || 160); } // FIX v10.2
  function proxyBreadcrumbHeight(){ var g = proxyG(); return Number(g.BREADCRUMBS_HEIGHT || 30); } // FIX v10.2
  function proxyNumberLineHeight(){ var g = proxyG(); return Number(g.NUMBER_LINE_HEIGHT || 35); } // FIX v10.2
  function proxyScrollbarSize(){ var g = proxyG(); return Number(g.SCROLLBAR_SIZE || 18); } // FIX v10.2

  function proxyMedianNumber(values){ // FIX v15.2
    values = (values || []).filter(function(v){ return isFinite(v) && v > 0; }).sort(function(a,b){ return a - b; });
    if (!values.length) return 0;
    var mid = Math.floor(values.length / 2);
    return values.length % 2 ? values[mid] : (values[mid - 1] + values[mid]) / 2;
  }

  function proxyMeasuredCellWidthFromWickCanvas(wickCanvas, LCW, BCH, NLH){ // FIX v15.2
    /* FIX v15.2: The proxy keys must use the same frame pitch Wick actually drew.
       Do not rely only on a stored constant, because tiny differences accumulate and the
       BoneWarp key rows drift away from the Wick frame grid by later frames. This reads
       the real timeline canvas and measures the spacing between vertical frame grid lines.
       If reading pixels is blocked or the scan is uncertain, it falls back to Wick's constant. */
    var fallback = Number(proxyCellWidth() || 38);
    try {
      if (!wickCanvas || !wickCanvas.getContext) return fallback;
      var ctx = wickCanvas.getContext('2d', { willReadFrequently:true });
      if (!ctx || !ctx.getImageData) return fallback;
      var w = Math.max(1, Math.floor(wickCanvas.width || 0));
      var h = Math.max(1, Math.floor(wickCanvas.height || 0));
      if (w < 120 || h < 80) return fallback;
      var xStart = clamp(Math.floor(LCW - fallback * 2), 0, w - 2);
      var xEnd = clamp(Math.floor(w - proxyScrollbarSize() - 4), xStart + 20, w - 2);
      var yStart = clamp(Math.floor(BCH + NLH + 6), 0, h - 2);
      var yEnd = clamp(Math.floor(yStart + Math.min(160, Math.max(24, h - yStart - 8))), yStart + 1, h - 1);
      var sampleH = Math.max(1, yEnd - yStart);
      var sampleW = Math.max(1, xEnd - xStart + 1);
      var data = ctx.getImageData(xStart, yStart, sampleW, sampleH).data;
      function lumaAt(localX, localY){
        var p = (localY * sampleW + localX) * 4;
        return data[p] * 0.299 + data[p + 1] * 0.587 + data[p + 2] * 0.114;
      }
      var scores = [];
      for (var x = 1; x < sampleW - 1; x++) {
        var score = 0;
        for (var y = 0; y < sampleH; y += 4) {
          var a = lumaAt(x - 1, y);
          var b = lumaAt(x, y);
          var c = lumaAt(x + 1, y);
          score += Math.abs(b - a) + Math.abs(c - b);
        }
        scores.push({ x:xStart + x, score:score });
      }
      if (!scores.length) return fallback;
      var scoreValues = scores.map(function(s){ return s.score; }).sort(function(a,b){ return a - b; });
      var medianScore = scoreValues[Math.floor(scoreValues.length * 0.70)] || 0;
      var threshold = Math.max(18, medianScore * 2.2);
      var peaks = [];
      scores.forEach(function(s){
        if (s.score < threshold) return;
        var last = peaks.length ? peaks[peaks.length - 1] : null;
        if (!last || s.x - last.x > 8) peaks.push({ x:s.x, score:s.score });
        else if (s.score > last.score) { last.x = s.x; last.score = s.score; }
      });
      if (peaks.length < 3) return fallback;
      var spacings = [];
      for (var i = 1; i < peaks.length; i++) {
        var d = peaks[i].x - peaks[i - 1].x;
        if (d >= Math.max(18, fallback * 0.55) && d <= Math.min(90, fallback * 1.75)) spacings.push(d);
      }
      var measured = proxyMedianNumber(spacings);
      if (!measured || measured < 18 || measured > 90) return fallback;
      return measured;
    } catch(e) {
      return fallback;
    }
  }

  function proxyFrameAreaX(scrollX){ // FIX v15.4
    /* FIX v15.4: Use Wick's documented timeline reference directly.
       The frames area starts exactly after the layer label column. The previous +8 correction
       caused cumulative visible drift against Wick's own frame grid at later frames. */
    return proxyLayerColumnWidth() - Number(scrollX || 0);
  }

  function proxyTimelineCanvas(){ // FIX v10.2
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc) return null;
    var viewH = window.parent && window.parent.innerHeight ? window.parent.innerHeight : window.innerHeight;
    var best = null, bestScore = -1;
    Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('canvas')).forEach(function(c){
      if (!c || c.id === 'ltbw-proxy-keyframe-canvas') return;
      var r = c.getBoundingClientRect();
      var score = (r.top > viewH * 0.35 ? 4 : 0) + (r.width > 300 ? 3 : 0) + (r.height > 0 && r.height < r.width * 0.35 ? 3 : 0);
      if (score > bestScore) { bestScore = score; best = c; }
    });
    return best;
  }

  function proxyScrollContainer(){ // FIX v11.2
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc) return null;
    var viewH = window.parent && window.parent.innerHeight ? window.parent.innerHeight : window.innerHeight;
    var wickCanvas = proxyTimelineCanvas();
    var canvasRect = null;
    try { if (wickCanvas) canvasRect = wickCanvas.getBoundingClientRect(); } catch(e){}
    var best = null, bestScore = -1;
    Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('div')).forEach(function(d){
      try {
        var r = d.getBoundingClientRect();
        if (r.top < viewH * 0.3) return;
        if (d.scrollHeight <= d.clientHeight + 2 && d.scrollWidth <= d.clientWidth + 2) return;
        var score = 0;
        if (r.width > 700) score += 5;
        if (canvasRect && r.top <= canvasRect.bottom + 40 && r.bottom >= canvasRect.top - 40) score += 8;
        if (d.scrollTop > 0 || d.scrollLeft > 0) score += 10;
        score += Math.min(10, (d.scrollHeight - d.clientHeight) / 40);
        if (score > bestScore) { bestScore = score; best = d; }
      } catch(ignore){}
    });
    return best;
  }

  function proxyAttachFollowListeners(){ // FIX v10.9
    var pwin = window.parent || window;
    var pdoc = pwin.document || document;
    proxyRemoveFollowListeners(); // FIX v10.9
    App.proxy.eventTargets = []; // FIX v10.9
    function add(target, type, fn, opts){ // FIX v10.9
      try {
        if (!target || !target.addEventListener) return;
        target.addEventListener(type, fn, opts || { passive:true, capture:true });
        App.proxy.eventTargets.push({ target:target, type:type, fn:fn, opts:opts || { passive:true, capture:true } });
      } catch(e){}
    }
    var follow = function(){ // FIX v10.9
      try { App.proxy.scrollContainer = proxyScrollContainer() || App.proxy.scrollContainer; } catch(e){}
      scheduleProxyFrame();
    };
    add(pdoc, 'wheel', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
    add(pdoc, 'mousemove', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
    add(pdoc, 'pointermove', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
    add(pdoc, 'mousedown', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
    add(pdoc, 'mouseup', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
    add(pwin, 'resize', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
    try {
      Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('div')).forEach(function(d){
        if (d.scrollHeight > d.clientHeight + 2 || d.scrollWidth > d.clientWidth + 2) add(d, 'scroll', follow, { passive:true, capture:true }); // FIX v10.9
      });
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function proxyRemoveFollowListeners(){ // FIX v10.9
    try {
      (App.proxy.eventTargets || []).forEach(function(item){
        try { item.target.removeEventListener(item.type, item.fn, item.opts); } catch(e){}
      });
    } catch(e){}
    App.proxy.eventTargets = []; // FIX v10.9
  }

  function proxyDomRowYForLayerInfo(info){ // FIX v10.9
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    var container = App.proxy && App.proxy.container ? App.proxy.container : null;
    if (!pdoc || !container || !info) return null;
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    var containerRect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
    var LCW = proxyLayerColumnWidth();
    var CH = proxyCellHeight();
    var wantedName = String(info.name || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
    var wantedIdx = -1;
    try { wantedIdx = tl && tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(info.wickLayer) : -1; } catch(e){}

    function rowRectForNode(node){ // FIX v10.9
      var current = node;
      var best = node.getBoundingClientRect();
      for (var i = 0; current && i < 6; i++, current = current.parentElement) {
        var r = current.getBoundingClientRect();
        if (r.height >= 22 && r.height <= Math.max(80, CH + 24) && r.width >= 60 && r.width <= LCW + 120 && r.left < containerRect.left + LCW + 80) {
          best = r;
        }
      }
      return best;
    }

    var exactMatches = [];
    var proxyRows = [];
    try {
      Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('div,span')).forEach(function(node){
        var txt = String(node.textContent || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
        if (!txt) return;
        if (txt.indexOf('BW Key') === -1 && txt.indexOf('F_Bone') === -1 && (!wantedName || txt.indexOf(wantedName) === -1)) return; // FIX v16.1
        var r = rowRectForNode(node);
        if (r.height < 12) return;
        if (r.top < containerRect.top - 120 || r.top > containerRect.bottom + 120) return;
        if (r.left > containerRect.left + LCW + 90) return;
        var row = { rect:r, text:txt, y:r.top - containerRect.top + 3 };
        if (txt.indexOf('BW Key') !== -1 || txt.indexOf('F_Bone') !== -1 || (wantedName && (txt === wantedName || txt.indexOf(wantedName) !== -1))) proxyRows.push(row); // FIX v16.1
        if (wantedName && (txt === wantedName || txt.indexOf(wantedName) !== -1 || wantedName.indexOf(txt) !== -1)) exactMatches.push(row);
      });
    } catch(e){}

    exactMatches.sort(function(a,b){ return a.rect.top - b.rect.top; });
    proxyRows.sort(function(a,b){ return a.rect.top - b.rect.top; });

    /* Prefer the exact row label. When there are duplicate clipped labels, use the layer order among BoneWarp proxy layers. */
    if (exactMatches.length === 1) return exactMatches[0].y;
    if (exactMatches.length > 1) {
      var sameNameIndex = 0;
      try {
        var seen = 0;
        (App.proxy.layers || []).forEach(function(layerInfo){
          if (layerInfo === info) sameNameIndex = seen;
          if (String(layerInfo.name || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim() === wantedName) seen++;
        });
      } catch(e){}
      if (exactMatches[sameNameIndex]) return exactMatches[sameNameIndex].y;
