      return exactMatches[0].y;
    }

    /* Fallback: map by visual order of proxy layers currently visible in the Wick layer list. */
    if (proxyRows.length) {
      var proxyOrder = [];
      try {
        (App.proxy.layers || []).slice().sort(function(a,b){
          var ai = tl && tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(a.wickLayer) : 0;
          var bi = tl && tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(b.wickLayer) : 0;
          return ai - bi;
        }).forEach(function(layerInfo){ proxyOrder.push(layerInfo); });
      } catch(e){}
      var orderIndex = proxyOrder.indexOf(info);
      if (orderIndex >= 0 && proxyRows[orderIndex]) return proxyRows[orderIndex].y;
    }

    return null;
  }

  function proxyScrollX(){ // FIX v11.3
    function clean(v){
      v = Number(v || 0);
      return (isFinite(v) && v >= 0) ? v : 0;
    }
    try {
      var tl = proxyTimeline();
      if (tl && tl.guiElement && tl.guiElement.project) return clean(tl.guiElement.project.scrollX); // FIX v11.3
    } catch(e){}
    try {
      var tl2 = getSelectedTimeline();
      if (tl2 && tl2.guiElement && tl2.guiElement.project) return clean(tl2.guiElement.project.scrollX); // FIX v11.3
    } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.proxy && App.proxy.scrollContainer) return clean(App.proxy.scrollContainer.scrollLeft); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.project) return clean(App.ed.project.scrollX); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project) return clean(App.project.scrollX); } catch(e){}
    return 0;
  }

  function proxyScrollY(){ // FIX v11.3
    /* FIX v11.3: Read the scroll value from the actual Wick GUIElement.Project used to draw the timeline.
       The model project and DOM scrollbars can stay at zero, while Wick's timeline canvas moves from
       selectedTimeline.guiElement.project.scrollY. */
    function clean(v){
      v = Number(v || 0);
      return (isFinite(v) && v >= 0) ? v : 0;
    }
    try {
      var tl = proxyTimeline();
      if (tl && tl.guiElement && tl.guiElement.project) return clean(tl.guiElement.project.scrollY); // FIX v11.3
    } catch(e){}
    try {
      var tl2 = getSelectedTimeline();
      if (tl2 && tl2.guiElement && tl2.guiElement.project) return clean(tl2.guiElement.project.scrollY); // FIX v11.3
    } catch(e){}
    try {
      var ed = App.bridge && App.bridge.getEditor ? App.bridge.getEditor() : null;
      if (!ed && window.parent && window.parent.LukeToolsBridge && window.parent.LukeToolsBridge.getEditor) ed = window.parent.LukeToolsBridge.getEditor();
      var activeTl = ed && ed.project && ed.project.activeTimeline ? ed.project.activeTimeline : null;
      if (activeTl && activeTl.guiElement && activeTl.guiElement.project) return clean(activeTl.guiElement.project.scrollY); // FIX v11.3
    } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.proxy && App.proxy.scrollContainer) return clean(App.proxy.scrollContainer.scrollTop); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.ed && App.ed.project) return clean(App.ed.project.scrollY); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project) return clean(App.project.scrollY); } catch(e){}
    return 0;
  }

  function proxyTimeline(){ // FIX v10.2
    return getSelectedTimeline();
  }

  function createProxyWickLayer(){ // FIX v10.2
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!tl || !App.Wick || !App.Wick.Layer) return null;
    if (App.proxy.wickLayer && tl.layers && tl.layers.indexOf(App.proxy.wickLayer) !== -1) return App.proxy.wickLayer;
    var layer = null;
    try { layer = new App.Wick.Layer({ name: App.proxy.name, identifier: makeValidIdentifier(App.proxy.name, 'BoneWarp_Proxy_Keys') }); } catch(e) { try { layer = new window.parent.Wick.Layer({ name: App.proxy.name, identifier: makeValidIdentifier(App.proxy.name, 'BoneWarp_Proxy_Keys') }); } catch(e2){} } // FIX v12.7
    if (!layer) return null;
    try { layer.name = App.proxy.name; } catch(e){}
    try { layer.identifier = makeValidIdentifier(App.proxy.name, 'BoneWarp_Proxy_Keys'); } catch(e){} // FIX v12.7
    try { layer.locked = true; } catch(e){}
    try {
      if (typeof tl.addLayer === 'function') tl.addLayer(layer);
      else if (tl.layers && typeof tl.layers.push === 'function') tl.layers.push(layer);
      else return null;
    } catch(addErr) { return null; }
    App.proxy.wickLayer = layer;
    markDirty();
    return layer;
  }

  function removeProxyWickLayer(){ // FIX v10.2
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    var wl = App.proxy.wickLayer;
    if (tl && wl) {
      try { if (typeof tl.removeLayer === 'function') tl.removeLayer(wl); }
      catch(e){}
      try { if (tl.layers) { var i = tl.layers.indexOf(wl); if (i !== -1) tl.layers.splice(i, 1); } } catch(e){}
      markDirty();
    }
    App.proxy.wickLayer = null;
  }

  function removeProxyOverlay(keepLayer){ // FIX v10.2
    try { if (App.proxy.rafId) window.parent.cancelAnimationFrame(App.proxy.rafId); } catch(e){}
    App.proxy.rafId = null;
    if (!keepLayer) removeProxyWickLayer();
    try { if (App.proxy.scrollContainer) App.proxy.scrollContainer.removeEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, true); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.proxy.container) App.proxy.container.removeEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, true); } catch(e){}
    proxyRemoveFollowListeners(); // FIX v10.9
    (App.proxy.hitDivs || []).forEach(function(d){ try { if (d && d.parentNode) d.parentNode.removeChild(d); } catch(e){} });
    (App.proxy.blockDivs || []).forEach(function(d){ try { if (d && d.parentNode) d.parentNode.removeChild(d); } catch(e){} });
    try { if (App.proxy.overlayCanvas && App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode) App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode.removeChild(App.proxy.overlayCanvas); } catch(e){}
    App.proxy.overlayCanvas = null;
    App.proxy.hitDivs = [];
    App.proxy.blockDivs = [];
    App.proxy.container = null;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = null;
    App.proxy.framePending = false;
    App.proxy.active = false;
    updateUI();
  }

  function scheduleProxyFrame(){ // FIX v10.2
    if (!App.proxy.active || !App.proxy.overlayCanvas) return;
    if (App.proxy.framePending) return;
    App.proxy.framePending = true;
    try { App.proxy.rafId = window.parent.requestAnimationFrame(renderProxyFrame); }
    catch(e) { App.proxy.rafId = requestAnimationFrame(renderProxyFrame); }
  }

  function startProxyLoop(){ // FIX v10.2
    if (App.proxy.rafId) return;
    function loop(){
      if (!App.proxy.active || !App.proxy.overlayCanvas) { App.proxy.rafId = null; return; }
      renderProxyFrame();
      try { App.proxy.rafId = window.parent.requestAnimationFrame(loop); }
      catch(e) { App.proxy.rafId = requestAnimationFrame(loop); }
    }
    loop();
  }

  function setupProxyLayer(){ // FIX v10.2
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc) { log('Proxy setup failed: parent document not available.'); return; }
    var wickCanvas = proxyTimelineCanvas();
    if (!wickCanvas) { log('Proxy setup failed: Wick timeline canvas not found.'); return; }
    var container = wickCanvas.parentElement;
    if (!container) { log('Proxy setup failed: Wick timeline canvas has no parent.'); return; }
    if (window.parent.getComputedStyle(container).position === 'static') container.style.position = 'relative';
    createProxyWickLayer();
    if (!App.proxy.wickLayer) { log('Proxy setup failed: could not create Wick proxy layer.'); return; }
    if (App.proxy.overlayCanvas && App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode) App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode.removeChild(App.proxy.overlayCanvas);
    var canvas = pdoc.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.id = 'ltbw-proxy-keyframe-canvas';
    canvas.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'proxy-keyframe-canvas');
    canvas.width = wickCanvas.width;
    canvas.height = wickCanvas.height;
    canvas.style.cssText = [
      'position:absolute','left:0','top:0',
      'width:' + wickCanvas.offsetWidth + 'px','height:' + wickCanvas.offsetHeight + 'px',
      'pointer-events:none','z-index:5000'
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(canvas);
    App.proxy.overlayCanvas = canvas;
    App.proxy.container = container;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = proxyScrollContainer();
    try { if (App.proxy.scrollContainer) App.proxy.scrollContainer.addEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, { passive:true, capture:true }); } catch(e){}
    try { container.addEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, { passive:true, capture:true }); } catch(e){}
    proxyAttachFollowListeners(); // FIX v10.9
    App.proxy.active = true;
    startProxyLoop();
    renderProxyFrame();
    updateUI();
    log('Proxy keyframe layer created. It is locked and only shows BoneWarp keyframe markers.');
  }

  function proxyLayerFrameSpan(){ // FIX v10.2
    var maxEnd = Math.max(1, App.frameCount || 1);
    try {
      var tl = proxyTimeline();
      if (tl && tl.layers) {
        tl.layers.forEach(function(layer){
          if (layer === App.proxy.wickLayer) return;
          (layer.frames || []).forEach(function(frame){ maxEnd = Math.max(maxEnd, getFrameEnd(frame)); });
        });
      }
    } catch(e){}
    return maxEnd;
  }

  function proxyCurrentPlayhead(){ // FIX v10.2
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    var frame = App.currentFrame || 1;
    try { if (tl && tl.playheadPosition) frame = Number(tl.playheadPosition); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project && App.project.currentFrameNumber) frame = Number(App.project.currentFrameNumber); } catch(e){}
    return clamp(Math.round(frame || 1), 1, Math.max(1, App.frameCount || 1));
  }


  function proxyLiveRowYForLayerInfo(info, tl, container, wickCanvas, CH, BCH, NLH, scrollY){ // FIX v11.3
    /* FIX v11.3: Do not use DOM label positions. The proxy layer is a real Wick layer, so use
       the exact Wick canvas row formula with the real GUI scrollY. This makes the diamond overlay
       move vertically with its matching proxy bone layer. */
    var layerIdx = -1;
    try { layerIdx = tl && tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(info.wickLayer) : -1; } catch(e){}
    if (layerIdx < 0) return null;
    return BCH + NLH + layerIdx * CH - Number(scrollY || 0) + 3;
  }

  function proxyFrameKeysForLayerInfo(info){ // FIX v11.3
    var bone = info && getBoneById ? getBoneById(info.boneId) : null;
    if (!bone) return [];
    return proxyKeyFramesForBone(bone);
  }

  function renderProxyFrame(){ // FIX v11.2
    App.proxy.framePending = false;
    var canvas = App.proxy.overlayCanvas;
    if (!canvas) return;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = proxyScrollContainer() || App.proxy.scrollContainer;
    var wickCanvas = proxyTimelineCanvas();
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!wickCanvas || !tl) return;
    if (canvas.width !== wickCanvas.width) canvas.width = wickCanvas.width;
    if (canvas.height !== wickCanvas.height) canvas.height = wickCanvas.height;
    canvas.style.width = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetWidth) + 'px'; // FIX v15.2: do not compress the overlay canvas width or frame positions drift horizontally.
    canvas.style.height = wickCanvas.offsetHeight + 'px';
    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    var cssW = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetWidth || canvas.width || 1); // FIX v15.4
    var cssH = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetHeight || canvas.height || 1); // FIX v15.4
    var scaleX = Math.max(0.01, (canvas.width || cssW) / cssW); // FIX v15.4: Wick draws the timeline in internal canvas pixels, not always CSS pixels.
    var scaleY = Math.max(0.01, (canvas.height || cssH) / cssH); // FIX v15.4
    var CH = proxyCellHeight() * scaleY; // FIX v15.4
    var LCW = proxyLayerColumnWidth() * scaleX; // FIX v15.4
    var BCH = proxyBreadcrumbHeight() * scaleY; // FIX v15.4
    var NLH = proxyNumberLineHeight() * scaleY; // FIX v15.4
    var baseCW = proxyCellWidth() * scaleX; // FIX v15.6: keep Wick cell width before manual correction.
    var proxyFirstCellShift = baseCW * 0.03; // FIX v16.0: move the proxy timeline to the right by 3 percent of one Wick cell.
    var CW = baseCW; // FIX v15.8: removed the 4.1 percent shrink. Use the Wick cell width unchanged.
    var scrollX = proxyScrollX() * scaleX; // FIX v15.8: removed the 4.1 percent shrink from scroll correction.
    var scrollY = proxyScrollY() * scaleY; // FIX v15.4
    var rowLeft = LCW;
    var rowRight = canvas.width - proxyScrollbarSize() * scaleX; // FIX v15.4
    var frameAreaX = LCW + proxyFirstCellShift - Number(scrollX || 0); // FIX v15.6: corrected first cell position moves right, then uses corrected timeline pitch.
    var span = proxyLayerFrameSpan();
    var ph = proxyCurrentPlayhead();
    var allHits = [];
    var clipTop = BCH + NLH; // FIX v11.3: clip all proxy drawing to below breadcrumb + number line
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.rect(rowLeft, clipTop, Math.max(1, canvas.width - rowLeft), Math.max(1, canvas.height - clipTop)); // FIX v16.1: clip proxy drawing at the layer-name edge.
    ctx.clip();

    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    (App.proxy.layers || []).forEach(function(info){
      if (!info || !info.wickLayer) return;
      var layerIdx = tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(info.wickLayer) : -1;
      if (layerIdx < 0) return;
      var rowY = proxyLiveRowYForLayerInfo(info, tl, App.proxy.container, wickCanvas, CH, BCH, NLH, scrollY);
      if (rowY == null) return;
      var rowH = CH - 3;
      if (rowY + rowH < BCH + NLH || rowY > canvas.height) return;
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,28,36,0.72)';
      ctx.fillRect(rowLeft, rowY, Math.max(1, rowRight - rowLeft), rowH);
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(30,226,154,0.16)';
      ctx.fillRect(frameAreaX, rowY, span * CW - 1, rowH); // FIX v15.4: Wick drawn frame width uses length * cell width minus 1.
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.25)';
      ctx.lineWidth = 1;
      for (var f = 1; f <= span; f++) {
        var gx = frameAreaX + (f - 1) * CW; // FIX v15.4: frame grid line position from Wick reference.
        if (gx < rowLeft || gx > rowRight) continue;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(gx, rowY); ctx.lineTo(gx, rowY + rowH); ctx.stroke();
      }
      var keys = proxyFrameKeysForLayerInfo(info);
      var DR = 7;
      var cy = rowY + CH / 2;
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length - 1; i++) {
        var x1 = frameAreaX + (keys[i] - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
        var x2 = frameAreaX + (keys[i + 1] - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
        if (x2 < rowLeft - 20 || x1 > rowRight + 20) continue;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x1 + DR + 2, cy); ctx.lineTo(x2 - DR - 2, cy);
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#8E8E8E'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
        var tip = x2 - DR - 2;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(tip - 7, cy - 4); ctx.lineTo(tip, cy); ctx.lineTo(tip - 7, cy + 4);
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#8E8E8E'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.lineJoin = 'round'; ctx.lineCap = 'round'; ctx.stroke();
      }
      keys.forEach(function(k){
        var cx = frameAreaX + (k - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
        if (cx < rowLeft || cx > rowRight + 20) return; // FIX v16.1
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(cx, cy - DR); ctx.lineTo(cx + DR, cy); ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + DR); ctx.lineTo(cx - DR, cy); ctx.closePath();
        ctx.fillStyle = '#1EE29A'; ctx.fill();
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#102a32'; ctx.lineWidth = 3; ctx.stroke();
        allHits.push({ frame:k, boneId:info.boneId, x:cx, y:cy, cssX:cx / scaleX, cssY:cy / scaleY }); // FIX v15.4
      });
      var px = frameAreaX + (ph - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px, rowY); ctx.lineTo(px, rowY + rowH); ctx.strokeStyle = '#FF5C5C'; ctx.lineWidth = 3; ctx.stroke();
    });
    ctx.restore(); // FIX v11.3: end clip region
    updateProxyHits(allHits, rowLeft / scaleX, rowRight / scaleX); // FIX v15.4: hit divs use CSS pixel positions.
  }


  function updateProxyHits(hitItems, rowLeft, rowRight){ // FIX v11.2
    if (!App.proxy.container) return;
    hitItems = hitItems || [];
    var needed = hitItems.length;
    while (App.proxy.hitDivs.length < needed) {
      var hd = window.parent.document.createElement('div');
      hd.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'proxy-keyframe-hit');
      hd.style.cssText = ['position:absolute','z-index:5002','pointer-events:auto','cursor:pointer','background:transparent','width:20px','height:20px'].join(';');
      hd.addEventListener('mousedown', function(evt){
        evt.preventDefault(); evt.stopPropagation();
        var frame = Number(this.getAttribute('data-frame') || 1);
        var boneId = Number(this.getAttribute('data-bone-id') || 0);
        var frameBoneId = Number(this.getAttribute('data-frame-bone-id') || 0); // FIX v13.7
        var hitType = this.getAttribute('data-hit-type') || 'bone'; // FIX v13.7
        if (hitType === 'frameBone' && frameBoneId) {
          App.selectedFrameBoneId = frameBoneId;
        } else if (boneId) {
          App.selectedBoneId = boneId;
        }
        setCurrentFrame(frame, false);
        setActiveTab('animate');
        renderOverlay();
        scheduleProxyFrame();
      });
      App.proxy.container.appendChild(hd);
      App.proxy.hitDivs.push(hd);
    }
    for (var i = needed; i < App.proxy.hitDivs.length; i++) App.proxy.hitDivs[i].style.display = 'none';
    hitItems.forEach(function(item, i){
      var hd = App.proxy.hitDivs[i];
      if (!hd) return;
      var checkX = Number(item.cssX != null ? item.cssX : item.x); // FIX v15.4
      if (checkX < rowLeft || checkX > rowRight + 20) { hd.style.display = 'none'; return; } // FIX v16.1
      hd.style.display = 'block';
      var hx = Number(item.cssX != null ? item.cssX : item.x); // FIX v15.4
      var hy = Number(item.cssY != null ? item.cssY : item.y); // FIX v15.4
      hd.style.left = (hx - 10) + 'px'; // FIX v15.4
      hd.style.top = (hy - 10) + 'px'; // FIX v15.4
      hd.setAttribute('data-frame', String(item.frame));
      hd.setAttribute('data-bone-id', String(item.boneId || 0));
    });
  }




  // FIX v10.9: Create the proxy layer at bone creation time, not later from a separate button.
  function ensureProxyLayerForCreatedBone(bone){
    try {
      if (!bone) return;
      proxyEnsureLayerStore();
      proxyCreateWickLayerForBone(bone); // FIX v12.5: create the row for the newly created bone
      syncProxyLayersToBones(true); // FIX v16.1: also backfill any missing proxy rows for existing bones
      ensureProxyOverlayCanvasForTimeline();
      renderProxyFrame();
      updateUI();
    } catch(e) {
      try { log('Proxy layer create warning: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e)); } catch(ignore){}
    }
  }

  function proxyRefreshWickTimelineUI(){ // FIX v10.9
    try {
      var ed = App.bridge && App.bridge.getEditor ? App.bridge.getEditor() : null;
      if (!ed && window.parent && window.parent.LukeToolsBridge && window.parent.LukeToolsBridge.getEditor) ed = window.parent.LukeToolsBridge.getEditor();
      if (ed) {
        if (ed.project) ed.project.unsavedChanges = true;
        if (typeof ed.projectDidChange === 'function') ed.projectDidChange();
        if (typeof ed.syncInterfaces === 'function') ed.syncInterfaces();
        if (ed.canvas && typeof ed.canvas.render === 'function') ed.canvas.render();
      }
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function ensureProxyOverlayCanvasForTimeline(){ // FIX v10.9
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc) return;
    var wickCanvas = proxyTimelineCanvas();
    if (!wickCanvas) return;
    var container = wickCanvas.parentElement;
    if (!container) return;
    if (window.parent.getComputedStyle(container).position === 'static') container.style.position = 'relative';
    if (App.proxy.overlayCanvas && App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode) {
      App.proxy.active = true;
      scheduleProxyFrame();
      return;
    }
    var canvas = pdoc.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.id = 'ltbw-proxy-keyframe-canvas';
    canvas.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'proxy-keyframe-canvas');
    canvas.width = wickCanvas.width;
    canvas.height = wickCanvas.height;
    canvas.style.cssText = [
      'position:absolute','left:0','top:0',
      'width:' + wickCanvas.offsetWidth + 'px','height:' + wickCanvas.offsetHeight + 'px',
      'pointer-events:none','z-index:5000'
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(canvas);
    App.proxy.overlayCanvas = canvas;
    App.proxy.container = container;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = proxyScrollContainer();
    try { if (App.proxy.scrollContainer) App.proxy.scrollContainer.addEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, { passive:true, capture:true }); } catch(e){}
    try { container.addEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, { passive:true, capture:true }); } catch(e){}
    proxyAttachFollowListeners(); // FIX v10.9
    App.proxy.active = true;
    startProxyLoop();
    scheduleProxyFrame();
  }

  // FIX v10.9: Real proxy timeline layers are now created per BoneWarp bone using the same approach as KeyframeOverlay_v32.
  function proxyLayerNameForBone(bone){
    return String((bone && bone.name) || ('Bone ' + (bone && bone.id || ''))).trim(); // FIX v16.1
  }

  function proxyLayerNameForFrameBone(frameBone){ // FIX v13.7
    return 'F_Bone ' + String((frameBone && frameBone.id) || '1').trim(); // FIX v16.1
  }

  function proxyKeyFramesForFrameBone(frameBone){ // FIX v13.7
    var out = [];
    var id = frameBone ? Number(frameBone.id) : 0;
    Object.keys(App.frameBoneKeys || {}).forEach(function(frame){
      var f = Number(frame);
      if (!isNaN(f) && App.frameBoneKeys[frame] && App.frameBoneKeys[frame][id] !== undefined) out.push(f);
    });
    out.sort(function(a,b){ return a-b; });
    return out;
  }

  function proxyFindLayerInfoForFrameBoneId(frameBoneId){ // FIX v13.7
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    frameBoneId = Number(frameBoneId);
    for (var i = 0; i < App.proxy.layers.length; i++) {
      if (App.proxy.layers[i].type === 'frameBone' && Number(App.proxy.layers[i].frameBoneId) === frameBoneId) return App.proxy.layers[i];
    }
    return null;
  }

  function proxyFindExistingWickProxyLayerForFrameBone(frameBone){ // FIX v13.7
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!tl || !tl.layers || !frameBone) return null;
    var wantedName = proxyLayerNameForFrameBone(frameBone);
    for (var i = 0; i < tl.layers.length; i++) {
      var layer = tl.layers[i];
      var layerName = '';
      try { layerName = String(layer.name || layer.identifier || ''); } catch(e){}
      try { if (Number(layer._ltbwProxyFrameBoneId) === Number(frameBone.id)) return layer; } catch(e){}
      if (layerName === wantedName) return layer;
    }
    return null;
  }

  function proxyCreateWickLayerForFrameBone(frameBone){ // FIX v13.7
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    if (!frameBone) return null;
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!tl || !tl.layers) return null;
    var layerName = proxyLayerNameForFrameBone(frameBone);
    var existing = proxyFindLayerInfoForFrameBoneId(frameBone.id);
    if (existing && existing.wickLayer && tl.layers.indexOf(existing.wickLayer) !== -1) {
      try { existing.wickLayer.name = layerName; } catch(e){}
      try { existing.wickLayer.identifier = frameBoneProxyIdentifierForFrameBone(frameBone); } catch(e){}
      existing.frameBoneName = frameBone.name;
      existing.name = layerName;
      return existing;
    }
    var foundLayer = proxyFindExistingWickProxyLayerForFrameBone(frameBone);
    if (foundLayer) {
      try { foundLayer.name = layerName; } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer.identifier = frameBoneProxyIdentifierForFrameBone(frameBone); } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer.locked = true; } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer._ltbwProxyFrameBoneId = frameBone.id; } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer._ltbwProxyLayer = true; } catch(e){}
      var recovered = { type:'frameBone', frameBoneId: frameBone.id, frameBoneName: frameBone.name, name: layerName, wickLayer: foundLayer };
      App.proxy.layers.push(recovered);
      return recovered;
    }
    if (!App.Wick || !App.Wick.Layer) return null;
    var layer = null;
    try { layer = new App.Wick.Layer({ name: layerName, identifier: frameBoneProxyIdentifierForFrameBone(frameBone) }); }
    catch(e) { try { layer = new window.parent.Wick.Layer({ name: layerName, identifier: frameBoneProxyIdentifierForFrameBone(frameBone) }); } catch(e2){} }
    if (!layer) return null;
    try { layer.name = layerName; } catch(e){}
    try { layer.identifier = frameBoneProxyIdentifierForFrameBone(frameBone); } catch(e){}
    try { layer.locked = true; } catch(e){}
    try { layer._ltbwProxyFrameBoneId = frameBone.id; } catch(e){}
    try { layer._ltbwProxyLayer = true; } catch(e){}
    try {
      if (typeof tl.addLayer === 'function') tl.addLayer(layer);
      else if (tl.layers && typeof tl.layers.push === 'function') tl.layers.push(layer);
      else return null;
    } catch(addErr) { return null; }
    var info = { type:'frameBone', frameBoneId: frameBone.id, frameBoneName: frameBone.name, name: layerName, wickLayer: layer };
    App.proxy.layers.push(info);
    markDirty();
    proxyRefreshWickTimelineUI();
    return info;
  }

  function removeProxyLayerForFrameBoneId(frameBoneId){ // FIX v13.7
    try {
      proxyEnsureLayerStore();
      var tl = proxyTimeline();
      for (var i = App.proxy.layers.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        var info = App.proxy.layers[i];
        if (info.type !== 'frameBone' || Number(info.frameBoneId) !== Number(frameBoneId)) continue;
        var wl = info.wickLayer;
        if (tl && wl) {
          try { if (typeof tl.removeLayer === 'function') tl.removeLayer(wl); } catch(e){}
          try { if (tl.layers) { var idx = tl.layers.indexOf(wl); if (idx !== -1) tl.layers.splice(idx, 1); } } catch(e){}
        }
        App.proxy.layers.splice(i, 1);
      }
      proxyRefreshWickTimelineUI();
      scheduleProxyFrame();
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function ensureProxyLayerForCreatedFrameBone(frameBone){ // FIX v13.7
    try {
      if (!frameBone) return;
      proxyEnsureLayerStore();
      proxyCreateWickLayerForFrameBone(frameBone);
      ensureProxyOverlayCanvasForTimeline();
      renderProxyFrame();
      updateUI();
    } catch(e) {
      try { log('Frame Bone proxy layer create warning: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e)); } catch(ignore){}
    }
  }

  function proxyEnsureLayerStore(){
    if (!App.proxy.layers) App.proxy.layers = [];
    if (!App.proxy.hitDivs) App.proxy.hitDivs = [];
    if (!App.proxy.blockDivs) App.proxy.blockDivs = [];
    if (!App.proxy.hitMeta) App.proxy.hitMeta = [];
  }

  function proxyFindLayerInfoForBoneId(boneId){
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    boneId = Number(boneId); // FIX v12.5
    for (var i = 0; i < App.proxy.layers.length; i++) {
      if ((App.proxy.layers[i].type === 'bone' || !App.proxy.layers[i].type) && Number(App.proxy.layers[i].boneId) === boneId) return App.proxy.layers[i];
    }
    return null;
  }

  function removeProxyLayerForBoneId(boneId){ // FIX v10.9
    try {
      proxyEnsureLayerStore();
      var tl = proxyTimeline();
      for (var i = App.proxy.layers.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        var info = App.proxy.layers[i];
        if (Number(info.boneId) !== Number(boneId)) continue;
        var wl = info.wickLayer;
        if (tl && wl) {
          try { if (typeof tl.removeLayer === 'function') tl.removeLayer(wl); } catch(e){}
          try { if (tl.layers) { var idx = tl.layers.indexOf(wl); if (idx !== -1) tl.layers.splice(idx, 1); } } catch(e){}
        }
        App.proxy.layers.splice(i, 1);
      }
      proxyRefreshWickTimelineUI();
      scheduleProxyFrame();
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function proxyFindExistingWickProxyLayerForBone(bone){ // FIX v12.5
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!tl || !tl.layers || !bone) return null;
    var wantedName = proxyLayerNameForBone(bone);
    for (var i = 0; i < tl.layers.length; i++) {
      var layer = tl.layers[i];
      var layerName = '';
      try { layerName = String(layer.name || layer.identifier || ''); } catch(e){}
      try { if (Number(layer._ltbwProxyBoneId) === Number(bone.id)) return layer; } catch(e){}
      if (layerName === wantedName) return layer;
    }
    return null;
  }

  function proxyCreateWickLayerForBone(bone){
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    if (!bone) return null; // FIX v12.5
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!tl || !tl.layers) return null;
    var layerName = proxyLayerNameForBone(bone);

    var existing = proxyFindLayerInfoForBoneId(bone.id);
    if (existing && existing.wickLayer && tl.layers.indexOf(existing.wickLayer) !== -1) {
      try { existing.wickLayer.name = layerName; } catch(e){}
      try { existing.wickLayer.identifier = boneProxyIdentifierForBone(bone); } catch(e){} // FIX v12.7
      existing.boneName = bone.name;
      existing.name = layerName;
      return existing;
    }

    var foundLayer = proxyFindExistingWickProxyLayerForBone(bone); // FIX v12.5: recover rows that exist in Wick but are missing from App.proxy.layers
    if (foundLayer) {
      try { foundLayer.name = layerName; } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer.identifier = boneProxyIdentifierForBone(bone); } catch(e){} // FIX v12.7
      try { foundLayer.locked = true; } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer._ltbwProxyBoneId = bone.id; } catch(e){}
      try { foundLayer._ltbwProxyLayer = true; } catch(e){}
      var recovered = { type:'bone', boneId: bone.id, boneName: bone.name, name: layerName, wickLayer: foundLayer };
      App.proxy.layers.push(recovered);
      return recovered;
    }

    if (!App.Wick || !App.Wick.Layer) return null;
    var layer = null;
    try { layer = new App.Wick.Layer({ name: layerName, identifier: boneProxyIdentifierForBone(bone) }); }
    catch(e) { try { layer = new window.parent.Wick.Layer({ name: layerName, identifier: boneProxyIdentifierForBone(bone) }); } catch(e2){} } // FIX v12.7
    if (!layer) return null;
    try { layer.name = layerName; } catch(e){}
    try { layer.identifier = boneProxyIdentifierForBone(bone); } catch(e){} // FIX v12.7
    try { layer.locked = true; } catch(e){}
    try { layer._ltbwProxyBoneId = bone.id; } catch(e){} // FIX v12.5
    try { layer._ltbwProxyLayer = true; } catch(e){} // FIX v12.5
    try {
      if (typeof tl.addLayer === 'function') tl.addLayer(layer);
      else if (tl.layers && typeof tl.layers.push === 'function') tl.layers.push(layer);
      else return null;
    } catch(addErr) { return null; }
    var info = { type:'bone', boneId: bone.id, boneName: bone.name, name: layerName, wickLayer: layer };
    App.proxy.layers.push(info);
    markDirty();
    proxyRefreshWickTimelineUI(); // FIX v10.9: make the new locked Wick layer appear immediately in the timeline
    return info;
  }

  function setupProxyLayer(){ // FIX v10.9: replacement for old single layer setup
    var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
    if (!pdoc) { log('Proxy setup failed: parent document not available.'); return; }
    var wickCanvas = proxyTimelineCanvas();
    if (!wickCanvas) { log('Proxy setup failed: Wick timeline canvas not found.'); return; }
    var container = wickCanvas.parentElement;
    if (!container) { log('Proxy setup failed: Wick timeline canvas has no parent.'); return; }
    if (window.parent.getComputedStyle(container).position === 'static') container.style.position = 'relative';
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    App.bones.forEach(function(bone){ proxyCreateWickLayerForBone(bone); });
    (App.frameBones || []).forEach(function(frameBone){ proxyCreateWickLayerForFrameBone(frameBone); }); // FIX v13.7
    if (!App.proxy.layers.length) { log('Proxy setup: create bones or frame bones first.'); return; }
    if (App.proxy.overlayCanvas && App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode) App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode.removeChild(App.proxy.overlayCanvas);
    (App.proxy.hitDivs || []).forEach(function(d){ try { if (d && d.parentNode) d.parentNode.removeChild(d); } catch(e){} });
    (App.proxy.blockDivs || []).forEach(function(d){ try { if (d && d.parentNode) d.parentNode.removeChild(d); } catch(e){} });
    App.proxy.hitDivs = [];
    App.proxy.blockDivs = [];
    var canvas = pdoc.createElement('canvas');
    canvas.id = 'ltbw-proxy-keyframe-canvas';
    canvas.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'proxy-keyframe-canvas');
    canvas.width = wickCanvas.width;
    canvas.height = wickCanvas.height;
    canvas.style.cssText = [
      'position:absolute','left:0','top:0',
      'width:' + wickCanvas.offsetWidth + 'px','height:' + wickCanvas.offsetHeight + 'px',
      'pointer-events:none','z-index:5000'
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(canvas);
    App.proxy.overlayCanvas = canvas;
    App.proxy.container = container;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = proxyScrollContainer();
    try { if (App.proxy.scrollContainer) App.proxy.scrollContainer.addEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, { passive:true, capture:true }); } catch(e){}
    try { container.addEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, { passive:true, capture:true }); } catch(e){}
    proxyAttachFollowListeners(); // FIX v10.9
    App.proxy.active = true;
    startProxyLoop();
    renderProxyFrame();
    updateUI();
    log('Proxy bone keyframe layers created: ' + App.proxy.layers.length + '.');
  }

  function createProxyWickLayer(){ // FIX v10.9: compatibility wrapper
    setupProxyLayer();
    return App.proxy.layers && App.proxy.layers.length ? App.proxy.layers[0].wickLayer : null;
  }

  function removeProxyWickLayer(){ // FIX v10.9: remove all BoneWarp proxy layers
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    App.proxy.layers.forEach(function(info){
      var wl = info && info.wickLayer;
      if (tl && wl) {
        try { if (typeof tl.removeLayer === 'function') tl.removeLayer(wl); } catch(e){}
        try { if (tl.layers) { var i = tl.layers.indexOf(wl); if (i !== -1) tl.layers.splice(i, 1); } } catch(e){}
      }
    });
    App.proxy.layers = [];
    App.proxy.wickLayer = null;
    markDirty();
  }

  function removeProxyOverlay(keepLayer){ // FIX v10.9
    try { if (App.proxy.rafId) window.parent.cancelAnimationFrame(App.proxy.rafId); } catch(e){}
    App.proxy.rafId = null;
    if (!keepLayer) removeProxyWickLayer();
    try { if (App.proxy.scrollContainer) App.proxy.scrollContainer.removeEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, true); } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.proxy.container) App.proxy.container.removeEventListener('scroll', scheduleProxyFrame, true); } catch(e){}
    proxyRemoveFollowListeners(); // FIX v10.9
    (App.proxy.hitDivs || []).forEach(function(d){ try { if (d && d.parentNode) d.parentNode.removeChild(d); } catch(e){} });
    (App.proxy.blockDivs || []).forEach(function(d){ try { if (d && d.parentNode) d.parentNode.removeChild(d); } catch(e){} });
    try { if (App.proxy.overlayCanvas && App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode) App.proxy.overlayCanvas.parentNode.removeChild(App.proxy.overlayCanvas); } catch(e){}
    App.proxy.overlayCanvas = null;
    App.proxy.hitDivs = [];
    App.proxy.blockDivs = [];
    App.proxy.hitMeta = [];
    App.proxy.container = null;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = null;
    App.proxy.framePending = false;
    App.proxy.active = false;
    updateUI();
  }

  function proxyKeyFramesForBone(bone){ // FIX v10.9
    var out = [];
    var keys = getSortedKeyFrames();
    keys.forEach(function(frame){
      var pose = App.keyframes[frame];
      if (pose && poseHasBone(pose, bone.id)) out.push(frame);
    });
    return out;
  }

  function proxyLayerFrameSpan(){ // FIX v10.9
    var maxEnd = Math.max(1, App.frameCount || 1);
    try {
      var tl = proxyTimeline();
      if (tl && tl.layers) {
        tl.layers.forEach(function(layer){
          var isProxy = false;
          (App.proxy.layers || []).forEach(function(info){ if (info.wickLayer === layer) isProxy = true; });
          if (isProxy) return;
          (layer.frames || []).forEach(function(frame){ maxEnd = Math.max(maxEnd, getFrameEnd(frame)); });
        });
      }
    } catch(e){}
    return maxEnd;
  }

  function proxyRowYForLayerInfo(info, tl, CH, BCH, NLH, scrollY){ // FIX v10.9
    /* FIX v10.9: Use the same Wick timeline formula as KeyframeOverlay_v32.
       Y = breadcrumbs + number line + layer index * cell height - project.scrollY.
       This makes the diamonds move vertically with their real Wick proxy layer rows. */
    var idx = -1;
    try { idx = tl && tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(info.wickLayer) : -1; } catch(e){}
    if (idx < 0) return null;
    return BCH + NLH + idx * CH - scrollY + 3;
  }


  function renderProxyFrame(){ // FIX v15.7: draw one proxy row per bone layer and keep it following Wick scroll using the active render path
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    App.proxy.framePending = false;
    App.proxy.scrollContainer = proxyScrollContainer() || App.proxy.scrollContainer; // FIX v10.9
    var canvas = App.proxy.overlayCanvas;
    if (!canvas) return;
    var wickCanvas = proxyTimelineCanvas();
    var tl = proxyTimeline();
    if (!wickCanvas || !tl || !App.proxy.layers.length) return;
    if (canvas.width !== wickCanvas.width) canvas.width = wickCanvas.width;
    if (canvas.height !== wickCanvas.height) canvas.height = wickCanvas.height;
    canvas.style.width = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetWidth) + 'px'; // FIX v15.7: do not compress the active overlay canvas by subtracting the scrollbar width.
    canvas.style.height = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetHeight) + 'px'; // FIX v15.7
    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    var cssW = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetWidth || canvas.width || 1); // FIX v15.7
    var cssH = Math.max(1, wickCanvas.offsetHeight || canvas.height || 1); // FIX v15.7
    var scaleX = Math.max(0.01, (canvas.width || cssW) / cssW); // FIX v15.7
    var scaleY = Math.max(0.01, (canvas.height || cssH) / cssH); // FIX v15.7
    var baseCW = proxyCellWidth() * scaleX; // FIX v15.7
    var CW = baseCW; // FIX v15.8: removed the 4.1 percent shrink. Use the Wick cell width unchanged.
    var CH = proxyCellHeight() * scaleY; // FIX v15.7
    var LCW = proxyLayerColumnWidth() * scaleX; // FIX v15.7
    var BCH = proxyBreadcrumbHeight() * scaleY; // FIX v15.7
    var NLH = proxyNumberLineHeight() * scaleY; // FIX v15.7
    var scrollX = proxyScrollX() * scaleX; // FIX v15.8: removed the 4.1 percent shrink from scroll correction.
    var scrollY = proxyScrollY() * scaleY; // FIX v15.7
    var proxyFirstCellShift = baseCW * 0.03; // FIX v16.0: move the proxy timeline to the right by 3 percent of one Wick cell.
    var rowLeft = LCW;
    var rowRight = canvas.width - proxyScrollbarSize() * scaleX; // FIX v15.7
    var frameAreaX = LCW + proxyFirstCellShift - Number(scrollX || 0); // FIX v16.0: apply a 3 percent right shift to the proxy timeline.
    var span = proxyLayerFrameSpan();
    var ph = proxyCurrentPlayhead();
    var DR = 7;
    var hitMeta = [];
    var clipTop = BCH + NLH; // FIX v11.3: clip all proxy drawing to below breadcrumb + number line
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.rect(rowLeft, clipTop, Math.max(1, canvas.width - rowLeft), Math.max(1, canvas.height - clipTop)); // FIX v16.1: clip proxy drawing at the layer-name edge.
    ctx.clip();

    App.proxy.layers.forEach(function(info, layerOrderIndex){
      var isFrameBoneLayer = info && info.type === 'frameBone'; // FIX v13.7
      var bone = isFrameBoneLayer ? null : getBoneById(info.boneId);
      var frameBone = isFrameBoneLayer ? getFrameBoneById(info.frameBoneId) : null;
      if (!isFrameBoneLayer && !bone) return;
      if (isFrameBoneLayer && !frameBone) return;
      var layerIdx = tl.layers ? tl.layers.indexOf(info.wickLayer) : -1;
      if (layerIdx < 0) return;
      var rowY = proxyRowYForLayerInfo(info, tl, CH, BCH, NLH, scrollY); // FIX v15.7
      if (rowY == null) return;
      var rowH = CH - 3;
      if (rowY + rowH < BCH + NLH || rowY > canvas.height) return;
      var cy = rowY + CH / 2;
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,28,36,0.72)';
      ctx.fillRect(rowLeft, rowY, Math.max(1, rowRight - rowLeft), rowH);
      ctx.fillStyle = isFrameBoneLayer ? 'rgba(226,181,61,0.18)' : (layerOrderIndex === 0 ? 'rgba(30,226,154,0.18)' : 'rgba(95,97,99,0.18)'); // FIX v13.7
      ctx.fillRect(frameAreaX, rowY, Math.max(1, span * CW - 1), rowH); // FIX v15.7: use corrected frame width.
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.24)';
      ctx.lineWidth = 1;
      for (var f = 1; f <= span; f++) {
        var gx = frameAreaX + (f - 1) * CW; // FIX v15.7
        if (gx < rowLeft || gx > rowRight) continue;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(gx, rowY); ctx.lineTo(gx, rowY + rowH); ctx.stroke();
      }
      var keys = isFrameBoneLayer ? proxyKeyFramesForFrameBone(frameBone) : proxyKeyFramesForBone(bone); // FIX v13.7
      for (var i = 0; i < keys.length - 1; i++) {
        var x1 = frameAreaX + (keys[i] - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
        var x2 = frameAreaX + (keys[i + 1] - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x1 + DR + 2, cy); ctx.lineTo(x2 - DR - 2, cy);
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#8E8E8E'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
        var tip = x2 - DR - 2;
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(tip - 7, cy - 4); ctx.lineTo(tip, cy); ctx.lineTo(tip - 7, cy + 4);
        ctx.strokeStyle = '#8E8E8E'; ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.lineJoin = 'round'; ctx.lineCap = 'round'; ctx.stroke();
      }
      keys.forEach(function(k){
        var cx = frameAreaX + (k - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
        if (cx >= rowLeft && cx <= rowRight + 20) { // FIX v16.1
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(cx + 2, cy - DR + 2); ctx.lineTo(cx + DR + 2, cy + 2); ctx.lineTo(cx + 2, cy + DR + 2); ctx.lineTo(cx - DR + 2, cy + 2); ctx.closePath();
          ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.9)'; ctx.fill();
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(cx, cy - DR); ctx.lineTo(cx + DR, cy); ctx.lineTo(cx, cy + DR); ctx.lineTo(cx - DR, cy); ctx.closePath();
          ctx.fillStyle = isFrameBoneLayer ? '#E2B53D' : '#1EE29A'; ctx.fill(); // FIX v13.7
          ctx.strokeStyle = '#222244'; ctx.lineWidth = 3; ctx.stroke();
          if (isFrameBoneLayer) {
            ctx.font = 'bold ' + Math.max(8, 9 * scaleY) + 'px Arial';
            ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
            ctx.fillText(frameBoneSlotTitle(frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(frameBone, k)), cx + 9, cy + 3);
            hitMeta.push({ frame:k, frameBoneId:frameBone.id, type:'frameBone', x:cx, y:cy, cssX:cx / scaleX, cssY:cy / scaleY }); // FIX v15.7
          } else {
            hitMeta.push({ frame:k, boneId:bone.id, type:'bone', x:cx, y:cy, cssX:cx / scaleX, cssY:cy / scaleY }); // FIX v15.7
          }
        }
      });
      var hx = frameAreaX + (ph - 1) * CW;
      ctx.strokeStyle = '#1EE29A'; ctx.lineWidth = 2;
      ctx.strokeRect(hx + 0.5, rowY + 0.5, Math.max(1, CW - 1), Math.max(1, CH - 1)); // FIX v15.7
      var px = frameAreaX + (ph - 1) * CW + CW / 2;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(px, rowY); ctx.lineTo(px, rowY + rowH); ctx.strokeStyle = '#FF5C5C'; ctx.lineWidth = 3; ctx.stroke();
    });
    ctx.restore(); // FIX v11.3: end clip region
    App.proxy.hitMeta = hitMeta;
    updateProxyHits(tl, rowLeft / scaleX, rowRight / scaleX); // FIX v15.7: convert hit clipping back to CSS pixels.
    if (el('proxyInfo')) {
      var boneLayerCount = 0, frameBoneLayerCount = 0;
      (App.proxy.layers || []).forEach(function(info){ if (info && info.type === 'frameBone') frameBoneLayerCount++; else boneLayerCount++; });
      el('proxyInfo').textContent = boneLayerCount + ' bone layer' + (boneLayerCount === 1 ? '' : 's') + ', ' + frameBoneLayerCount + ' frame bone layer' + (frameBoneLayerCount === 1 ? '' : 's');
    }
  }

  function updateProxyHits(tl, rowLeft, rowRight){ // FIX v15.7
    if (!App.proxy.container) return;
    var meta = App.proxy.hitMeta || [];
    var HIT = 18;
    while (App.proxy.hitDivs.length < meta.length) {
      var hd = window.parent.document.createElement('div');
      hd.setAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-kind', 'proxy-keyframe-hit');
      hd.style.cssText = ['position:absolute','z-index:5002','pointer-events:auto','cursor:pointer','background:transparent','width:' + HIT + 'px','height:' + HIT + 'px'].join(';');
      hd.addEventListener('mousedown', function(evt){
        evt.preventDefault(); evt.stopPropagation();
        var frame = Number(this.getAttribute('data-frame') || 1);
        var boneId = Number(this.getAttribute('data-bone-id') || 0);
        var frameBoneId = Number(this.getAttribute('data-frame-bone-id') || 0); // FIX v13.9
        var hitType = this.getAttribute('data-hit-type') || 'bone'; // FIX v13.9: restore missing hit type so bone key dragging does not crash
        if (hitType === 'frameBone') { // FIX v13.9: frame bone keys select and jump without blocking bone key dragging
          if (frameBoneId) App.selectedFrameBoneId = frameBoneId;
          setCurrentFrame(frame, false);
          setActiveTab('animate');
          renderOverlay();
          scheduleProxyFrame();
          return;
        }
        if (boneId) App.selectedBoneId = boneId;
        setCurrentFrame(frame, false);
        setActiveTab('animate');
        renderOverlay();
        scheduleProxyFrame();

        // FIX v13.9: drag to move this one bone's keyframe to a different Wick frame
        var startX = evt.clientX;
        var dragFrame = frame;
        var dragging = false;
        var dragWin = (window.parent && window.parent !== window) ? window.parent : window;

        function frameFromClientX(clientX){ // FIX v15.7
          var rect = App.proxy.container ? App.proxy.container.getBoundingClientRect() : null;
          var scaleX = rect && rect.width ? (App.proxy.overlayCanvas.width / rect.width) : 1;
          var baseCW = proxyCellWidth() * scaleX;
          var correctedCW = baseCW; // FIX v15.8
          var correctedStartX = (proxyLayerColumnWidth() * scaleX) + (baseCW * 0.03) - (proxyScrollX() * scaleX); // FIX v16.0: apply the same 3 percent right shift to key dragging.
          var localX = rect ? (clientX - rect.left) * scaleX : (correctedStartX + (frame - 1) * correctedCW + correctedCW / 2);
          return clamp(Math.floor((localX - correctedStartX) / correctedCW) + 1, 1, App.frameCount);
        }

        function onDragMove(e){
          e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
          if (Math.abs(e.clientX - startX) > 3) dragging = true;
          if (!dragging) return;
          var targetFrame = frameFromClientX(e.clientX);
          if (targetFrame === dragFrame) return;
          if (App.keyframes[dragFrame] && App.keyframes[dragFrame][boneId] !== undefined) {
            var movedPose = clone(App.keyframes[dragFrame][boneId]);
            if (!App.keyframes[targetFrame]) App.keyframes[targetFrame] = {};
            App.keyframes[targetFrame][boneId] = movedPose;
            delete App.keyframes[dragFrame][boneId];
            removeEmptyKeyFrame(dragFrame);
            dragFrame = targetFrame;
            setCurrentFrame(targetFrame, false);
            markDirty();
            scheduleProxyFrame();
            renderOverlay();
          }
        }

        function onDragUp(e){
          if (e) { e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation(); }
          dragWin.removeEventListener('mousemove', onDragMove, true);
          dragWin.removeEventListener('mouseup', onDragUp, true);
          if (dragging) { markDirty(); scheduleProxyFrame(); renderOverlay(); }
        }

        dragWin.addEventListener('mousemove', onDragMove, true);
        dragWin.addEventListener('mouseup', onDragUp, true);
      });
      App.proxy.container.appendChild(hd);
      App.proxy.hitDivs.push(hd);
    }
    for (var i = meta.length; i < App.proxy.hitDivs.length; i++) App.proxy.hitDivs[i].style.display = 'none';
    meta.forEach(function(item, i){
      var hd = App.proxy.hitDivs[i];
      if (!hd) return;
      var hx = Number(item.cssX != null ? item.cssX : item.x); // FIX v15.7
      var hy = Number(item.cssY != null ? item.cssY : item.y); // FIX v15.7
      if (hx < rowLeft || hx > rowRight + 20) { hd.style.display = 'none'; return; } // FIX v16.1
      hd.style.display = 'block';
      hd.style.left = (hx - HIT / 2) + 'px';
      hd.style.top = (hy - HIT / 2) + 'px';
      hd.setAttribute('data-frame', String(item.frame));
      hd.setAttribute('data-hit-type', item.type || 'bone'); // FIX v13.7
      hd.setAttribute('data-bone-id', String(item.boneId || 0));
      hd.setAttribute('data-frame-bone-id', String(item.frameBoneId || 0)); // FIX v13.7
    });
  }

  function syncProxyLayersToBones(force){ // FIX v12.5
    if (!force && !App.proxy.active) return;
    proxyEnsureLayerStore();
    App.bones.forEach(function(bone){ proxyCreateWickLayerForBone(bone); }); // FIX v16.1: every bone must have its own proxy row
    (App.frameBones || []).forEach(function(frameBone){ proxyCreateWickLayerForFrameBone(frameBone); }); // FIX v13.7: every Frame Bone gets its own visible key row
    scheduleProxyFrame();
  }

  function renderTimelineOverlay(){
    // FIX v4.3: removed the extra warp timeline indicator.
    // Wick's real timeline is the only timeline display now.
    return;
  }

  function roundedRectPath(ctx, x, y, w, h, r){
    r = Math.min(r, w*0.5, h*0.5);
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x+r, y);
    ctx.lineTo(x+w-r, y);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(x+w, y, x+w, y+r);
    ctx.lineTo(x+w, y+h-r);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(x+w, y+h, x+w-r, y+h);
    ctx.lineTo(x+r, y+h);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(x, y+h, x, y+h-r);
    ctx.lineTo(x, y+r);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(x, y, x+r, y);
    ctx.closePath();
  }

  function onTimelineMouseDown(e){
    // FIX v4.3: no separate warp timeline overlay.
    return;
  }

  function dataURLToFile(dataUrl, filename){
    var parts = dataUrl.split(',');
    var mime = parts[0].match(/:(.*?);/)[1];
    var bstr = atob(parts[1]);
    var arr = new Uint8Array(bstr.length);
    for (var i = 0; i < bstr.length; i++) arr[i] = bstr.charCodeAt(i);
    return new File([arr], filename, { type: mime });
  }

  function waitForAssets(names, timeoutMs){
    var target = {};
    names.forEach(function(n){ target[n] = true; });
    var start = Date.now();
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      (function tick(){
        var assets = [];
        try { assets = App.project.getAssets ? App.project.getAssets() : App.project.assets || []; } catch(e){}
        var found = {};
        assets.forEach(function(a){
          try {
            var nm = a.name || a.filename || a.identifier;
            if (target[nm]) found[nm] = a;
          } catch(e){}
        });
        if (Object.keys(found).length === names.length) return resolve(found);
        if (Date.now() - start > timeoutMs) return reject(new Error('Timed out waiting for assets'));
        setTimeout(tick, 120);
      })();
    });
  }

  function createImagePathFromAssetAny(asset){
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      try {
        if (App.Wick && App.Wick.Path && typeof App.Wick.Path.createImagePath === 'function') {
          App.Wick.Path.createImagePath(asset, function(path){ resolve(path); });
          return;
        }
      } catch(e){}
      reject(new Error('Wick.Path.createImagePath is not available in this build'));
    });
  }

  function fileToDataUrlForCommit(file){ // FIX v14.1
    return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
      try {
        var reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(){ resolve(String(reader.result || '')); };
        reader.onerror = function(){ reject(reader.error || new Error('Could not read commit file.')); };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
      } catch(e) { reject(e); }
    });
  }

  function getProjectAssetsArray(){ // FIX v14.1
    try { if (App.project && typeof App.project.getAssets === 'function') return App.project.getAssets() || []; } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project && Array.isArray(App.project.assets)) return App.project.assets; } catch(e){}
    try { if (App.project && App.project.assetLibrary && Array.isArray(App.project.assetLibrary.assets)) return App.project.assetLibrary.assets; } catch(e){}
    return [];
  }

  function projectHasAssetNamed(name){ // FIX v14.1
    var assets = getProjectAssetsArray();
    for (var i = 0; i < assets.length; i++) {
      try {
        var nm = assets[i].name || assets[i].filename || assets[i].identifier;
        if (nm === name) return true;
      } catch(e){}
    }
    return false;
  }

  function makeSyntheticSvgAssetForProject(name, dataUrl, file){ // FIX v14.1 fallback only when the editor API refuses SVG asset creation
    var asset = {
      name: name,
      filename: name,
      identifier: makeValidIdentifier(name, 'BoneWarp_SVG_Asset'),
      src: dataUrl,
      dataUrl: dataUrl,
      file: file,
      mimeType: file && file.type ? file.type : 'image/svg+xml',
      type: 'image/svg+xml',
      _ltbwSyntheticSvgAsset: true
    };
    return asset;
  }

  async function forceCommitFilesIntoAssets(files, names){ // FIX v14.1
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    try {
      if (App.ed && typeof App.ed.createAssets === 'function') {
        await new Promise(function(resolve){
          var done = false;
          function finish(){ if (done) return; done = true; resolve(); }
          try { App.ed.createAssets(files, finish); } catch(e) { finish(); }
          setTimeout(finish, 500);
        });
      }
    } catch(e){}

    /* Some Wick builds import PNGs through createAssets but silently ignore SVG files.
       Keep a real asset record in the project asset array as a fallback so the committed
       SVG frames are project content and not only temporary object URLs. */
    try {
      if (App.project && !Array.isArray(App.project.assets)) App.project.assets = [];
    } catch(e){}
    for (var i = 0; i < files.length; i++) {
      var name = names[i] || (files[i] && files[i].name) || ('BoneWarp_' + i + '.svg');
      if (projectHasAssetNamed(name)) continue;
      if (/\.svg$/i.test(name)) {
        try {
          var dataUrl = await fileToDataUrlForCommit(files[i]);
          var synthetic = makeSyntheticSvgAssetForProject(name, dataUrl, files[i]);
          try {
            if (App.project && typeof App.project.addAsset === 'function') App.project.addAsset(synthetic);
            else if (App.project && Array.isArray(App.project.assets)) App.project.assets.push(synthetic);
          } catch(addErr) {
            try { if (App.project && Array.isArray(App.project.assets)) App.project.assets.push(synthetic); } catch(e2){}
          }
        } catch(readErr){}
      }
    }
    markDirty();
  }

  function rotatedBoxBounds(cx, cy, w, h, angle){ // FIX v14.1
    var hw = Math.max(0, Number(w || 0)) * 0.5;
    var hh = Math.max(0, Number(h || 0)) * 0.5;
    var c = Math.cos(Number(angle || 0));
    var s2 = Math.sin(Number(angle || 0));
    var pts = [
      { x:-hw, y:-hh }, { x:hw, y:-hh }, { x:hw, y:hh }, { x:-hw, y:hh }
    ].map(function(p){ return { x: cx + p.x * c - p.y * s2, y: cy + p.x * s2 + p.y * c }; });
    var minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;
    pts.forEach(function(pt){ if (pt.x < minX) minX = pt.x; if (pt.y < minY) minY = pt.y; if (pt.x > maxX) maxX = pt.x; if (pt.y > maxY) maxY = pt.y; });
    return { minX:minX, minY:minY, maxX:maxX, maxY:maxY };
  }

  function getVisibleWarpBoundsForPose(pose, frameNum){ // FIX v14.1: include frame bone extents so commit cannot clip them
    var minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity; // FIX v6.9
    function addPoint(pt){ // FIX v6.9
      if (!pt) return; // FIX v6.9
      if (pt.x < minX) minX = pt.x; // FIX v6.9
      if (pt.y < minY) minY = pt.y; // FIX v6.9
      if (pt.x > maxX) maxX = pt.x; // FIX v6.9
      if (pt.y > maxY) maxY = pt.y; // FIX v6.9
    }
    if (App.source.svgNative && App.source.svgNative.shapes && App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) { // FIX v7.5
      App.source.svgNative.shapes.forEach(function(shape){ // FIX v7.5
        (shape.cmdSubpaths || []).forEach(function(sp){ // FIX v7.5
          (sp.commands || []).forEach(function(cmd){ // FIX v7.5
            if (cmd.p) addPoint(skinPointByPose(cmd.p, pose)); // FIX v7.5
            if (cmd.c1) addPoint(skinPointByPose(cmd.c1, pose)); // FIX v7.5
            if (cmd.c2) addPoint(skinPointByPose(cmd.c2, pose)); // FIX v7.5
          });
        });
      });
    } else {
      var rest = buildRestVertices(); // FIX v6.9
      var warped = buildWarpedVertices(pose); // FIX v6.9
      for (var y = 0; y < App.grid.rows; y++) { // FIX v6.9
        for (var x = 0; x < App.grid.cols; x++) { // FIX v6.9
          var i00 = vertexIndex(x, y); // FIX v6.9
          var i10 = vertexIndex(x + 1, y); // FIX v6.9
          var i01 = vertexIndex(x, y + 1); // FIX v6.9
          var i11 = vertexIndex(x + 1, y + 1); // FIX v6.9
          var s00 = rest[i00], s10 = rest[i10], s01 = rest[i01], s11 = rest[i11]; // FIX v6.9
          var d00 = warped[i00], d10 = warped[i10], d01 = warped[i01], d11 = warped[i11]; // FIX v6.9
          if (triangleHasOpaqueContent(s00, s10, s11)) { addPoint(d00); addPoint(d10); addPoint(d11); } // FIX v6.9
          if (triangleHasOpaqueContent(s00, s11, s01)) { addPoint(d00); addPoint(d11); addPoint(d01); } // FIX v6.9
        }
      }
    }
    (App.frameBones || []).forEach(function(fb){ // FIX v14.1: frame bone SVGs can extend outside the source SVG bounds
      var slot = frameBoneSlotForTimelineFrame(fb, frameNum || App.currentFrame || 1);
      var data = fb && fb.frames ? fb.frames[slot] : null;
      if (!data) return;
      var fp = frameBonePointFromPose(fb, pose);
      var s = frameBoneScale(fb);
      var w = Math.max(1, Number(data.width || 80)) * s;
      var h = Math.max(1, Number(data.height || 80)) * s;
      var b = rotatedBoxBounds(fp.x, fp.y, w, h, (fp.angle || 0) + frameBoneRotationRad(fb));
      addPoint({ x:b.minX, y:b.minY }); addPoint({ x:b.maxX, y:b.maxY });
    });
    if (!isFinite(minX) || !isFinite(minY) || !isFinite(maxX) || !isFinite(maxY)) { // FIX v6.9
      return { minX: 0, minY: 0, maxX: App.source.width, maxY: App.source.height, width: App.source.width, height: App.source.height }; // FIX v6.9
    }
    return { minX: minX, minY: minY, maxX: maxX, maxY: maxY, width: Math.max(1, maxX - minX), height: Math.max(1, maxY - minY) }; // FIX v6.9
  }

  function computeAnimationExportBounds(){ // FIX v6.9
    var minX = 0, minY = 0, maxX = Math.max(1, App.source.width), maxY = Math.max(1, App.source.height); // FIX v6.9
    for (var i = 1; i <= App.frameCount; i++) { // FIX v6.9
      var b = getVisibleWarpBoundsForPose(getPoseForFrame(i), i); // FIX v14.1
      if (b.minX < minX) minX = b.minX; // FIX v6.9
      if (b.minY < minY) minY = b.minY; // FIX v6.9
      if (b.maxX > maxX) maxX = b.maxX; // FIX v6.9
      if (b.maxY > maxY) maxY = b.maxY; // FIX v6.9
    }
    var pad = 2; // FIX v6.9
    minX = Math.floor(minX - pad); // FIX v6.9
    minY = Math.floor(minY - pad); // FIX v6.9
    maxX = Math.ceil(maxX + pad); // FIX v6.9
    maxY = Math.ceil(maxY + pad); // FIX v6.9
    return {
      minX: minX, // FIX v6.9
      minY: minY, // FIX v6.9
      maxX: maxX, // FIX v6.9
      maxY: maxY, // FIX v6.9
      offsetX: -minX, // FIX v6.9
      offsetY: -minY, // FIX v6.9
      width: Math.max(1, Math.round(maxX - minX)), // FIX v6.9
      height: Math.max(1, Math.round(maxY - minY)) // FIX v6.9
    };
  }

  function getCommitTimeline(project){ // FIX v13.8
    project = project || App.project;
    var tl = null;
    try { if (project && project.activeTimeline) tl = project.activeTimeline; } catch(e){}
    try { if (!tl && project && project.focus && project.focus.timeline) tl = project.focus.timeline; } catch(e){}
    try { if (!tl && project && project.timeline) tl = project.timeline; } catch(e){}
    return tl;
  }

  function getTimelinePlayheadForCommit(project, tl){ // FIX v13.8
    var ph = 1;
    try { if (tl && tl.playheadPosition) ph = Number(tl.playheadPosition) || ph; } catch(e){}
    try { if (project && project.currentFrameNumber) ph = Number(project.currentFrameNumber) || ph; } catch(e){}
    return Math.max(1, Math.round(ph || 1));
  }

  function ensureCommitLayer(tl){ // FIX v13.8
    if (!tl) throw new Error('Project timeline missing');
    var layer = null;
    try { layer = tl.activeLayer; } catch(e){}
    if (typeof layer === 'number') {
      try { layer = tl.layers[layer] || null; } catch(e){ layer = null; }
    }
    try { if (!layer && tl.layers && tl.layers.length) layer = tl.layers[0]; } catch(e){}
    if (layer) return layer;
    if (!App.Wick || !App.Wick.Layer) throw new Error('Wick.Layer is not available');
    layer = new App.Wick.Layer();
    try { layer.name = 'Layer'; } catch(e){}
    try {
      if (typeof tl.addLayer === 'function') tl.addLayer(layer);
      else if (tl.layers && typeof tl.layers.push === 'function') tl.layers.push(layer);
      else throw new Error('No layer insertion API found');
    } catch(err) {
      throw new Error('Could not create target Wick layer: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err));
    }
    return layer;
  }

  function ensureCommitFrame(layer, frameNumber){ // FIX v13.8
    frameNumber = Math.max(1, Math.round(frameNumber || 1));
    var frame = null;
    try { if (typeof layer.getFrameAtPlayheadPosition === 'function') frame = layer.getFrameAtPlayheadPosition(frameNumber); } catch(e){}
    try { if (!frame && typeof layer.getFrame === 'function') frame = layer.getFrame(frameNumber); } catch(e){}
    try {
      if (!frame && layer.frames && layer.frames.length) {
        for (var i = 0; i < layer.frames.length; i++) {
          var f = layer.frames[i];
          if (!f) continue;
          var st = Number(f.start || f.startFrame || f.startFrameNumber || 1);
          var en = Number(f.end || f.endFrame || f.endFrameNumber || st);
          if (st <= frameNumber && en >= frameNumber) { frame = f; break; }
        }
      }
    } catch(e){}
    if (frame) return frame;
    if (!App.Wick || !App.Wick.Frame) throw new Error('Wick.Frame is not available');
    frame = new App.Wick.Frame({ start: frameNumber, end: frameNumber });
    try { frame.start = frameNumber; frame.end = frameNumber; } catch(e){}
    try { frame.identifier = makeValidIdentifier('frame_' + frameNumber, 'frame_' + frameNumber); } catch(e){}
    try {
      if (typeof layer.addFrame === 'function') layer.addFrame(frame);
      else if (layer.frames && typeof layer.frames.push === 'function') layer.frames.push(frame);
      else throw new Error('No frame insertion API found');
    } catch(err) {
      throw new Error('Could not create target Wick frame: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err));
    }
    return frame;
  }

  function getActiveFrame(project){ // FIX v13.8
    project = project || App.project;
    try { if (project && project.activeFrame) return project.activeFrame; } catch(e){}
    var tl = getCommitTimeline(project);
    if (!tl) return null;
    var layer = null;
    try { layer = ensureCommitLayer(tl); } catch(e){ return null; }
    return ensureCommitFrame(layer, getTimelinePlayheadForCommit(project, tl));
  }

  function addToFrame(frame, obj){ // FIX v14.9: use every Wick insertion route needed for Clip objects and Path objects
    if (!frame) throw new Error('Active frame missing');
    var isClip = !!(obj && (
      (App.Wick && App.Wick.Clip && obj instanceof App.Wick.Clip) ||
      obj.classname === 'Clip' ||
      (obj.timeline && obj.transformation && !obj.json)
    ));
    var errors = [];
    function ensureChildArrayContains(){ // FIX v14.9
      try {
        if (Array.isArray(frame._children) && frame._children.indexOf(obj) < 0) frame._children.push(obj);
      } catch(e){}
    }
    function attempt(fn){ try { fn(); ensureChildArrayContains(); return true; } catch(e){ errors.push(e && e.message ? e.message : String(e)); return false; } }
    if (isClip) {
      if (typeof frame.addClip === 'function' && attempt(function(){ frame.addClip(obj); })) return;
      if (typeof frame.addObject === 'function' && attempt(function(){ frame.addObject(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame.clips) && attempt(function(){ frame.clips.push(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame.objects) && attempt(function(){ frame.objects.push(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame.children) && attempt(function(){ frame.children.push(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame._children) && attempt(function(){ frame._children.push(obj); })) return; // FIX v14.9
    } else {
      if (typeof frame.addPath === 'function' && attempt(function(){ frame.addPath(obj); })) return;
      if (typeof frame.addObject === 'function' && attempt(function(){ frame.addObject(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame.paths) && attempt(function(){ frame.paths.push(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame.objects) && attempt(function(){ frame.objects.push(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame.children) && attempt(function(){ frame.children.push(obj); })) return;
      if (Array.isArray(frame._children) && attempt(function(){ frame._children.push(obj); })) return; // FIX v14.9
    }
    throw new Error('No frame insertion API found' + (errors.length ? ': ' + errors.join(' | ') : ''));
  }

  function rememberSelectedCurveSourceTimeline(){ // FIX v14.8
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    var tl = getCommitTimeline(App.project);
    var layer = null;
    var frame = null;
    var frameNumber = getTimelinePlayheadForCommit(App.project, tl);
    try { layer = tl && tl.activeLayer; } catch(e){}
    if (typeof layer === 'number') { try { layer = tl.layers[layer] || null; } catch(e2){ layer = null; } }
    try { if (!layer && tl && tl.layers && tl.layers.length) layer = tl.layers[0]; } catch(e3){}
    try { if (layer) frame = ensureCommitFrame(layer, frameNumber); } catch(e4){}
    App.source.sourceTimeline = tl || null;
    App.source.sourceLayer = layer || null;
    App.source.sourceFrame = frame || null;
    App.source.sourceFrameNumber = frameNumber || 1;
  }

  function addClipToSpecificWickTimeline(clip, tl, layer, frameNumber){ // FIX v14.8
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    tl = tl || getCommitTimeline(App.project);
    if (!tl) throw new Error('Could not find the target Wick timeline');
    if (!layer) layer = ensureCommitLayer(tl);
    frameNumber = Math.max(1, Math.round(frameNumber || getTimelinePlayheadForCommit(App.project, tl) || 1));
    var frame = ensureCommitFrame(layer, frameNumber);
    addToFrame(frame, clip);
    try { App.project.activeTimeline = tl; } catch(e){}
    try { tl.activeLayer = layer; } catch(e){}
    try { App.project.activeFrame = frame; } catch(e){}
    return frame;
  }

  function addClipToWickProject(clip){ // FIX v13.8
    return addClipToSpecificWickTimeline(clip, App.source.sourceTimeline || null, App.source.sourceLayer || null, App.source.sourceFrameNumber || null); // FIX v14.8
  }

  function escapeXmlAttr(value){ // FIX v5.2
    return String(value == null ? '' : value)
      .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
      .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
      .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
      .replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
  }

  function getEmbeddedSourceDataUrl(){ // FIX v5.2
    if (App.source.embeddedDataUrl) return App.source.embeddedDataUrl;
    if (App.source.dataUrl && String(App.source.dataUrl).indexOf('data:') === 0) {
      App.source.embeddedDataUrl = App.source.dataUrl;
      return App.source.embeddedDataUrl;
    }
    try {
      var c = document.createElement('canvas');
      c.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width));
      c.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height));
      var ctx = c.getContext('2d', { alpha: true });
      ctx.clearRect(0, 0, c.width, c.height);
      ctx.drawImage(App.source.image, 0, 0, c.width, c.height);
      App.source.embeddedDataUrl = c.toDataURL('image/png');
      return App.source.embeddedDataUrl;
    } catch(e) {
      return App.source.dataUrl || '';
    }
  }

  function triangleMatrix(sx0, sy0, sx1, sy1, sx2, sy2, dx0, dy0, dx1, dy1, dx2, dy2){ // FIX v5.2
    var denom = sx0*(sy1 - sy2) + sx1*(sy2 - sy0) + sx2*(sy0 - sy1);
    if (Math.abs(denom) < 0.00001) return null;
    return {
      a: (dx0*(sy1 - sy2) + dx1*(sy2 - sy0) + dx2*(sy0 - sy1)) / denom,
      b: (dy0*(sy1 - sy2) + dy1*(sy2 - sy0) + dy2*(sy0 - sy1)) / denom,
      c: (dx0*(sx2 - sx1) + dx1*(sx0 - sx2) + dx2*(sx1 - sx0)) / denom,
      d: (dy0*(sx2 - sx1) + dy1*(sx0 - sx2) + dy2*(sx1 - sx0)) / denom,
      e: (dx0*(sx1*sy2 - sx2*sy1) + dx1*(sx2*sy0 - sx0*sy2) + dx2*(sx0*sy1 - sx1*sy0)) / denom,
      f: (dy0*(sx1*sy2 - sx2*sy1) + dy1*(sx2*sy0 - sx0*sy2) + dy2*(sx0*sy1 - sx1*sy0)) / denom
    };
  }

  function svgFileFromFrame(frameNum, fileName, exportBounds){ // FIX v6.9
    var pose = getPoseForFrame(frameNum);
    exportBounds = exportBounds || { width: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width)), height: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height)), offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 }; // FIX v6.9
    var w = Math.max(1, Math.round(exportBounds.width)); // FIX v6.9
    var h = Math.max(1, Math.round(exportBounds.height)); // FIX v6.9
    var ox = Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0); // FIX v6.9
    var oy = Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0); // FIX v6.9
    var rest = buildRestVertices();
    var warped = buildWarpedVertices(pose);
    var href = escapeXmlAttr(getEmbeddedSourceDataUrl());
    var defs = [];
    var body = [];
    var triId = 0;
    var seamOverlap = 0.9; // FIX v5.3: overlap the warped SVG triangles so the grid seams do not show through

    defs.push('<image id="ltbw_src" href="' + href + '" xlink:href="' + href + '" x="0" y="0" width="' + w + '" height="' + h + '" preserveAspectRatio="none" />');

    function expandPointFromCentroid(pt, cx, cy, amount){ // FIX v5.3
      var dx = pt.x - cx;
      var dy = pt.y - cy;
      var len = Math.sqrt(dx * dx + dy * dy) || 1;
      return { x: pt.x + (dx / len) * amount, y: pt.y + (dy / len) * amount };
    }

    function addTriangle(s0, s1, s2, d0, d1, d2){
      if (!triangleHasOpaqueContent(s0, s1, s2)) return;
      var m = triangleMatrix(s0.x, s0.y, s1.x, s1.y, s2.x, s2.y, d0.x, d0.y, d1.x, d1.y, d2.x, d2.y);
      if (!m) return;
      triId += 1;
      var id = 'ltbw_cp_' + triId;
      var td0 = { x: d0.x + ox, y: d0.y + oy }; // FIX v6.9
      var td1 = { x: d1.x + ox, y: d1.y + oy }; // FIX v6.9
      var td2 = { x: d2.x + ox, y: d2.y + oy }; // FIX v6.9
      var cx = (td0.x + td1.x + td2.x) / 3; // FIX v6.9
      var cy = (td0.y + td1.y + td2.y) / 3; // FIX v6.9
      var e0 = expandPointFromCentroid(td0, cx, cy, seamOverlap); // FIX v6.9
      var e1 = expandPointFromCentroid(td1, cx, cy, seamOverlap); // FIX v6.9
      var e2 = expandPointFromCentroid(td2, cx, cy, seamOverlap); // FIX v6.9
      defs.push('<clipPath id="' + id + '" clipPathUnits="userSpaceOnUse"><polygon points="' + round(e0.x) + ',' + round(e0.y) + ' ' + round(e1.x) + ',' + round(e1.y) + ' ' + round(e2.x) + ',' + round(e2.y) + '" /></clipPath>');
      body.push('<g clip-path="url(#' + id + ')" style="shape-rendering:geometricPrecision"><use href="#ltbw_src" xlink:href="#ltbw_src" transform="matrix(' + [round(m.a), round(m.b), round(m.c), round(m.d), round(m.e + ox), round(m.f + oy)].join(' ') + ')" /></g>');
    }

    for (var y = 0; y < App.grid.rows; y++) {
      for (var x = 0; x < App.grid.cols; x++) {
        var i00 = vertexIndex(x, y);
        var i10 = vertexIndex(x+1, y);
        var i01 = vertexIndex(x, y+1);
        var i11 = vertexIndex(x+1, y+1);
        var s00 = rest[i00], s10 = rest[i10], s01 = rest[i01], s11 = rest[i11];
        var d00 = warped[i00], d10 = warped[i10], d01 = warped[i01], d11 = warped[i11];
        addTriangle(s00, s10, s11, d00, d10, d11);
        addTriangle(s00, s11, s01, d00, d11, d01);
      }
    }

    var svg = [
      '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>',
      '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" xmlns:xlink="http://www.w3.org/1999/xlink" width="' + w + '" height="' + h + '" viewBox="0 0 ' + w + ' ' + h + '" preserveAspectRatio="none">',
      '<defs>', defs.join(''), '</defs>',
      body.join(''),
      '</svg>'
    ].join('');

    return new File([svg], fileName, { type: 'image/svg+xml' });
  }

  function nativeCurveBoundsFromRecords(records){ // FIX v15.0
    var minX = Infinity, minY = Infinity, maxX = -Infinity, maxY = -Infinity;
    function includePoint(x, y){
      x = Number(x); y = Number(y);
      if (!isFinite(x) || !isFinite(y)) return;
      if (x < minX) minX = x;
      if (y < minY) minY = y;
      if (x > maxX) maxX = x;
      if (y > maxY) maxY = y;
    }
    (records || []).forEach(function(record){
      try {
        var json = record && record.paperJson;
        var data = Array.isArray(json) ? json[1] : null;
        var segs = data && Array.isArray(data.segments) ? data.segments : [];
        segs.forEach(function(seg){
          var p = seg && seg[0] ? seg[0] : null;
          if (p && p.length >= 2) includePoint(p[0], p[1]);
        });
      } catch(e){}
    });
    if (!isFinite(minX) || !isFinite(minY) || !isFinite(maxX) || !isFinite(maxY)) return null;
    return { minX:minX, minY:minY, maxX:maxX, maxY:maxY, width:Math.max(1, maxX - minX), height:Math.max(1, maxY - minY), cx:(minX + maxX) * 0.5, cy:(minY + maxY) * 0.5 };
  }

  function getFirstBoneOriginLocalForFrame(frameNumber){ // FIX v16.8
    var frame = Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(frameNumber || 1)));
    var firstBone = null;
    try { firstBone = (App.bones || [])[0] || null; } catch(e) { firstBone = null; }
    if (!firstBone) return null;
    var pose = null;
    try { pose = getPoseForFrame(frame); } catch(e2) { pose = null; }
    var item = pose ? getBonePoseLike(firstBone, pose) : firstBone;
    if (!item) item = firstBone;
    var p = item.head || firstBone.head || null; // FIX v16.8: first bone sets the native clip origin by its head position.
    if (!p) return null;
    var x = Number(p.x);
    var y = Number(p.y);
    if (!isFinite(x) || !isFinite(y)) return null;
    return { x:x, y:y, boneId:firstBone.id, boneName:firstBone.name || 'Bone 1', kind:'head', frame:frame };
  }

  function getFirstBoneOriginLocal(){ // FIX v16.8
    return getFirstBoneOriginLocalForFrame(1);
  }

  function computeNativeCurveFirstBoneOriginForExportBounds(exportBounds){ // FIX v16.8
    exportBounds = exportBounds || { width: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width)), height: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height)), offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 };
    var origin = getFirstBoneOriginLocalForFrame(1); // FIX v16.8: native curve clip origin is set by Bone 1 on frame 1.
    if (origin) {
      exportBounds.nativeOriginX = Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0) + origin.x;
      exportBounds.nativeOriginY = Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0) + origin.y;
      exportBounds.nativeOriginBoneId = origin.boneId;
      exportBounds.nativeOriginBoneName = origin.boneName;
      exportBounds.nativeOriginBonePoint = origin.kind;
      exportBounds.nativeOriginFrame = origin.frame;
      exportBounds.nativeOriginMode = 'first-bone-head-frame-1';
      return exportBounds;
    }
    exportBounds.nativeOriginX = Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0) + Math.max(0, Number(exportBounds.width || 0) * 0.5);
    exportBounds.nativeOriginY = Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0);
    exportBounds.nativeOriginMode = 'fallback-top-centre';
    return exportBounds;
  }

  function nativeShapePathRecordsFromFrame(frameNum, exportBounds){ // FIX v14.9
    if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) return [];
    var pose = getPoseForFrame(frameNum);
    exportBounds = exportBounds || { width: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width)), height: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height)), offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 };
    var ox = Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0);
    var oy = Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0);
    var nativeOriginX = Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginX || 0); // FIX v15.0
    var nativeOriginY = Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginY || 0); // FIX v15.0
    var records = [];
    App.source.svgNative.shapes.forEach(function(shape){
      var style = clone(shape.style || {});
      if (shape.cmdSubpaths && shape.cmdSubpaths.length) {
        shape.cmdSubpaths.forEach(function(sp){
          var warpedCmds = (sp.commands || []).map(function(cmd){
            var out = { type: cmd.type };
            if (cmd.p) { var pp = skinPointByPose(cmd.p, pose); out.p = { x: pp.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: pp.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; } // FIX v15.1
            if (cmd.c1) { var pc1 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c1, pose); out.c1 = { x: pc1.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: pc1.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; } // FIX v15.1
            if (cmd.c2) { var pc2 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c2, pose); out.c2 = { x: pc2.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: pc2.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; } // FIX v15.1
            return out;
          });
          warpedCmds = smoothNativeCommandsForOutput(warpedCmds);
          var d = pathCommandsToD(warpedCmds);
          if (d.trim()) records.push({ d: d.trim(), style: clone(style), paperJson: paperJsonFromNativeCommands(warpedCmds, style) }); // FIX v14.9
        });
      } else if (shape.subpaths && shape.subpaths.length) {
        shape.subpaths.forEach(function(sp){
          var warped = sp.points.map(function(p){ var q = skinPointByPose(p, pose); return { x: q.x + ox - nativeOriginX, y: q.y + oy - nativeOriginY }; }); // FIX v15.1
          var d = pointsToSubpath(warped, sp.closed);
          if (d.trim()) records.push({ d: d.trim(), style: clone(style), paperJson: paperJsonFromPointList(warped, !!sp.closed, style) }); // FIX v14.9
        });
      }
    });
    return records;
  }

  function svgColorToPaperColor(value){ // FIX v14.8
    value = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
    if (!value || value === 'none' || value === 'transparent') return null;
    return value;
  }

  function paperJsonStyleFromSvgStyle(style){ // FIX v14.9
    style = style || {};
    var data = { applyMatrix: true };
    var fill = svgColorToPaperColor(style.fill);
    var stroke = svgColorToPaperColor(style.stroke);
    if (fill) data.fillColor = fill;
    else data.fillColor = null;
    if (stroke) data.strokeColor = stroke;
    else data.strokeColor = null;
    if (style['stroke-width'] != null) data.strokeWidth = Number(style['stroke-width']) || 1;
    if (style.opacity != null) data.opacity = Number(style.opacity);
    if (style['stroke-linecap'] != null) data.strokeCap = style['stroke-linecap'];
    if (style['stroke-linejoin'] != null) data.strokeJoin = style['stroke-linejoin'];
    return data;
  }

  function paperJsonSegment(point, handleIn, handleOut){ // FIX v14.9
    point = point || { x:0, y:0 };
    handleIn = handleIn || { x:0, y:0 };
    handleOut = handleOut || { x:0, y:0 };
    return [[round(point.x), round(point.y)], [round(handleIn.x), round(handleIn.y)], [round(handleOut.x), round(handleOut.y)]];
  }

  function paperJsonFromPointList(points, closed, style){ // FIX v14.9
    var data = paperJsonStyleFromSvgStyle(style);
    data.closed = !!closed;
    data.segments = (points || []).map(function(p){ return paperJsonSegment(p); });
    return ['Path', data];
  }

  function paperJsonFromNativeCommands(cmds, style){ // FIX v14.9
    var data = paperJsonStyleFromSvgStyle(style);
    var segments = [];
    var currentPoint = null;
    var closed = false;
    function pushPoint(p, handleIn){
      var seg = paperJsonSegment(p, handleIn || { x:0, y:0 }, { x:0, y:0 });
      segments.push(seg);
      currentPoint = { x:p.x, y:p.y };
      return seg;
    }
    (cmds || []).forEach(function(cmd){
      if (!cmd || !cmd.type) return;
      if (cmd.type === 'M' && cmd.p) {
        pushPoint(cmd.p);
      } else if (cmd.type === 'L' && cmd.p) {
        pushPoint(cmd.p);
