      } else if (cmd.type === 'Q' && cmd.c1 && cmd.p && currentPoint) {
        var c1 = { x: currentPoint.x + (2 / 3) * (cmd.c1.x - currentPoint.x), y: currentPoint.y + (2 / 3) * (cmd.c1.y - currentPoint.y) };
        var c2 = { x: cmd.p.x + (2 / 3) * (cmd.c1.x - cmd.p.x), y: cmd.p.y + (2 / 3) * (cmd.c1.y - cmd.p.y) };
        if (segments.length) segments[segments.length - 1][2] = [round(c1.x - currentPoint.x), round(c1.y - currentPoint.y)];
        pushPoint(cmd.p, { x: c2.x - cmd.p.x, y: c2.y - cmd.p.y });
      } else if (cmd.type === 'C' && cmd.c1 && cmd.c2 && cmd.p && currentPoint) {
        if (segments.length) segments[segments.length - 1][2] = [round(cmd.c1.x - currentPoint.x), round(cmd.c1.y - currentPoint.y)];
        pushPoint(cmd.p, { x: cmd.c2.x - cmd.p.x, y: cmd.c2.y - cmd.p.y });
      } else if (cmd.type === 'Z') {
        closed = true;
      }
    });
    data.closed = !!closed;
    data.segments = segments;
    return ['Path', data];
  }

  function applyNativeCurveStyle(path, style){ // FIX v14.8
    style = style || {};
    try { path.fillColor = svgColorToPaperColor(style.fill); } catch(e){}
    try { path.strokeColor = svgColorToPaperColor(style.stroke); } catch(e){}
    try { if (style['stroke-width'] != null) path.strokeWidth = Number(style['stroke-width']) || 1; } catch(e){}
    try { if (style.opacity != null) path.opacity = Number(style.opacity); } catch(e){}
    try { if (style['stroke-linecap'] != null) path.strokeCap = style['stroke-linecap']; } catch(e){}
    try { if (style['stroke-linejoin'] != null) path.strokeJoin = style['stroke-linejoin']; } catch(e){}
    return path;
  }

  function createNativeWickPathFromRecord(record, frameIndex, shapeIndex){ // FIX v14.9
    var d = String(record && record.d || '').trim();
    if (!d) throw new Error('Empty native curve path data');
    var style = record.style || {};
    var paperJson = record && record.paperJson ? clone(record.paperJson) : null; // FIX v14.9
    var paperItem = null;
    try {
      if (!paperJson && App.paper && App.paper.project && typeof App.paper.project.importSVG === 'function') {
        var svg = '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="' + escapeXmlAttr(d) + '"' + styleMapToAttrs(style) + '/></svg>';
        paperItem = App.paper.project.importSVG(svg, { insert:false });
        try { if (paperItem && paperItem.children && paperItem.children.length === 1) paperItem = paperItem.children[0]; } catch(e0){}
        if (paperItem) {
          applyNativeCurveStyle(paperItem, style);
          try { paperJson = paperItem.exportJSON({ asString:false }); } catch(e1){} // FIX v14.9
          try { if (typeof paperItem.remove === 'function') paperItem.remove(); } catch(e2){}
        }
      }
    } catch(e3){}
    if (!paperJson) throw new Error('Could not build Paper JSON for native Wick curve.'); // FIX v14.9
    var path = null;
    var errors = [];
    function attempt(fn){ try { var made = fn(); if (made) { path = made; return true; } } catch(e){ errors.push(e && e.message ? e.message : String(e)); } return false; }
    if (App.Wick && App.Wick.Path) {
      attempt(function(){ var p = new App.Wick.Path(); p.json = clone(paperJson); return p; }); // FIX v14.9
      if (!path) attempt(function(){ return new App.Wick.Path({ json: clone(paperJson) }); }); // FIX v14.9
      if (!path) attempt(function(){ var p2 = new App.Wick.Path({ json: clone(paperJson) }); p2.json = clone(paperJson); return p2; }); // FIX v14.9
    }
    if (!path) throw new Error('Could not create native Wick curve path' + (errors.length ? ': ' + errors.join(' | ') : ''));
    try { path.identifier = makeValidIdentifier('native_curve_' + frameIndex + '_' + shapeIndex, 'native_curve_' + frameIndex + '_' + shapeIndex); } catch(e4){}
    try { path.name = 'Native_Curve_' + frameIndex + '_' + shapeIndex; } catch(e5){}
    try { path.json = clone(paperJson); } catch(e6){} // FIX v14.9
    try { path.pathData = d; } catch(e7){}
    applyNativeCurveStyle(path, style);
    return path;
  }

  function countNativeCurveClipPaths(clip){ // FIX v14.9
    var total = 0;
    try {
      (clip.timeline.layers || []).forEach(function(layer){
        (layer.frames || []).forEach(function(frame){
          if (Array.isArray(frame.paths)) total += frame.paths.length;
          else if (Array.isArray(frame._children)) total += frame._children.filter(function(child){ return child && child.json; }).length;
          else if (Array.isArray(frame.children)) total += frame.children.length;
          else if (Array.isArray(frame.objects)) total += frame.objects.length;
        });
      });
    } catch(e){}
    return total;
  }

  function buildNativeCurveClip(clipName, exportBounds){ // FIX v14.9
    if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) throw new Error('Native Wick curve commit needs parsed SVG Native shapes.');
    exportBounds = computeNativeCurveFirstBoneOriginForExportBounds(exportBounds); // FIX v16.8
    var clipIdentifier = makeValidIdentifier(clipName, 'BoneWarpNativeCurveClip');
    var clip = new App.Wick.Clip({ identifier: clipIdentifier });
    try { clip.name = clipName; } catch(e){}
    try { clip.width = Math.max(1, Number(exportBounds.width || App.source.width || 1)); } catch(e2){}
    try { clip.height = Math.max(1, Number(exportBounds.height || App.source.height || 1)); } catch(e3){}
    try { clip.bounds = { x:-(Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginX || 0)), y:0, width:clip.width, height:clip.height }; } catch(e4){} // FIX v15.0
    var safeN = 10;
    while (clip.timeline.layers.length && safeN-- > 0) {
      try { clip.timeline.removeLayer(clip.timeline.layers[0]); } catch(e5){ break; }
    }
    var layer = new App.Wick.Layer();
    layer.name = 'native curves';
    clip.timeline.addLayer(layer);
    for (var fi = 1; fi <= App.frameCount; fi++) {
      var frame = new App.Wick.Frame({ start: fi, end: fi });
      frame.identifier = 'frame_' + fi;
      layer.addFrame(frame);
      var records = nativeShapePathRecordsFromFrame(fi, exportBounds);
      for (var si = 0; si < records.length; si++) {
        var path = createNativeWickPathFromRecord(records[si], fi, si + 1);
        addToFrame(frame, path);
      }
    }
    return clip;
  }

  function nativeSvgFileFromFrame(frameNum, fileName, exportBounds){ // FIX v7.3
    if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) return svgFileFromFrame(frameNum, fileName, exportBounds);
    var pose = getPoseForFrame(frameNum);
    exportBounds = exportBounds || { width: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width)), height: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height)), offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 };
    var w = Math.max(1, Math.round(exportBounds.width));
    var h = Math.max(1, Math.round(exportBounds.height));
    var ox = Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0);
    var oy = Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0);
    var body = [];
    App.source.svgNative.shapes.forEach(function(shape){
      var d = '';
      if (shape.cmdSubpaths && shape.cmdSubpaths.length) {
        shape.cmdSubpaths.forEach(function(sp){
          var warpedCmds = (sp.commands || []).map(function(cmd){
            var out = { type: cmd.type };
            if (cmd.p) { var pp = skinPointByPose(cmd.p, pose); out.p = { x: pp.x + ox, y: pp.y + oy }; }
            if (cmd.c1) { var pc1 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c1, pose); out.c1 = { x: pc1.x + ox, y: pc1.y + oy }; }
            if (cmd.c2) { var pc2 = skinPointByPose(cmd.c2, pose); out.c2 = { x: pc2.x + ox, y: pc2.y + oy }; }
            return out;
          });
          warpedCmds = smoothNativeCommandsForOutput(warpedCmds); // FIX v8.7
          d += pathCommandsToD(warpedCmds) + ' ';
        });
      } else if (shape.subpaths && shape.subpaths.length) {
        shape.subpaths.forEach(function(sp){
          var warped = sp.points.map(function(p){ var q = skinPointByPose(p, pose); return { x: q.x + ox, y: q.y + oy }; });
          d += pointsToSubpath(warped, sp.closed) + ' ';
        });
      }
      if (d.trim()) body.push('<path d="' + escapeXmlAttr(d.trim()) + '"' + styleMapToAttrs(shape.style) + ' />');
    });
    body.push(buildFrameBoneSvgMarkup(frameNum, pose, ox, oy)); // FIX v13.2
    var svg = ['<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>','<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="' + w + '" height="' + h + '" viewBox="0 0 ' + w + ' ' + h + '">',body.join(''),'</svg>'].join('');
    return new File([svg], fileName, { type: 'image/svg+xml' });
  }

  function forceCanvasTransparency(canvas){ // FIX v5.1
    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { willReadFrequently: true }); // FIX v5.1
    if (!ctx) return; // FIX v5.1
    var imgData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height); // FIX v5.1
    var d = imgData.data; // FIX v5.1
    for (var i = 0; i < d.length; i += 4) { // FIX v5.1
      if (d[i + 3] <= 8) { // FIX v5.1
        d[i] = 0; // FIX v5.1
        d[i + 1] = 0; // FIX v5.1
        d[i + 2] = 0; // FIX v5.1
        d[i + 3] = 0; // FIX v5.1
      }
    }
    ctx.putImageData(imgData, 0, 0); // FIX v5.1
  }

  function healTransparentTriangleSeams(canvas){ // FIX v6.1
    var ctx = canvas.getContext('2d', { willReadFrequently: true }); // FIX v6.1
    if (!ctx) return; // FIX v6.1
    var w = canvas.width; // FIX v6.1
    var h = canvas.height; // FIX v6.1
    if (w < 3 || h < 3) return; // FIX v6.1
    var imgData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, w, h); // FIX v6.1
    var src = imgData.data; // FIX v6.1
    var out = new Uint8ClampedArray(src); // FIX v6.1
    for (var y = 1; y < h - 1; y++) { // FIX v6.1
      for (var x = 1; x < w - 1; x++) { // FIX v6.1
        var i = (y * w + x) * 4; // FIX v6.1
        if (src[i + 3] > 16) continue; // FIX v6.1
        var totalA = 0; // FIX v6.1
        var totalR = 0; // FIX v6.1
        var totalG = 0; // FIX v6.1
        var totalB = 0; // FIX v6.1
        var strong = 0; // FIX v6.1
        for (var oy = -1; oy <= 1; oy++) { // FIX v6.1
          for (var ox = -1; ox <= 1; ox++) { // FIX v6.1
            if (!ox && !oy) continue; // FIX v6.1
            var ni = ((y + oy) * w + (x + ox)) * 4; // FIX v6.1
            var na = src[ni + 3]; // FIX v6.1
            if (na > 48) { // FIX v6.1
              strong++; // FIX v6.1
              totalA += na; // FIX v6.1
              totalR += src[ni] * na; // FIX v6.1
              totalG += src[ni + 1] * na; // FIX v6.1
              totalB += src[ni + 2] * na; // FIX v6.1
            }
          }
        }
        if (strong >= 3 && totalA > 0) { // FIX v6.1
          out[i] = Math.round(totalR / totalA); // FIX v6.1
          out[i + 1] = Math.round(totalG / totalA); // FIX v6.1
          out[i + 2] = Math.round(totalB / totalA); // FIX v6.1
          out[i + 3] = Math.min(255, Math.round(totalA / strong)); // FIX v6.1
        }
      }
    }
    imgData.data.set(out); // FIX v6.1
    ctx.putImageData(imgData, 0, 0); // FIX v6.1
  }

  function canvasFromFrame(frameNum, exportBounds){
    var pose = getPoseForFrame(frameNum);
    exportBounds = exportBounds || { width: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.width)), height: Math.max(1, Math.round(App.source.height)), offsetX: 0, offsetY: 0 }; // FIX v6.9
    var c = document.createElement('canvas');
    c.width = Math.max(1, Math.round(exportBounds.width)); // FIX v6.9
    c.height = Math.max(1, Math.round(exportBounds.height)); // FIX v6.9
    var ctx = c.getContext('2d', { alpha: true, willReadFrequently: true }); // FIX v5.1
    var prevImage = App.flags.showImage, prevMesh = App.flags.showMesh, prevBones = App.flags.showBones;
    App.flags.showImage = true;
    App.flags.showMesh = false;
    App.flags.showBones = false;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, c.width, c.height); // FIX v5.1
    renderWarpToContext(ctx, pose, { canvasWidth: c.width, canvasHeight: c.height, offsetX: exportBounds.offsetX || 0, offsetY: exportBounds.offsetY || 0 }); // FIX v6.9
    healTransparentTriangleSeams(c); // FIX v6.1
    forceCanvasTransparency(c); // FIX v5.1
    App.flags.showImage = prevImage;
    App.flags.showMesh = prevMesh;
    App.flags.showBones = prevBones;
    return c;
  }

  function isSvgCommitFile(file, name){ // FIX v14.2
    var n = String(name || (file && file.name) || '');
    var t = String((file && file.type) || '');
    return /\.svg$/i.test(n) || t.indexOf('svg') !== -1;
  }

  function markCommittedObjectAsSvg(path, asset, file, name, frameIndex){ // FIX v14.2
    if (!path) return path;
    var safeName = String(name || (file && file.name) || ('svg_' + frameIndex + '.svg'));
    try { path.identifier = makeValidIdentifier('svg_' + frameIndex, 'svg_' + frameIndex); } catch(e){}
    try { path.name = safeName.replace(/\.svg$/i, ''); } catch(e){}
    try { path.filename = safeName; } catch(e){}
    try { path.mimeType = 'image/svg+xml'; } catch(e){}
    try { path.type = 'image/svg+xml'; } catch(e){}
    try { path._ltbwCommittedSvg = true; } catch(e){}
    try { path._ltbwAssetName = safeName; } catch(e){}
    try { path.asset = asset; } catch(e){}
    try { if (asset) asset.mimeType = asset.mimeType || 'image/svg+xml'; } catch(e){}
    try { if (asset) asset.type = asset.type || 'image/svg+xml'; } catch(e){}
    return path;
  }

  async function stampAnimationIntoClip(){
    if (!refreshBridgeRefs()) {
      log('Bridge/editor not available.');
      return;
    }
    if (!App.source.image) {
      log('No source image captured.');
      return;
    }
    if (!App.bones.length) {
      log('No bones created.');
      return;
    }
    syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
    stop();
    var clipName = (el('inpClipName').value || '').trim() || ('BoneWarpClip_' + Date.now());
    var base = clipName.replace(/\s+/g, '_');
    var exportMode = (el('selExportMode') && el('selExportMode').value) || 'nativeCurve'; // FIX v16.9: native Wick curves are the default commit mode.
    if (exportMode === 'png' && App.source.captureMode === 'stage-crop') { // FIX v5.5
      log('WARNING: PNG export is using a stage crop source, so transparency will not be correct until the original PNG asset is captured.');
    }
    var exportBounds = computeAnimationExportBounds(); // FIX v6.9
    log('Committing ' + App.frameCount + ' warped ' + (exportMode === 'nativeCurve' ? 'native Wick curve' : (exportMode === 'svgNative' ? 'SVG native' : (exportMode === 'svg' ? 'SVG mesh' : 'PNG'))) + ' frames from the real Wick timeline...'); // FIX v14.8
    if (!Object.keys(App.keyframes || {}).length) log('Commit note: no animation keys found. The clip will commit the current rest pose on every frame. Use the Animate tab to create keys.'); // FIX v16.7
    if (exportBounds.width > App.source.width || exportBounds.height > App.source.height || exportBounds.minX < 0 || exportBounds.minY < 0) { // FIX v6.9
      log('Auto expanded the export area to avoid clipping: ' + exportBounds.width + ' x ' + exportBounds.height + ' px.'); // FIX v6.9
    }
    if (exportMode === 'nativeCurve') { // FIX v14.8
      try {
        var nativeClip = buildNativeCurveClip(clipName, exportBounds);
        var syncWithParentNative = !!(el('chkSyncWithParent') && el('chkSyncWithParent').checked);
        try { nativeClip.animationType = 'loop'; } catch(e){} // FIX v16.7: Wick rejects syncWithParent for clips, so keep commit animation valid.
        try { nativeClip.timeline.playheadPosition = 1; } catch(e2){}
        addClipToWickProject(nativeClip);
        try { log('Native curve clip created with ' + countNativeCurveClipPaths(nativeClip) + ' Wick path object' + (countNativeCurveClipPaths(nativeClip) === 1 ? '' : 's') + '. Origin: ' + (exportBounds.nativeOriginMode || 'first-bone-head') + '.'); } catch(countErr){} // FIX v16.7
        try {
          if (!App.committedClipIdentifiers) App.committedClipIdentifiers = [];
          App.committedClipIdentifiers.push(nativeClip.identifier || nativeClip.name || clipName);
        } catch(e3){}
        var placeAtSourceNative = el('chkPlaceAtSource').checked;
        var stampBoundsNative = getSetAreaStageBounds() || App.source.stageBounds || null;
        if (placeAtSourceNative && stampBoundsNative) {
          try {
            var srcWNative = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.width) || 1);
            var srcHNative = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.height) || 1);
            var scaleXNative = stampBoundsNative.w / srcWNative;
            var scaleYNative = stampBoundsNative.h / srcHNative;
            var nativeOriginSourceX = Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginX || 0) - Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0); // FIX v15.0
            var nativeOriginSourceY = Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginY || 0) - Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0); // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.x = stampBoundsNative.x + (nativeOriginSourceX * scaleXNative); // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.y = stampBoundsNative.y + (nativeOriginSourceY * scaleYNative); // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.scaleX = scaleXNative;
            nativeClip.transformation.scaleY = scaleYNative;
            nativeClip.transformation.rotation = 0;
          } catch(e4){}
        } else if (placeAtSourceNative && App.source.stageBounds) { // FIX v15.0
          try {
            var srcWNativeB = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.width) || 1); // FIX v15.0
            var srcHNativeB = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.height) || 1); // FIX v15.0
            var nativeOriginSourceXB = Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginX || 0) - Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0); // FIX v15.0
            var nativeOriginSourceYB = Number(exportBounds.nativeOriginY || 0) - Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0); // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.x = App.source.stageBounds.x + (nativeOriginSourceXB / srcWNativeB) * App.source.stageBounds.w; // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.y = App.source.stageBounds.y + (nativeOriginSourceYB / srcHNativeB) * App.source.stageBounds.h; // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.scaleX = App.source.stageBounds.w / srcWNativeB; // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.scaleY = App.source.stageBounds.h / srcHNativeB; // FIX v15.0
            nativeClip.transformation.rotation = App.source.stageRotation || 0;
          } catch(e5){}
        } else if (placeAtSourceNative && App.source.stageCenter) {
          try {
            nativeClip.transformation.x = App.source.stageCenter.x;
            nativeClip.transformation.y = App.source.stageCenter.y;
            nativeClip.transformation.scaleX = 1;
            nativeClip.transformation.scaleY = 1;
            nativeClip.transformation.rotation = App.source.stageRotation || 0;
          } catch(e5b){}
        }
        try { removeOverlay(); } catch(e6){}
        try { removeSetAreaOverlay(); } catch(e7){}
        markDirty();
        log('Clip committed to Wick with native editable curves on each frame: ' + clipName);
      } catch(nativeErr) {
        log('Native curve commit failed: ' + (nativeErr && nativeErr.message ? nativeErr.message : nativeErr));
      }
      return;
    }

    var files = [];
    var names = [];
    for (var i = 1; i <= App.frameCount; i++) {
      if (exportMode === 'svgNative') { // FIX v7.1
        if (!App.source.svgNative || !App.source.svgNative.shapes || !App.source.svgNative.shapes.length) {
          log('SVG Native Mode has no parsed SVG shapes. Falling back to SVG mesh warp.');
          exportMode = 'svg';
        } else {
          var nativeName = base + '_' + String(i).padStart(3, '0') + '.svg';
          files.push(nativeSvgFileFromFrame(i, nativeName, exportBounds));
          names.push(nativeName);
          continue;
        }
      }
      if (exportMode === 'svg') { // FIX v5.4
        var svgName = base + '_' + String(i).padStart(3, '0') + '.svg';
        files.push(svgFileFromFrame(i, svgName, exportBounds)); // FIX v6.9
        names.push(svgName);
      } else {
        var canvas = canvasFromFrame(i, exportBounds); // FIX v6.9
        var pngName = base + '_' + String(i).padStart(3, '0') + '.png';
        files.push(dataURLToFile(canvas.toDataURL('image/png'), pngName));
        names.push(pngName);
      }
    }

    try {
      await forceCommitFilesIntoAssets(files, names); // FIX v14.1: SVG frames must become project assets, not temporary data only
      var found = await waitForAssets(names, 15000);
      log('Assets imported into Wick. Building unclipped clip...');

      var clipIdentifier = makeValidIdentifier(clipName, 'BoneWarpClip'); // FIX v12.7
      var clip = new App.Wick.Clip({ identifier: clipIdentifier }); // FIX v12.7
      try { clip.name = clipName; } catch(e){} // FIX v12.7
      clip.name = clipName;
      try { clip.width = Math.max(1, Number(exportBounds.width || App.source.width || 1)); } catch(e){} // FIX v14.1
      try { clip.height = Math.max(1, Number(exportBounds.height || App.source.height || 1)); } catch(e){} // FIX v14.1
      try { clip.bounds = { x:0, y:0, width:clip.width, height:clip.height }; } catch(e){} // FIX v14.1

      var safeN = 10;
      while (clip.timeline.layers.length && safeN-- > 0) {
        try { clip.timeline.removeLayer(clip.timeline.layers[0]); } catch(e){ break; }
      }
      var layer = new App.Wick.Layer();
      layer.name = 'content';
      clip.timeline.addLayer(layer);

      for (var fi = 1; fi <= App.frameCount; fi++) {
        var frame = new App.Wick.Frame({ start: fi, end: fi });
        frame.identifier = 'frame_' + fi;
        layer.addFrame(frame);
        var asset = found[names[fi - 1]];
        var commitFile = files[fi - 1]; // FIX v14.2
        var path = await createImagePathFromAssetAny(asset);
        if (isSvgCommitFile(commitFile, names[fi - 1])) markCommittedObjectAsSvg(path, asset, commitFile, names[fi - 1], fi); // FIX v14.2
        else { try { path.identifier = 'img_' + fi; } catch(e){} }
        try { path.x = 0; path.y = 0; } catch(e){}
        try { path.width = Math.max(1, Number(exportBounds.width || App.source.width || 1)); } catch(e){} // FIX v14.1
        try { path.height = Math.max(1, Number(exportBounds.height || App.source.height || 1)); } catch(e){} // FIX v14.1
        try { path.bounds = { x:0, y:0, width:path.width || exportBounds.width, height:path.height || exportBounds.height }; } catch(e){} // FIX v14.1
        addToFrame(frame, path);
      }

      var syncWithParent = !!(el('chkSyncWithParent') && el('chkSyncWithParent').checked); // FIX v6.1
      try { clip.animationType = 'loop'; } catch(e){} // FIX v16.7: Wick rejects syncWithParent for clips, so keep commit animation valid.
      try { clip.timeline.playheadPosition = 1; } catch(e){} // FIX v6.1

      addClipToWickProject(clip); // FIX v13.8: create a real Wick clip on the active Wick timeline/frame
      try { // FIX v14.0: remember committed Wick clips as project content. Close cleanup must never remove these.
        if (!App.committedClipIdentifiers) App.committedClipIdentifiers = [];
        App.committedClipIdentifiers.push(clip.identifier || clip.name || clipName);
      } catch(e){}

      var placeAtSource = el('chkPlaceAtSource').checked;
      var stampBounds = getSetAreaStageBounds() || App.source.stageBounds || null; // FIX v6.8
      if (placeAtSource && stampBounds) { // FIX v6.8
        try {
          var srcW = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.width) || 1); // FIX v6.8
          var srcH = Math.max(1, Number(App.source.height) || 1); // FIX v6.8
          var scaleX = stampBounds.w / srcW; // FIX v6.9
          var scaleY = stampBounds.h / srcH; // FIX v6.9
          var localShiftX = ((Number(exportBounds.offsetX || 0) + srcW * 0.5) - (Number(exportBounds.width || srcW) * 0.5)); // FIX v6.9
          var localShiftY = ((Number(exportBounds.offsetY || 0) + srcH * 0.5) - (Number(exportBounds.height || srcH) * 0.5)); // FIX v6.9
          clip.transformation.x = stampBounds.cx - (localShiftX * scaleX); // FIX v6.9
          clip.transformation.y = stampBounds.cy - (localShiftY * scaleY); // FIX v6.9
          clip.transformation.scaleX = scaleX; // FIX v6.9
          clip.transformation.scaleY = scaleY; // FIX v6.9
          clip.transformation.rotation = 0; // FIX v6.8: Set Area stamping should match the dragged area rectangle exactly.
        } catch(e){}
      } else if (placeAtSource && App.source.stageCenter) {
        try {
          clip.transformation.x = App.source.stageCenter.x;
          clip.transformation.y = App.source.stageCenter.y;
          clip.transformation.scaleX = 1;
          clip.transformation.scaleY = 1;
          clip.transformation.rotation = App.source.stageRotation || 0;
        } catch(e){}
      }

      try { removeOverlay(); } catch(e){} // FIX v6.8: once the bone stamp is created the Set Area overlay should vanish.
      try { removeSetAreaOverlay(); } catch(e){} // FIX v6.8
      markDirty();
      log('Clip committed to Wick with expanded bounds and SVG asset references, not PNG conversion: ' + clipName);
    } catch(err) {
      log('Commit failed: ' + (err && err.message ? err.message : err));
    }
  }

  function bindEvents(){
    var panelEl = el('panel'); // FIX v8.2
    if (panelEl) { // FIX v8.2
      panelEl.addEventListener('wheel', function(ev){ ev.stopPropagation(); }, { passive:true }); // FIX v8.2
      panelEl.addEventListener('touchmove', function(ev){ ev.stopPropagation(); }, { passive:true }); // FIX v8.2
    }
    qa('.tabBtn').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){ setActiveTab(btn.getAttribute('data-tab')); });
    });

    ['numEditHeadX','numEditHeadY','numEditTailX','numEditTailY','numEditLength','numEditAngle','numEditEnvStart','numEditEnvEnd','numEditStrength'].forEach(function(id){ // FIX v6.7
      var node = el(id);
      if (!node) return;
      node.addEventListener('change', applyEditBoneFields);
    });
    if (el('btnEditApplyBone')) el('btnEditApplyBone').addEventListener('click', applyEditBoneFields); // FIX v6.7
    if (el('btnEditRefreshBone')) el('btnEditRefreshBone').addEventListener('click', function(){ updateEditBoneControls(); updateUI(); }); // FIX v6.7
    if (el('btnEditBoneModeBone')) el('btnEditBoneModeBone').addEventListener('click', function(){ setEditBoneMode('bone'); }); // FIX v16.6
    if (el('btnEditBoneModeEnvelope')) el('btnEditBoneModeEnvelope').addEventListener('click', function(){ setEditBoneMode('envelope'); }); // FIX v16.6

    el('btnSetArea').addEventListener('click', beginSetAreaMode); // FIX v6.0
    el('btnLoadImage').addEventListener('click', function(){ if (!App.source.viewportRect) { log('Set the area first.'); return; } promptLocalImageFile(); }); // FIX v6.0
    if (el('btnUseSelectedCurve')) el('btnUseSelectedCurve').addEventListener('click', useSelectedWickCurveAsSource); // FIX v14.4
    if (el('btnUseSelectedCurveRemove')) el('btnUseSelectedCurveRemove').addEventListener('click', useSelectedWickCurveAsSourceAndRemoveOriginal); // FIX v14.5
    el('fileImageLoader').addEventListener('change', onImageFileChosen); // FIX v6.0
    el('btnRefreshOverlay').addEventListener('click', function(){ if (!App.source.image) { updateUI(); return; } ensureOverlay(); hideSetAreaVisualFrame(); fitOverlayToSource(); renderOverlay(); updateUI(); }); // FIX v7.8
    el('btnRemoveOverlay').addEventListener('click', function(){ removeSetAreaOverlay(); removeOverlay(); updateUI(); }); // FIX v6.0

    if (el('chkSvgSmoothEnabled')) el('chkSvgSmoothEnabled').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.smooth.enabled = !!this.checked; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v8.7
    if (el('rngSvgSmoothAmount')) el('rngSvgSmoothAmount').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.smooth.amount = clamp((parseInt(this.value,10) || 0) / 100, 0, 1); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v8.7
    if (el('rngSvgCurveStrength')) el('rngSvgCurveStrength').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.smooth.curveStrength = clamp((parseInt(this.value,10) || 0) / 100, 0, 1); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v8.7
    if (el('chkSvgSmoothPreserveEnds')) el('chkSvgSmoothPreserveEnds').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.smooth.preserveEnds = !!this.checked; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v8.7
    if (el('chkSvgSmoothKeepFlatEnds')) el('chkSvgSmoothKeepFlatEnds').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.smooth.keepFlatEnds = !!this.checked; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v16.2
    if (el('rngSelectedCurvePointDensity')) el('rngSelectedCurvePointDensity').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.selectedCurve.pointDensity = clamp(parseInt(this.value,10) || 0, 0, 100); updateUI(); }); // FIX v14.6
    if (el('btnSvgSmoothPreview')) el('btnSvgSmoothPreview').addEventListener('click', function(){ renderOverlay(); updateUI(); }); // FIX v8.7

    el('chkShowImage').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.flags.showImage = !!this.checked; renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('chkShowMesh')) el('chkShowMesh').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.flags.showMesh = !!this.checked; renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v13.5
    el('chkShowBones').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.flags.showBones = !!this.checked; renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('rngGridResolution')) el('rngGridResolution').addEventListener('input', function(){ // FIX v13.1: grid control removed for SVG Native workflow, guard kept for compatibility
      App.grid.resolution = clamp(parseInt(this.value, 10) || 18, 3, 40);
      App.grid.cols = App.grid.resolution;
      App.grid.rows = App.grid.resolution;
      buildAlphaMask();
      updateUI();
      renderOverlay();
    });
    el('rngOverlayOpacity').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.overlay.opacity = (parseInt(this.value,10) || 100) / 100; updateUI(); if (App.overlay.root) App.overlay.root.style.opacity = String(App.overlay.opacity); });
    if (el('chkMeshOpaqueOnly')) el('chkMeshOpaqueOnly').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.rig.meshOpaqueOnly = !!this.checked; renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v13.5
    if (el('rngAlphaThreshold')) el('rngAlphaThreshold').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.source.alphaThreshold = parseInt(this.value,10) || 8; buildAlphaMask(); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v13.5

    if (el('selFrameBoneCreateMode')) el('selFrameBoneCreateMode').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.frameBoneCreateMode = this.value === 'pin' ? 'pin' : 'attach'; updateFrameBoneUI(); }); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnAddFrameBone')) el('btnAddFrameBone').addEventListener('click', addFrameBoneFromMode); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnAddFrameBoneAttach')) el('btnAddFrameBoneAttach').addEventListener('click', function(){ App.frameBoneCreateMode = 'attach'; App.frameBonePinMode = false; addFrameBoneFromMode(); }); // FIX v13.4
    if (el('btnAddFrameBonePin')) el('btnAddFrameBonePin').addEventListener('click', function(){ App.frameBoneCreateMode = 'pin'; App.frameBonePinMode = false; addFrameBoneFromMode(); }); // FIX v13.4
    if (el('btnDeleteFrameBone')) el('btnDeleteFrameBone').addEventListener('click', deleteSelectedFrameBone); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnApplyFrameBoneCount')) el('btnApplyFrameBoneCount').addEventListener('click', applySelectedFrameBoneCount); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnLoadFrameBoneSvg')) el('btnLoadFrameBoneSvg').addEventListener('click', promptFrameBoneSvgFile); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('fileFrameBoneSvgLoader')) el('fileFrameBoneSvgLoader').addEventListener('change', function(){ onFrameBoneSvgFileChosen(this.files && this.files[0]); }); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnLoadAllFrameBoneSvgs')) el('btnLoadAllFrameBoneSvgs').addEventListener('click', promptLoadAllFrameBoneSvgs); // FIX v13.6
    if (el('fileFrameBoneSvgAllLoader')) el('fileFrameBoneSvgAllLoader').addEventListener('change', function(){ onFrameBoneSvgAllFilesChosen(this.files); }); // FIX v13.6
    if (el('btnApplyFrameBoneTransform')) el('btnApplyFrameBoneTransform').addEventListener('click', applySelectedFrameBoneTransform); // FIX v13.6
    if (el('numFrameBoneScale')) el('numFrameBoneScale').addEventListener('change', applySelectedFrameBoneTransform); // FIX v13.6
    if (el('numFrameBoneRotation')) el('numFrameBoneRotation').addEventListener('change', applySelectedFrameBoneTransform); // FIX v13.6
    if (el('btnSetFrameBoneKey')) el('btnSetFrameBoneKey').addEventListener('click', setSelectedFrameBoneKey); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnClearFrameBoneKey')) el('btnClearFrameBoneKey').addEventListener('click', clearSelectedFrameBoneKey); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnSaveRigProject')) el('btnSaveRigProject').addEventListener('click', saveRigProjectState); // FIX v13.4
    if (el('btnLoadRigProject')) el('btnLoadRigProject').addEventListener('click', promptLoadRigProject); // FIX v13.4
    if (el('fileRigProjectLoader')) el('fileRigProjectLoader').addEventListener('change', function(){ onRigProjectFileChosen(this.files && this.files[0]); }); // FIX v13.4
    el('btnDeleteBone').addEventListener('click', deleteSelectedBone);
    el('btnClearBones').addEventListener('click', clearBones);
    el('btnRenameBone').addEventListener('click', renameSelectedBone);
    if (el('selBoneType')) el('selBoneType').addEventListener('change', function(){ setSelectedBoneType(this.value); }); // FIX v17.0
    el('selBoneParent').addEventListener('change', function(){ setSelectedBoneParent(this.value); });
    el('selRigMode').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.rig.mode = (this.value === 'chainIk' || this.value === 'splineIk') ? this.value : 'fk'; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    el('chkAutoConnect').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.rig.autoConnect = !!this.checked; updateUI(); });
    el('rngConnectDistance').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.rig.connectDistance = parseInt(this.value,10) || 18; updateUI(); });
    el('rngBoneRadius').addEventListener('input', function(){ var b = getSelectedBone(); if (!b) return; var v = parseInt(this.value,10) || 90; b.radius = v; b.envStart = v; b.envEnd = v; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('rngEnvStart')) el('rngEnvStart').addEventListener('input', function(){ var b = getSelectedBone(); if (!b) return; b.envStart = parseInt(this.value,10) || 90; b.radius = Math.max(getBoneEnvStart(b), getBoneEnvEnd(b)); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('rngEnvEnd')) el('rngEnvEnd').addEventListener('input', function(){ var b = getSelectedBone(); if (!b) return; b.envEnd = parseInt(this.value,10) || 90; b.radius = Math.max(getBoneEnvStart(b), getBoneEnvEnd(b)); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    el('rngBoneStrength').addEventListener('input', function(){ var b = getSelectedBone(); if (!b) return; b.strength = (parseInt(this.value,10) || 100) / 100; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('btnToggleWeightPaint')) el('btnToggleWeightPaint').addEventListener('click', function(){ App.paint.enabled = !App.paint.enabled; App.interaction.addBoneMode = App.activeTab === 'bones' && !App.paint.enabled; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); }); // FIX v13.2
    if (el('btnClearWeightPaint')) el('btnClearWeightPaint').addEventListener('click', function(){ clearWeightMapForBone(getSelectedBone()); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('selWeightPaintAction')) el('selWeightPaintAction').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.paint.action = this.value === 'erase' ? 'erase' : 'paint'; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('rngWeightBrushSize')) el('rngWeightBrushSize').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.paint.brushSize = parseInt(this.value,10) || 28; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('rngWeightBrushStrength')) el('rngWeightBrushStrength').addEventListener('input', function(){ App.paint.brushStrength = clamp((parseInt(this.value,10) || 35) / 100, 0.01, 1); updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });
    if (el('chkShowWeightOverlay')) el('chkShowWeightOverlay').addEventListener('change', function(){ App.paint.showOverlay = !!this.checked; updateUI(); renderOverlay(); });

    el('btnApplyTimeline').addEventListener('click', function(){
      App.fps = clamp(parseInt(el('inpFPS').value,10) || 12, 1, 60);
      syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
      updateUI(); renderOverlay(); scheduleProxyFrame();
      log('Synced to Wick timeline: ' + App.frameCount + ' frame' + (App.frameCount === 1 ? '' : 's') + '.');
    });
    el('btnPrevFrame').addEventListener('click', function(){ setCurrentFrame(App.currentFrame - 1, false); }); // FIX v8.5
    el('btnNextFrame').addEventListener('click', function(){ setCurrentFrame(App.currentFrame + 1, false); }); // FIX v8.5
    el('inpCurrentFrame').addEventListener('change', function(){ setCurrentFrame(parseInt(this.value,10) || 1, false); }); // FIX v8.5
    if (el('wickFrameIndicator')) { // FIX v8.3
      el('wickFrameIndicator').addEventListener('mousedown', startFrameIndicatorScrub); // FIX v8.3
      el('wickFrameIndicator').addEventListener('touchstart', startFrameIndicatorScrub, { passive:false }); // FIX v8.3
    }
    el('btnPlay').addEventListener('click', play);
    el('btnStop').addEventListener('click', stop);
    el('btnPreviewFromWick').addEventListener('click', function(){
      syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
      var tl = getSelectedTimeline();
      if (!tl) return;
      var pos = Number(tl.playheadPosition || App.project.currentFrameNumber || 1);
      setCurrentFrame(pos, false);
    });
    el('chkFollowWick').addEventListener('change', function(){ if (App.playing) stop(false); App.flags.followWick = !!this.checked; updateUI(); }); // FIX v8.2

    el('btnSetKey').addEventListener('click', function(){ setCurrentKeyFromPose(getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame)); });
    el('btnClearKey').addEventListener('click', clearCurrentKey);
    el('btnCopyPrevPose').addEventListener('click', copyPreviousPose);
    el('btnResetCurrentToRest').addEventListener('click', resetCurrentToRest);
    if (el('btnProxySetup')) el('btnProxySetup').addEventListener('click', setupProxyLayer); // FIX v10.9
    if (el('btnProxyAddKey')) el('btnProxyAddKey').addEventListener('click', function(){ setCurrentKeyFromPose(getPoseForFrame(App.currentFrame)); if (!App.proxy.active) setupProxyLayer(); else { syncProxyLayersToBones(); scheduleProxyFrame(); } }); // FIX v10.9
    if (el('btnProxySync')) el('btnProxySync').addEventListener('click', function(){ if (!App.proxy.active) setupProxyLayer(); else { syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline(); syncProxyLayersToBones(); renderProxyFrame(); updateUI(); } }); // FIX v10.9
    if (el('btnProxyRemove')) el('btnProxyRemove').addEventListener('click', function(){ removeProxyOverlay(false); log('Proxy keyframe layer removed.'); }); // FIX v10.2

    el('btnStampClip').addEventListener('click', stampAnimationIntoClip);
  }

  function purgeStaleOwnedOverlays(){
    try {
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (!pdoc) return;
      var stale = Array.prototype.slice.call(pdoc.querySelectorAll('[data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay]'));
      stale.forEach(function(node){
        var owner = node.getAttribute('data-luketools-bonewarp-overlay');
        if (owner && owner !== App.interaction.overlayOwnerId) {
          try { if (node.parentNode) node.parentNode.removeChild(node); } catch(e){}
        }
      });
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function startCloseObserver(){
    try {
      var pdoc = window.parent && window.parent.document ? window.parent.document : null;
      if (!pdoc || !window.MutationObserver || !window.frameElement) return;
      if (App.interaction.closeObserver) App.interaction.closeObserver.disconnect();
      App.interaction.closeObserver = new MutationObserver(function(){
        try {
          var frame = window.frameElement;
          if (!frame || !frame.isConnected) cleanupToolOverlays();
        } catch(e){ cleanupToolOverlays(); }
      });
      App.interaction.closeObserver.observe(pdoc.body || pdoc.documentElement, { childList:true, subtree:true });
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function startCloseWatcher(){ // FIX v8.4
    try { if (App.closeWatchTimer) clearInterval(App.closeWatchTimer); } catch(e){}
    App.closeWatchTimer = setInterval(function(){
      try {
        var frame = window.frameElement;
        if (!frame) return;
        // FIX v8.4: only destroy when the panel iframe is actually removed. Do not destroy just because the panel is hidden or resized.
        if (!frame.isConnected) cleanupToolOverlays();
      } catch(e){}
    }, 500);
  }

  function forceToolPanelFill(){ // FIX v7.6
    try {
      var frame = window.frameElement;
      if (!frame) return;
      frame.style.width = '100%';
      frame.style.height = '100%';
      frame.style.minHeight = '0';
      frame.style.flex = '1 1 auto';
      frame.style.display = 'block';
      frame.style.alignSelf = 'stretch';
      var parent = frame.parentElement;
      if (parent) {
        var cs = window.parent && window.parent.getComputedStyle ? window.parent.getComputedStyle(parent) : null;
        if (cs && cs.display !== 'flex') parent.style.display = 'flex';
        parent.style.flexDirection = 'column';
        parent.style.minHeight = '0';
        parent.style.height = parent.style.height || '100%';
      }
      var grand = parent && parent.parentElement ? parent.parentElement : null;
      if (grand) {
        grand.style.minHeight = '0';
      }
    } catch(e){}
  }

  function init(){
    forceToolPanelFill(); // FIX v7.6
    refreshBridgeRefs();
    bindEvents();
    purgeStaleOwnedOverlays();
    startFollowWick();
    startCloseWatcher();
    startCloseObserver();
    installParentCloseCleanup(); // FIX v9.7
    try { window.addEventListener('resize', forceToolPanelFill); } catch(e){} // FIX v7.6
    try { window.parent && window.parent.addEventListener && window.parent.addEventListener('resize', forceToolPanelFill); } catch(e){} // FIX v7.6
    try { window.addEventListener('message', function(e){ if (e && e.data && (e.data.type === 'LukeToolsClose' || e.data.type === 'LukeToolsToolClosed')) cleanupToolOverlays(); }); } catch(e){}
    syncFrameCountFromWickTimeline();
    updateUI();
    log('LukeTools Bone Warp Stamp v13.2 ready. Closing the tool now destroys all BoneWarp overlays, masks, hosts, listeners and timers.'); // FIX v11.3
    if (!App.B) log('Warning: LukeToolsBridge not found yet. The tool will still retry when you capture selection.');
  }

  init();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
dy>
</html>
